Chalo bhai, shuru karte hain aapke Figma (Beginner-to-Job-Ready) notes ka Module 1!

Yeh hamara 'Foundation' module hai. Yahan hum Figma ke building blocks ko samjhenge. Ekdum zero se.

---

### 1.1: Figma Kya Hai aur Kyun?

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Figma Kya Hai aur Kyun? (Figma ka Introduction).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Figma ek **all-in-one, browser-based** (cloud-based) UI/UX design tool hai, jisse aap websites, mobile apps, aur digital products design, prototype (clickable banana), aur developers ko handoff kar sakte hain.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yeh industry standard ban gaya hai kyunki yeh **real-time collaboration** (ek saath kaam karna) allow karta hai. Designers, Product Managers, aur Developers sab ek hi file mein, ek hi time par kaam kar sakte hain. Yeh "Google Docs for Designers" jaisa hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Jab bhi aapko koi digital screen (website, app, watch UI) design karni ho. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh "Design_v5_final_FINAL_v2.psd" waali problem ko solve karta hai. Sirf ek hi version hota hai, jo hamesha latest hota hai (single source of truth).
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aap slow ho jayenge. Aapko files share karne (e.g., email ya drive se) mein time lagega. Collaboration (teamwork) bohot mushkil ho jayega aur developers ko design specs samjhana (handoff) ek alag kaam ban jayega.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Concept breakdown:**
    * **Design:** Aap UI banate hain (buttons, text, images).
    * **Prototype:** Aap unhe clickable banate hain (screens ko jodte hain).
    * **Handoff (Inspect):** Developers aapke design se seedha code (CSS, Swift, XML) nikaal sakte hain.
    * **Cloud:** Sab kuch browser mein chalta hai (Desktop app bhi hai, par woh bhi cloud se synced rehti hai).
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Figma ka interface samajhna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  **Left Panel (Layers/Assets/Pages):** Yahan aapke saare elements (layers) aur screens (pages) ki list hoti hai.
        2.  **Top Panel (Toolbar):** Yahan aapke tools hote hain (Move, Frame, Shapes, Pen, Text).
        3.  **Center (Canvas):** Yeh aapka infinite drawing area hai.
        4.  **Right Panel (Design/Prototype/Inspect):** Yeh "Inspector" hai. Yahan aap selected element ki properties (color, size, font) badalte hain.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapko Figma ka basic layout samajh aa jayega ki kaun si cheez kahan hai.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Sochna ki yeh "Photoshop" jaisa hai (Yeh photo editing ke liye nahi, UI *design* ke liye hai).
    * Desktop app download karna aur sochna ki files local save ho rahi hain (Woh abhi bhi cloud mein save ho rahi hain).
    * Internet ke bina isko use karne ki koshish karna (Yeh primarily online tool hai).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main toh akela kaam karta hoon, mujhe collaboration ki kya zaroorat hai? Main Photoshop/Illustrator kyun na use karun?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Aap design karenge, usi file mein prototype banayenge, aur client ko *sirf ek link* bhejenge. Client us link ko browser mein kholega, design dekhega, prototype chala kar dekhega, aur wahin par comments de dega. Koi file export/import nahi karni padegi.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Ek designer (Aap) "Login Screen" bana rahe hain. Saath mein, doosra designer (Aapka colleague) "Home Screen" bana raha hai. Ek Product Manager usi file mein comments de raha hai. Aur ek Developer "Inspect Tab" se button ka CSS code copy kar raha hai... *sab ek hi time par, ek hi file mein.*
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Google, Microsoft, Airbnb, Dropbox... sab badi companies Figma use karti hain apne design systems aur products banane ke liye.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Aapko shuru karne ke liye bas ek free account aur Google Chrome browser chahiye.
    * Figma files hamesha "Drafts" mein shuru hoti hain.
    * Har cheez automatically save hoti hai.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Kya Figma free hai?** Haan, iska "Starter" (Free) plan bohot powerful hai. Aap unlimited files bana sakte hain (3 project files tak).
    * **Figma vs Sketch vs Adobe XD?** Figma collaboration aur cross-platform (Mac/Windows/Linux) hone ki wajah se jeet gaya hai.
    * **Kya mujhe powerful computer chahiye?** Nahi, kyunki yeh browser mein chalta hai, isliye normal laptop par bhi aaraam se chalta hai.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. Figma.com par jaakar ek free account banayein.
    * 2. Ek "New design file" create karein.
    * 3. File ka naam (top center mein) "My First Project" rakhein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **FigJam:** Yeh Figma ka hi whiteboarding tool hai (brainstorming aur user flows ke liye). Hum isse Module 2 mein detail mein dekhenge.

---

### 1.2: File Organization (Using 'Pages')

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** File Organization (Using 'Pages') ğŸ—ƒï¸ (Apni file ko saaf-suthra rakhna).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** 'Pages' aapki Figma file ke andar *tabs* (jaise browser tabs) ya sections hote hain. Yeh aapki ek hi `.fig` file ko alag-alag hisson mein baantne ka tareeka hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Sabse zaroori! Ek professional designer ki file hamesha organized hoti hai. Isse aap (aur aapki team) confuse nahi hote. Developers ko pata hota hai ki "final designs" kahan milenge aur "wireframes" kahan.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** **Har project mein, project shuru karte hi.** Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh us problem ko solve karta hai jahan aapke Wireframes, Low-Fidelity, High-Fidelity designs, Prototypes, aur Components... sab *ek hi jagah* (ek hi canvas par) mix ho jaate hain aur file ekdum messy (gandi) dikhti hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapki file "khichdi" ban jayegi. Aapko khud apne designs dhoondhne mein time lagega. Team members confuse honge. File load hone mein bhi zyada time legi agar ek hi page par hazaaron elements honge.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Concept breakdown:**
    * Aapki Figma file ek kitaab (Book) hai.
    * 'Pages' us kitaab ke chapters (Chapters) hain.
    * Har Page ke andar 'Frames' (jo hum aage sikhenge) us chapter ke panne (Pages) hain.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek naye project ke liye 'Pages' structure set up karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Figma file kholein. **Left Panel** (Layers tab) mein top par dekhein, wahan "Page 1" likha hoga.
        2.  "Page 1" par right-click karein aur "Rename" chunein. Iska naam rakhein "ğŸ“± High-Fidelity (App)".
        3.  Ab Left Panel mein "Pages" header ke paas `+` icon par click karein.
        4.  Ek nayi "Page 2" ban jayegi. Isse rename karke "ğŸ§© Components" rakhein.
        5.  Ek aur Page banayein aur naam rakhein "ğŸš§ Wireframes".
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Ab aapke paas Left Panel mein 3 alag-alag tabs (Pages) hain, aur aap unke beech switch kar sakte hain. Har page ka apna alag, independent Canvas hoga.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Sirf "Page 1" par hi saara kaam karte rehna.
    * Har *screen* (e.g., Home, Profile) ke liye ek alag 'Page' bana dena. (Galat! Screens ke liye hum 'Frames' use karte hain, jo ek hi Page par rehte hain).
    * Pages ko clear naam na dena (e.g., "Page 1", "Page 2", "Page 3").
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Mera toh chota sa 5-page ka website project hai. Kya mujhe 'Pages' ki zaroorat hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Haan! Kam se kam 3 pages banayein:
        1.  `Design:` Yahan aapki final website screens hongi.
        2.  `Components:` Yahan aapke reusable elements (Buttons, Navbars) honge.
        3.  `Archive/Trash:` Yahan aap apne puraane, rejected designs rakhein taaki main file saaf rahe.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Ek team ke paas bohot strict Page structure hota hai:
        * `Cover:` File ka thumbnail, project details.
        * `âœ… Ready for Dev:` Woh screens jo final hain aur developers bana sakte hain.
        * `ğŸš§ In Progress (Designer Name):` Yahan designers kaam kar rahe hote hain.
        * `ğŸ—ƒï¸ Design System:` Poore project ke Styles aur Components.
        * `User Flows:` (FigJam ya Figma mein user ka path).
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek e-commerce app ki file mein "iOS App", "Android App", aur "Web" ke liye alag-alag Pages ho sakte hain.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Project shuru karte hi Pages set up karo.
    * Clear naam rakho. Emojis use karna achha rehta hai (jaise ğŸ“±, ğŸŒ, ğŸ§©, ğŸ—‘ï¸).
    * Apne puraane designs ko delete mat karo, unhe "Archive" page par move kar do.
    * (Free plan mein 3 pages ki limit hai. Paid plan mein unlimited).
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Pages aur Frames mein kya fark hai?** Pages poori file ko sections mein baantte hain (har page ka apna canvas hota hai). Frames ek hi canvas ke upar artboards/screens hote hain.
    * **Pages aur Sections mein kya fark hai?** Pages (Left Panel) file ko divide karte hain. Sections (Toolbar mein 'Frame' ke paas) ek hi *Canvas* par elements ko group karne ke liye hote hain.
    * **Kya main Pages ko re-order kar sakta hoon?** Haan, bas Left Panel mein unhe drag-and-drop karein.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. Apni "My First Project" file kholein.
    * 2. 3 Pages banayein: "Cover", "High-Fidelity", "Components".
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Sections:** Yeh ek naya feature hai jo *ek hi Page ke andar* Frames ko organize karne mein help karta hai.

---

### 1.3: Canvas, Frames, aur Layers Panel

**(Yeh ek CORE Foundational topic hai. Poora dhyaan dein.)**

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Canvas, Frames (F), aur Layers Panel (Figma ke 3 Stambh).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):**
    * **Canvas:** Yeh aapka infinite (unlimited) grey background hai jahan aap saara design karte hain. Yeh aapka "desk" hai.
    * **Frames (Tool: F):** Yeh aapke "artboards" ya "kaagaz ke tukde" (papers) hain. Yeh aapki app ki screen (e.g., iPhone 14) ya website ka page (e.g., Desktop) hota hai.
    * **Layers Panel (Left Panel):** Yeh aapke saare elements (Frames, Shapes, Text) ki list hai, top-to-bottom.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Inke bina aap design shuru hi nahi kar sakte. **Frames sabse zaroori hain** kyunki responsive design (Constraints/Auto Layout) aur Prototyping (screens ko jodna) *sirf Frames par* kaam karta hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):**
    * **Canvas:** Aap hamesha Canvas par hote hain.
    * **Frames:** Design shuru karne se pehle, sabse pehla kadam. Jab bhi aapko ek *nayee screen* (e.g., Home Page, About Page, Login Screen) banani ho, aap ek 'Frame' banayenge.
    * **Layers Panel:** Hamesha khula rehta hai (Left Panel). Isko aap elements ko select, re-order, ya group karne ke liye use karte hain.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):**
    * **â—ï¸Sabse badi galti:** Agar aap 'Frame' (F) ki jagah 'Rectangle' (R) use karte hain. Ek Rectangle (Shape) ek screen nahi hota. Aap usmein Constraints nahi laga sakte, use prototype nahi kar sakte, aur uske andar elements 'clip' (chhup) nahi hote.
    * Agar aap 'Layers Panel' ko ignore karenge, toh 50+ elements hone par aapka design messy ho jayega. Aapko "Header" dhoondhne ke liye canvas par click karte rehna padega, jo bohot inefficient (slow) hai.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Concept breakdown:**
    * Aapka Canvas (desk) hai.
    * Aapne 'F' daba kar ek Frame (paper) liya.
    * Aapne 'R' (Rectangle) aur 'T' (Text) se us Frame ke *andar* elements banaye.
    * Layers Panel (left) mein ab aapko aisa structure dikhega:
        * `â–¼ Frame 1` (Aapki Screen)
            * `Text`
            * `Rectangle`
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek 'iPhone 14' screen (Frame) banana aur usmein ek Layer add karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Toolbar se 'Frame' tool select karein (ya keyboard par `F` dabayein).
        2.  Jaise hi aap 'F' dabayenge, **Right Panel (Inspector)** mein dekhein. Wahan "Frame" ke neeche aapko popular device presets milenge (iPhone, Android, Desktop, etc.).
        3.  "Phone" section ke andar "iPhone 14 Pro" par click karein.
        4.  **ğŸš€ Quick run (Output):** Aapke Canvas par ek perfect iPhone 14 Pro ke size ka container (Frame) ban jayega.
        5.  Ab 'R' daba kar us Frame ke *andar* ek Rectangle banayein.
        6.  **Left Panel (Layers)** mein dekhein. Aapko dikhega ki "Rectangle 1" us "iPhone 14 Pro - 1" Frame ke *andar* (nested) hai.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * **Frames (F) ki jagah Rectangles (R) ka istemaal karna** screens banane ke liye. (Yeh sabse badi galti hai).
    * Frames ke *baahar* elements design karna. Woh elements "loose" hote hain aur prototype ka hissa nahi banenge.
    * Layers Panel mein elements ko rename na karna. (Aapke paas "Rectangle 54" aur "Rectangle 55" honge, jinka koi matlab nahi nikalta).
    * Elements ko 'Lock' (Ctrl+Shift+L) na karna. (Jaise background image, jo baar-baar move hoti rehti hai).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Frame aur Group (Ctrl+G) mein kya farak hai? Dono hi elements ko ikattha rakhte hain."
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Ek student har screen ke liye ek Frame banata hai (e.g., "Home", "About", "Contact"). Phir woh Layers Panel mein jaakar har cheez ko rename karta hai (e.g., "Header", "Footer", "Main Button") taaki uski file saaf dikhe.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Ek team mein, Layers Panel hygiene bohot zaroori hai. Har layer ka naam clear hota hai (e.g., `Button/Primary/Default`). **Frame aur Group ka fark:**
        * **Group (Ctrl+G):** Sirf elements ko saath mein move karne ke liye hai. Iska apna koi size nahi hota, yeh bas andar ke elements ka size le leta hai.
        * **Frame (F):** Ek proper container hai. Iski apni `height` aur `width` hoti hai, iska apna `Fill` (background color), `Stroke` (border), `Layout Grids` ho sakte hain. Auto Layout aur Constraints *Frames* par lagte hain. **Rule: Jab doubt ho, Frame use karo.**
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Aap ek website bana rahe hain. Poori website (10 pages) 10 alag-alag 'Frames' mein design hogi, jo sab ek hi Canvas par rakhe honge.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Hamesha `F` (Frame) use karo screen banane ke liye. `R` (Rectangle) nahi.
    * Layers Panel mein hamesha apne elements ko rename karo (Shortcut: `Ctrl+R` ya `Cmd+R`).
    * Jo elements move nahi karne (jaise background), unhe Layer Panel mein 'Lock' ğŸ”’ kardo.
    * Apne Frames ko Canvas par align karke rakho (left-to-right).
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Canvas ka color kaise badlein?** Canvas par kahin bhi (Frame ke baahar) click karein aur Right Panel mein 'Page' ke neeche 'Fill' color badlein.
    * **Layer ko upar-neeche kaise karein?** Layers Panel mein drag-and-drop karein. Ya element select karke `[` (peeche) aur `]` (aage) use karein.
    * **Frame ka size kaise badlein?** Frame ko select karein aur Right Panel mein 'W' (width) aur 'H' (height) badlein.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. Ek "Desktop" preset ka Frame banayein (e.g., "Desktop 1440").
    * 2. Ek "Google Pixel 6" preset ka Frame banayein.
    * 3. Layers Panel mein, "Desktop" waale Frame ko lock ğŸ”’ kar dein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Sections:** (Toolbar mein). Yeh Frames ko group karne ke liye hai. (Jaise "Mobile Screens" ka ek section, "Web Screens" ka doosra).

---

### 1.4: Shapes, Text, Selection, aur Grouping

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Basic Tools (Shapes, Text, Selection, Grouping) ğŸ¨ (Design ke building blocks).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):**
    * **Selection (V):** Aapka default mouse cursor (Arrow). Elements ko select karne, move karne, ya resize karne ke liye.
    * **Shapes (R, O, L):** Basic shapes jaise Rectangle `(R)`, Oval/Circle `(O)`, Line `(L)`, Polygon, Star.
    * **Text (T):** Text (content) likhne ke liye.
    * **Grouping (Ctrl+G):** Multiple elements (e.g., ek rectangle aur uske upar text) ko ek saath baandhne (group) ke liye, taaki woh ek saath move hon.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Inhi se saara UI banta hai. Ek Button = Ek Rectangle `(R)` + Ek Text `(T)`. Ek Profile Picture = Ek Circle `(O)`. Inke bina aap kuch bana nahi sakte.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Aap inhe design process ke har second mein use karenge.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aap design nahi bana payenge.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Concept breakdown:**
    * `R` (Rectangle) se aap button background, cards, aur content blocks banate hain.
    * `O` (Oval) se aap profile pictures, avatars, ya status indicators banate hain.
    * `T` (Text) se aap headings, paragraphs, aur button labels likhte hain.
    * `Ctrl+G` (Group) se aap in sabko combine karte hain (jaise ek icon + label) taaki woh ek unit ban jaaye.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek basic "Sign Up" button banana (bina Auto Layout ke).
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  `F` daba kar ek Frame banayein (taaki hum uske andar kaam karein).
        2.  `R` daba kar ek Rectangle banayein. Right Panel mein 'Fill' se uska color badlein (e.g., Blue).
        3.  `T` daba kar us rectangle ke *upar* click karein aur "Sign Up" likhein.
        4.  Right Panel (Text section) mein, 'Fill' ko White karein aur 'Font Weight' ko "Medium" ya "SemiBold" karein.
        5.  Text ko rectangle ke andar manually (haath se) center mein rakhein.
        6.  Shift daba kar dono (Rectangle aur Text) ko select karein.
        7.  `Ctrl+G` (ya `Cmd+G` Mac par) dabayein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapke Layers Panel mein ek "Group 1" ban jayega. Ab aap us group ko kahin bhi move karenge, toh rectangle aur text saath mein move honge.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Elements ko group na karna. (Button ka text kahin aur, background kahin aur move ho jaata hai).
    * Text ko manually center align karne ki koshish karna (Top right mein 'Alignment' tools use karein).
    * **Group (Ctrl+G) aur Frame (F) mein confuse hona.** (Aage hum sikhenge ki 'Auto Layout' Frame, 'Grouping' se behtar tareeka hai button banane ka).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main 'Group' (Ctrl+G) kab use karun aur 'Frame' (F) kab?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Shuruaat mein, student har cheez ke liye 'Group' use karta hai (jaise ek icon aur uska label). Yeh aasan hai.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** **Pro Rule:** Professionals 'Group' (Ctrl+G) bohot kam use karte hain. Woh 'Frame' (F) ya 'Auto Layout Frame' (Shift+A) ka istemaal karte hain.
        * **Group:** Tab use karein jab aapko bas cheezon ko *ek saath* move karna hai (jaise ek illustration ke parts).
        * **Frame:** Tab use karein jab aapko us container ka apna `background color`, `padding` (spacing), ya `responsive rules` (Auto Layout/Constraints) chahiye. **Ek Button hamesha ek Frame hona chahiye, Group nahi.** (Yeh hum Module 4 mein detail mein sikhenge).
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek logo (jisme 2-3 shapes hain) ko 'Group' kiya jaata hai. Lekin ek "Product Card" (jisme image, title, price hai) ko 'Frame' banaya jaata hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Shapes aur Text ko hamesha 'Frame' ke andar rakhein.
    * `V` (Selection) tool par wapas aane ki aadat daalein.
    * Text ko align karne ke liye Right Panel ke 'Alignment' tools (Align center, Align middle) ka istemaal karein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Group ko ungroup kaise karein?** Group select karein aur `Ctrl+Shift+G` (ya `Cmd+Shift+G`) dabayein.
    * **Text ki properties (font, size) kahan hain?** Element ko select karein aur Right Panel mein 'Text' section dekhein.
    * **Shape ka color kahan se badlein?** Shape select karein aur Right Panel mein 'Fill' (andar ka color) ya 'Stroke' (border) section dekhein.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. Ek Circle `(O)` banayein.
    * 2. Uske neeche Text `(T)` mein "Profile" likhein.
    * 3. Dono ko select karke 'Group' `(Ctrl+G)` karein.
    * 4. Us group ko move karke dekhein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Auto Layout:** Yeh 'Grouping' ka super-advanced version hai. Hum isse Module 4 mein master karenge.

---

### 1.5: View Options (Design vs Prototype vs Inspect)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** View Options (Design / Prototype / Inspect) ğŸ‘ï¸ (Kaam badalne ke tabs).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh **Right Panel (Inspector)** ke top par 3 tabs hote hain. Yeh aapka "context" (kaam karne ka mode) switch karte hain.
    * **Design:** Yahan aap cheezon ka look (color, size, font, spacing) badalte hain.
    * **Prototype:** Yahan aap screens ko link karte hain (clickable banate hain).
    * **Inspect:** Yahan aap (ya developers) design ka code (CSS, Swift, Android XML) dekhte hain.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yeh Figma ka "all-in-one" nature dikhata hai. Yeh interface ko clean rakhta hai. Jab aap design kar rahe hain, toh aapko prototype ke options nahi dikhte, aur jab prototype kar rahe hain, toh color ke options nahi dikhte.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):**
    * **Design Tab:** 90% of the time, jab aap UI bana rahe hote hain.
    * **Prototype Tab:** Jab aapka design (kam se kam 2 screens) ready ho aur aap unhe jodna chahte hon.
    * **Inspect Tab:** Jab aap developers ko file handoff kar rahe hon.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aap confuse ho jayenge. Aap 'Design' tab mein 'Prototyping' ke options (jaise 'onClick') dhoondhte rahenge aur woh aapko milenge nahi.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Concept breakdown:** Yeh 3 alag-alag "modes" hain aapke Right Panel ke liye. Aapka baaki UI (Toolbar, Layers) same rehta hai, sirf Right Panel badalta hai.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Design se Prototype mode mein switch karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Apne canvas par ek 'Frame' select karein.
        2.  **Right Panel** mein dekhein. By default, `Design` tab selected hoga. Aapko Fill, Stroke, Auto Layout ke options dikhenge.
        3.  Ab, `Design` tab ke aage `Prototype` tab par click karein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Right Panel poora badal jayega. Ab aapko 'Interactions' (e.g., "Add interaction") aur 'Flows' ke options dikhenge. Design waale options (Fill, Stroke) gayab ho jayenge.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Yeh bhool jaana ki yeh 3 tabs exist karte hain.
    * 'Design' tab mein rehkar 'Prototyping' options dhoondhna (e.g., "Main is button ko link kaise karun?").
    * 'Inspect' tab mein galti se chale jaana aur confuse ho jaana.
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Yeh 'Inspect' tab mere (designer ke) kis kaam ka hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Aap pehle 1-2 din `Design` tab mein kaam karenge (poora UI banayenge). Phir, 1 ghante ke liye `Prototype` tab mein jaakar sab screens ko link karenge. Phir client ko link bhej denge.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Designers 95% time `Design` aur `Prototype` tabs mein rehte hain. Developers (jinke paas 'View Only' access hota hai) 95% time `Inspect` tab mein rehte hain. Woh wahin se padding, font size, aur color codes (`#FFFFFF`) copy karte hain.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Designer `Design` tab mein Button ka color 'Blue' set karta hai. Developer `Inspect` tab mein jaata hai aur usse seedha CSS mil jaata hai: `background-color: #0D99FF;`.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Design (Looks) ke liye -> `Design` Tab.
    * Interaction (Linking) ke liye -> `Prototype` Tab.
    * Code (Specs) ke liye -> `Inspect` Tab.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Yeh tabs kahan hain?** Right Panel (Inspector) ke bilkul top par.
    * **Mera Right Panel gayab ho gaya hai!** Aapne 'View' menu se 'Show/Hide UI' kar diya hoga, ya `Ctrl + \` (Cmd + \) daba diya hoga.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. Ek Frame select karein.
    * 2. `Design` tab mein uska 'Fill' (color) badlein.
    * 3. `Prototype` tab par click karein (options note karein).
    * 4. `Inspect` tab par click karein (aur dekhein CSS code kaise dikhta hai).
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Developer Handoff:** Hum Module 10 mein 'Inspect' tab ko detail mein cover karenge.

---

### 1.6: Zaroori Shortcuts

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Zaroori Shortcuts âš¡ï¸ (Speed se kaam karne ke liye).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh keyboard commands (hotkeys) hain jo aapko tools (mouse se) select kiye bina use karne dete hain.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Speed! Ek professional designer aur beginner mein sabse bada fark 'speed' ka hota hai. Professionals mouse ko kam se kam use karte hain. Toolbar par click karna (e.g., Text tool lene ke liye) bohot slow hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** **Hamesha!** Inhe pehle din se yaad karne ki koshish karein. Problem: Har tool ke liye mouse ko toolbar tak le jaana.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka workflow bohot slow (dheema) hoga. Aap "junior" designer lagenge. Simple tasks (ek button banana) mein bhi bohot time lagega.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Concept breakdown:** Har zaroori tool ka ek 'single-key' shortcut hai.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Bina toolbar (mouse) use kiye ek button banana.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation (Shortcuts):**
        1.  `F` dabayein (Frame tool activate hoga) -> Ek frame banayein.
        2.  `R` dabayein (Rectangle tool) -> Frame ke andar ek rectangle banayein.
        3.  `T` dabayein (Text tool) -> Rectangle ke upar "Click Me" likhein.
        4.  `V` dabayein (Move tool/Selection tool) -> Text ko select karke rectangle ke center mein rakhein.
        5.  `V` se, Shift daba kar, Rectangle aur Text dono ko select karein.
        6.  `Ctrl + G` dabayein (Group karne ke liye).
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapne 5-10 seconds mein ek button bana liya, bina ek baar bhi top toolbar par click kiye.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Shortcuts yaad hi na karna.
    * Kaam karne ke baad 'V' (Move tool) par wapas na aana. (Jaise 'T' se text likha aur fir 'T' active rehte hue hi kahin aur click kar diya, naya text box ban jayega).
    * Mac (Cmd) aur Windows (Ctrl) ke shortcuts mein confuse hona.
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Itne saare shortcuts hain, main kaise yaad karun?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Aapko saare yaad nahi karne. Bas 5-6 sabse zaroori waale (Tools aur Navigation) se shuru karein.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Professionals ka ek haath hamesha keyboard par hota hai. Woh 'V', 'F', 'R', 'T' ke beech muscle memory se switch karte hain. 'Spacebar' (Pan) aur 'Ctrl + Scroll' (Zoom) poore din use hota hai.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek designer ko canvas "Pan" (move) karna hai. Beginner: Mouse se scrollbar dhoondhega. Professional: `Spacebar` dabayega aur click-drag karega. (1 second vs 5 second).
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices (Must-Know Shortcuts):**
    * **Tools:**
        * `V`: Move / Select (Sabse zaroori. Har kaam ke baad 'V' dabayein).
        * `F`: Frame
        * `R`: Rectangle
        * `T`: Text
        * `O`: Oval / Circle
    * **Navigation:**
        * `Spacebar + Drag`: Pan (Canvas ko move karna).
        * `Ctrl/Cmd + Scroll`: Zoom In / Zoom Out.
        * `Shift + 1`: Zoom to Fit (Sab kuch fit karke dikhao).
        * `Shift + 2`: Zoom to Selection (Selected cheez par zoom karo).
    * **Actions:**
        * `Ctrl/Cmd + G`: Group
        * `Ctrl/Cmd + D`: Duplicate (Copy-Paste se tez).
        * `Ctrl/Cmd + R`: Rename Layer.
        * `Ctrl/Cmd + Alt + K`: Component banana (Boht zaroori, aage sikhenge).
        * `Alt + Drag`: Duplicate (Drag karte hue 'Alt' dabao).
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Saare shortcuts kahan milenge?** Figma mein, neeche-right (bottom-right) corner mein `?` (Help) icon par click karein, aur "Keyboard Shortcuts" chunein. Ek interactive panel khul jayega.
    * **Mac aur Windows mein kya fark hai?** `Ctrl` (Windows) = `Cmd` (Mac). `Alt` (Windows) = `Option` (Mac).
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. Sirf keyboard shortcuts use karke (V, F, R, T, O) ek basic profile card banayein (Ek 'Frame' (F), usmein ek 'Circle' (O) profile pic ke liye, aur 'Rectangle' (R) + 'Text' (T) naam ke liye).
    * 2. `Spacebar` daba kar canvas ko move (pan) karein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Figma Shortcut Cheat Sheets:** Google par search karein, aapko bohot si images mil jayengi.

---

Yeh tha hamara Module 1! ğŸ¥³ Humne Figma ka basic setup, interface, aur sabse zaroori tools (Frames, Shapes, Text) ko cover kar liya hai. Foundations set ho gayi hain.

Jab aap ready hon, bas **"Module 2 shuru karo"** likh dena, aur hum design *process* (sochne ka tareeka, FigJam, wireframing) seekhna shuru karenge!


=============================================================

Chalo bhai, shuru karte hain aapke Figma (Beginner-to-Job-Ready) notes ka Module 2!

Module 1 mein humne tools seekhe (kya *bana* sakte hain). Ab Module 2 mein hum process seekhenge (kya *sochna* hai). Yeh module aapko ek "Tool User" se "Designer" banayega.

---

### 2.1: FigJam (Brainstorming & Ideation)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** FigJam ğŸ§  (Figma ka Whiteboard tool).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** FigJam, Figma ka hi ek doosra tool hai, jo ek **online digital whiteboard** hai. Yeh design *karne* ke liye nahi, balki design se *pehle* ideas jama karne (brainstorming), user flows, aur diagrams banane ke liye hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Kyunki achha design seedha high-fidelity (sundar) screens banane se shuru nahi hota. Woh pehle research, brainstorming, aur planning se shuru hota hai. FigJam aapko (aur aapki team ko) woh "messy" (raw) ideas discuss karne ki jagah deta hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Project ke **bilkul shuruaati phase** mein. Jab aapko problem ka solution dhoondhna ho. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh us problem ko solve karta hai jahan aap seedha Figma (design file) mein jump karke "Login Page" banane lagte hain, bina yeh soche ki "User ko login kyun karna hai?" ya "Login ke baad kya hoga?".
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka design process kamzor hoga. Aap features (design) bana denge jinki user ko zaroorat hi nahi thi. Aap "solutions" par jump kar jayenge, bina "problem" ko theek se samjhe. Team collaboration mushkil hogi.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Concept breakdown:**
    * Yeh ek alag file type hai (`.figjam` vs `.fig`).
    * Ismein tools alag hote hain: Sticky Notes, Connectors (arrows), Shapes, Text, Stamps (voting ke liye).
    * Iska canvas bhi infinite hota hai.
    * Yeh collaboration ke liye bana hai.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek "Food Delivery App" ke features brainstorm karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Figma ke dashboard se "New FigJam file" kholein.
        2.  Neeche toolbar se 'Sticky Note' (ya shortcut `S`) select karein.
        3.  Canvas par click karein aur apna idea likhein (e.g., "Restaurant Search").
        4.  Ek aur sticky note banayein ("Live Order Tracking").
        5.  Ek aur banayein ("Ratings & Reviews").
        6.  Ab toolbar se 'Connector' (arrow) lein aur in ideas ko jodein (agar woh related hain).
        7.  Apne team members ko file ka link share karein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapke paas ek digital whiteboard hoga jispar alag-alag color ki sticky notes par aapke app ke saare possible features likhe honge.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * FigJam mein *UI design* (High-fidelity) karne ki koshish karna. (Galat! Yeh uske liye nahi hai).
    * Figma design file (`.fig`) mein sticky notes dhoondhna. (Galat! Woh FigJam mein hain).
    * Sticky notes ko organize na karna, bas canvas par faila dena.
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main toh akela kaam karta hoon, mujhe brainstorming ki kya zaroorat hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Aap akele bhi brainstorm kar sakte hain! FigJam ko aap apne "digital rough notebook" ki tarah use karein. Client se mile project requirements ko sticky notes mein todo. Apne ideas (jo aapko lagta hai achhe hain) wahan likho. Isse aapko clarity milegi.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Ek poori team (Designer, Product Manager, Engineer) ek FigJam call par hoti hai. PM user problem batata hai. Sab log 5 minute tak 'Silent Brainstorming' karte hain (apne-apne ideas sticky notes par likhte hain). Phir sab apne ideas discuss karte hain aur 'Stamps' (voting) se best ideas chunte hain.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek team "User Onboarding" process ko improve karne ke liye FigJam use karti hai. Woh har step (Sign Up, Verify Email, Add Profile Pic) ko ek sticky note par likhte hain aur unhe arrows se jodkar "flow" banate hain.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Design (Figma) mein jump karne se pehle FigJam mein 'socho'.
    * Sticky notes ko group karna (e.g., saare 'Payment' related ideas ek saath).
    * Clear titles aur text ka istemaal karein.
    * Apne FigJam boards ko Figma project file ke paas hi rakhein taaki sab organized rahe.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Kya FigJam free hai?** Haan, Figma ke free plan mein FigJam ki files bhi included hain (kuch limitations ke saath).
    * **FigJam vs Miro/Mural?** Teeno similar whiteboard tools hain. FigJam ka sabse bada fayda hai ki yeh Figma ke saath seamlessly integrated (juda hua) hai. Aap Figma designs ko FigJam mein copy-paste kar sakte hain.
    * **Main FigJam se Figma file mein kaise jaun?** Aap dono alag-alag tabs mein khol sakte hain.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. Ek nayi FigJam file banayein.
    * 2. Ek "Travel Booking Website" ke 5 main features sticky notes par likhein (e.g., Flight Search, Hotel Booking, User Profile, etc.).
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Miro, Mural:** Popular alternative whiteboarding tools.
    * **Templates:** FigJam mein bohot saare built-in templates hote hain (e.g., "Brainstorming", "User Flow Diagram"). Unhe zaroor explore karein.

---

### 2.2: User Journeys & Site Maps

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** User Journeys aur Site Maps (User ka raasta plan karna).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):**
    * **Site Map:** Yeh aapki website ya app ka "blueprint" (naksha) hota hai. Yeh ek hierarchical diagram (tree jaisa) hota hai jo dikhata hai ki kaun se pages hain aur woh kaise organized hain (e.g., Home -> About Us, Home -> Products -> Product Detail).
    * **User Journey (ya User Flow):** Yeh ek diagram hai jo dikhata hai ki ek user kisi *task ko poora karne* ke liye aapki app mein kin-kin steps aur screens se guzrega. (e.g., App Open -> Click Login -> Enter Email/Pass -> Click Submit -> Arrive at Homepage).
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yeh aapko "individual screens" (ek screen) ki jagah "poora experience" (poora raasta) design karne mein madad karta hai. Agar aapko raasta (flow) clear nahi hai, toh aap aisi screens design kar denge jo ek doosre se judi hui (connected) nahi lagengi.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Brainstorming (FigJam) ke *baad*, aur Wireframing (actual design) se *pehle*. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh "Dead End" screens ki problem solve karta hai (e.g., user ne payment kar di, par ab 'Back' button nahi hai ya 'Go to Home' ka option nahi hai).
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka design toota-toota (disconnected) lagega. User confuse ho jayega. Aap important screens (jaise "Forgot Password" ya "Error Message") design karna hi bhool jayenge. Aapka prototype (clickable design) logical nahi banega.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Concept breakdown:**
    * **Site Map (Structure):** Focuses on *Information* aur *Hierarchy*. (Kya-kya hai?)
    * **User Flow (Path):** Focuses on *Tasks* aur *Steps*. (Kaise hoga?)
    * Dono ko banane ke liye FigJam best tool hai.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek "E-commerce App" ke liye "Product Purchase" ka User Flow banana.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation (in FigJam):**
        1.  Toolbar se 'Shape' tool (Square) lein. Ek box banayein aur "Home Screen" likhein.
        2.  Ek aur box banayein ("Product Detail Screen").
        3.  Ek 'Connector' (arrow) lein aur "Home Screen" se "Product Detail Screen" ko jodein. Arrow par "User clicks on product" likhein.
        4.  Aage ke steps add karein:
            * ... -> "Cart Screen" (Arrow: "User clicks 'Add to Cart'")
            * ... -> "Checkout Screen" (Arrow: "User clicks 'Proceed to Checkout'")
            * ... -> "Payment Screen" (Arrow: "User enters address")
            * ... -> "Order Confirmation Screen" (Arrow: "User clicks 'Pay Now'")
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapke paas ek complete visual map hoga jo dikhata hai ki ek user ko product khareedne ke liye kin-kin screens se jaana padega.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Site Map aur User Flow ko ek hi cheez samajhna.
    * Sirf "Happy Path" design karna (jab sab a-chha hota hai). "Sad Paths" (e.g., "Payment Fail ho gaya toh kya hoga?") ko bhool jaana.
    * User Flow ko bohot complex bana dena.
    * Figma design file mein hi flow banane ki koshish karna (FigJam iske liye behtar hai).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main seedha screens design karke unhe prototype mein kyun nahi jod sakta? Yeh (User Flow) toh extra kaam lag raha hai."
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Aap pehle FigJam mein 5-6 boxes (screens) ka flow banate hain. Isse aapko pata chalta hai ki "Oh, mujhe 'Order Confirmation' screen bhi banani hai." Phir aap Figma design file mein jaate hain aur unhi 5-6 screens ke *Frames* banate hain. Aapka kaam organized ho jaata hai.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Product Manager aur Designer milkar FigJam mein User Flows define karte hain. Woh har possible scenario (happy path, sad path, error states) ko map karte hain. Yeh flow hi unka "To-Do List" ban jaata hai. (e.g., "Humein yeh 7 screens design karni hain").
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek food delivery app ka "Order" flow design karna. Ismein "Restaurant closed hai toh kya hoga?" ya "Delivery agent nahi mila toh kya hoga?" jaise 'sad paths' bhi FigJam mein map kiye jaate hain.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Simple rakhein (Boxes aur Arrows).
    * Har arrow par action (e.g., "User clicks...") likhein.
    * "Happy Path" ke saath-saath "Sad Paths" (errors) ke baare mein bhi sochein.
    * Apne User Flow ko FigJam mein banayein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Pehle Site Map banta hai ya User Flow?** Aksar pehle Site Map (structure) banta hai, phir us structure ke upar User Flows (tasks) banaye jaate hain.
    * **User Flow kitna detailed hona chahiye?** Itna ki developer ko samajh aa jaaye ki user kahan se kahan jayega. Har chote click (jaise pop-up) ko dikhana zaroori nahi.
    * **Yeh UX (User Experience) hai ya UI (User Interface)?** Yeh 100% UX design ka core part hai.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. Apni FigJam file mein, ek "Login Flow" banayein. Ismein "Forgot Password" ka 'sad path' bhi include karein. (e.g., Login Screen -> Forgot Password -> Enter Email -> Reset Link Sent).
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Autoflow (Plugin):** Figma/FigJam plugin jo do objects ko select karke automatic arrow (connector) bana deta hai.

---

### 2.3: Wireframing (Low-Fidelity Design)

**(Yeh ek CORE Foundational concept hai. Poora dhyaan dein.)**

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Wireframing (Low-Fidelity Design) ğŸ“ (Design ka 'kacha chittha' ya skeleton).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Wireframe ek **low-fidelity** (Lo-Fi) ya basic blueprint hota hai ek screen ka. Ismein *sirf* structure (layout), content (kahan kya aayega), aur functionality (button kya karega) par focus hota hai. Ismein **koi colors, fonts, ya final images nahi** hote. Sab kuch grey boxes aur simple text hota hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Kyunki yeh **bohot tez (fast)** bante hain. Yeh aapko design ke *layout* par focus karne deta hai, na ki uske *look* par. Agar aap seedha sundar (High-Fidelity) design banayenge, toh aap "Blue color" par 1 ghanta waste kar denge, jabki zaroori tha "Button ki position".
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** User Flows final hone ke *baad*. High-Fidelity design se *pehle*. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh us problem ko solve karta hai jahan aap 10 ghante laga kar ek "perfect" Home Page banate hain, aur fir client/manager kehta hai "Layout hi galat hai, sab kuch change karo." Wireframe par feedback lena aasan aur sasta (time ke maamle mein) hota hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka bohot saara time waste hoga. Aap colors, fonts, aur shadows mein ulajh jayenge, jabki aapka basic layout (information hierarchy) hi galat hoga. Changes karna bohot mushkil aur time-consuming ho jayega.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Concept breakdown:**
    * **Low-Fidelity (Lo-Fi) Wireframe:** (Jo hum yahan seekh rahe hain). Sirf grey boxes aur basic text. (Tool: Figma/FigJam).
    * **Medium-Fidelity (Mid-Fi):** Thoda aur detail, real text, par abhi bhi colors/images nahi.
    * **High-Fidelity (Hi-Fi):** Final pixel-perfect design, colors, fonts, images ke saath.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek "Home Page" ka Lo-Fi Wireframe banana (Figma Design File mein).
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Ek naya 'Page' (Left Panel) banayein aur naam rakhein "ğŸš§ Wireframes".
        2.  `F` daba kar ek "Desktop" Frame banayein.
        3.  `R` (Rectangle) se, top par ek lamba box banayein. Yeh aapka "Navbar" (Header) hai.
        4.  `R` se ek bohot bada box banayein "Hero Section" ke liye. Uske andar 'X' bana dein (yeh image ka placeholder hota hai).
        5.  `T` (Text) se "Main Heading" likhein (Font: Inter, Size: 48, Color: Black).
        6.  Neeche 3 medium size ke 'Rectangles' banayein "Features Section" ke liye.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapke paas ek basic, grey-and-white layout hoga jo dikhata hai ki Home Page par kahan kya hoga, bina kisi "design" (color/font) ke.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * **Wireframes mein colors add kar dena.** (Nahi karna!).
    * "Perfect" font dhoondhne mein time waste karna. (Sirf default 'Inter' ya 'Arial' use karein).
    * Real images (Unsplash se) daal dena. (Sirf grey box banakar uspar 'X' banayein).
    * Wireframing skip karke seedha Hi-Fi design par jump kar jaana. (Sabse badi galti!).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Yeh toh bohot plain (saada) aur boring lag raha hai. Main client ko yeh kaise dikhaunga?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Aap client ko samjhayenge ki "Yeh final design nahi hai. Abhi hum *sirf layout aur content* par focus kar rahe hain. Please colors ko ignore karein aur batayein ki kya saari zaroori information sahi jagah par hai?" Isse aapko better feedback milega.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Designers pehle Lo-Fi wireframes banate hain. In wireframes ko *prototype* (clicky) banakar internal team (PMs, Engineers) se test karwate hain. Jab sab agree karte hain ki "haan, layout theek hai aur flow sahi kaam kar raha hai," *tab hi* UI Designer us wireframe ko High-Fidelity (sundar) banana shuru karta hai.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek poori app (e.g., 20 screens) ko pehle 2 din mein Lo-Fi wireframes mein design kiya jaata hai. Layout final hone ke baad, agle 2 hafte unhe Hi-Fi banaya jaata hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * **Stick to Grayscale:** Sirf Black, White, aur grey ke shades use karein.
    * **Use One Font:** Koi bhi ek system font (e.g., Inter) use karein.
    * **Focus on Hierarchy:** Kya important hai (badi heading), kya kam important hai (chota text).
    * **Use Placeholders:** Images ke liye [X] use karein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Wireframe FigJam mein banayein ya Figma mein?** Dono mein ban sakte hain. Agar bohot rough aur 'sketchy' banana hai, toh FigJam. Agar thoda clean (box-wala) banana hai jise baad mein Hi-Fi mein convert karna hai, toh Figma Design File (jaise humne exercise mein kiya).
    * **Kya wireframes ko prototype karna chahiye?** Haan! Lo-Fi prototype banana bohot common hai. Isse aap layout aur flow dono ko jaldi test kar lete hain.
    * **Low-Fidelity aur High-Fidelity mein kya fark hai?** Lo-Fi (Structure) vs Hi-Fi (Visual Polish).
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. Apni Figma file ke "Wireframes" page par, ek mobile frame (`F` -> iPhone 14) lein.
    * 2. Ek "Login Screen" ka Lo-Fi wireframe banayein (Sirf boxes aur text use karke: Logo ke liye ek box, "Email" field ke liye box, "Password" field ke liye box, aur "Login" button ke liye ek box).
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Balsamiq:** Ek dedicated tool jo sirf Lo-Fi wireframes banane ke liye hi famous hai.

---

### 2.4: Atomic Design (Philosophy)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Atomic Design âš›ï¸ (Chote parts se bada system banana).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh ek **design methodology** (sochne ka tareeka) hai, tool nahi. Ismein aap UI ko chote-chote building blocks mein tod dete hain, bilkul Chemistry ki tarah.
    * **Atoms (Parmanu):** Sabse chote elements jinhe aur toda nahi jaa sakta (e.g., ek Color, ek Font, ek Icon, ek Text label).
    * **Molecules (Anu):** Atoms ka group jo milkar ek kaam karta (e.g., ek Input Field = Label (Atom) + Text Box (Atom) + Border Color (Atom)).
    * **Organisms (Jeev):** Molecules ka group jo ek section banata (e.g., ek Header = Logo (Atom) + Navigation Links (Molecule) + Search Bar (Molecule)).
    * **Templates:** Organisms ko milakar poora page *layout* (bina real content ke).
    * **Pages:** Template mein jab real content (images, text) daal diya jaata hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yeh "Design Systems" (jo hum aage sikhenge) ki neenv (foundation) hai. Yeh aapko *consistent* (ek jaisa) aur *scalable* (bada karne laayak) design banane mein madad karta hai. Aap "har baar" naya button nahi banate, aap pehle se banaye hue "Button Molecule" ko reuse karte hain.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Jab aap apna project shuru kar rahe hon aur apne 'Components' (Module 6) ko plan kar rahe hon. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh "Inconsistency" (alag-alag design) ki problem solve karta hai. (e.g., Ek screen par Blue button, doosri par Dark Blue button. Ek jagah font 16px, doosri jagah 17px).
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka design "khichdi" ban jayega. Har screen thodi alag dikhegi. Agar client ne kaha "Saare buttons ka color badal do," toh aapko 100 jagah jaakar manually (haath se) badalna padega. Aapka workflow bohot slow aur inefficient hoga.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Concept breakdown:**
    * **Atom:** Color: `#007BFF` (Blue)
    * **Atom:** Text Style: "16px Medium"
    * **Molecule (Button):** [Rectangle (jismein `#007BFF` Atom hai)] + [Text (jismein "16px Medium" Atom hai)]
    * **Organism (Login Form):** [Email Input (Molecule)] + [Password Input (Molecule)] + [Login Button (Molecule)]
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Atomic Design ke hisaab se sochna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  **Identify Atoms:** Apne design ko dekhein. Sabse choti cheezein kya hain? Colors (Primary, Secondary, Text Color). Font Styles (Heading 1, Body). Icons.
        2.  **Plan Molecules:** In atoms se kya banega? Ek button, ek search bar, ek list item.
        3.  **Plan Organisms:** In molecules se kya banega? Ek Navbar, ek Footer, ek Product Card.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapke dimaag mein ek clear structure hoga ki aapko pehle choti, reusable cheezein (Components) banani hain, aur phir unhe jodkar badi cheezein banani hain.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Is concept se confuse ho jaana. (Yaad rakhein: Yeh sirf ek 'sochne ka tareeka' hai, Figma mein 'Atom' naam ka koi tool nahi hai).
    * Seedha 'Organisms' (e.g., poora header) design karna, bina 'Atoms' (colors, fonts) define kiye.
    * Har cheez ko 'Atom' ya 'Molecule' mein fit karne ki koshish karna. Yeh ek guide hai, strict rule nahi.
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main toh bas ek 5-page ki simple website bana raha hoon. Kya mujhe itna complicate karne ki zaroorat hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Haan! Aapko "Atomic Design" naam lene ki zaroorat nahi, par concept use karna hai. Iska matlab hai:
        1.  Pehle (Module 5 mein) apne **Colors aur Text Styles** define karo (Yeh aapke Atoms hain).
        2.  Phir (Module 6 mein) apne **Reusable Components** (jaise Button, Navbar) banao (Yeh aapke Molecules/Organisms hain).
        3.  Phir un components ko use karke apni pages (Screens) banao.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Poori Design System Team (jo badi companies mein hoti hai) Atomic Design par hi chalti hai. Unki Figma file mein "Atoms" (Colors, Typography), "Molecules" (Buttons, Inputs), aur "Organisms" (Headers, Cards) ke alag-alag 'Pages' (jo humne 1.2 mein seekha) bane hote hain.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek designer ko "Profile Card" (Organism) banana hai. Woh `Avatar` (Molecule), `User Name` (Atom - Text), aur `Follow Button` (Molecule) ko 'Assets' panel se drag karta hai aur 10 second mein card bana deta hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Pehle choti cheezein design karo (Colors, Fonts).
    * Phir unhe jodkar badi cheezein banao (Components).
    * **Don't Repeat Yourself (DRY):** Agar aap ek hi cheez (jaise button) ko copy-paste kar rahe ho, toh aap galat kar rahe ho. Uska 'Component' banao.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Yeh Figma mein kaise karte hain?** Yeh concept Figma ke **Styles** (Atoms) aur **Components** (Molecules/Organisms) features se laagu (implement) hota hai.
    * **Yeh Brad Frost kaun hai?** Brad Frost woh designer hain jinhone yeh 'Atomic Design' methodology popular ki thi.
    * **Kya yeh zaroori hai?** Haan, agar aap professional, scalable designs banana chahte hain toh yeh 'soch' bohot zaroori hai.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. (Mental Exercise) Ek "Twitter/X Post" (jaise aap timeline mein dekhte hain) ko dekhein.
    * 2. Uske Atoms (Colors, Font styles, Icons), Molecules (Like/RT/Reply buttons), aur Organism (poora post) ko identify (pehchanne) ki koshish karein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **"Atomic Design" by Brad Frost:** (Yeh original kitaab hai is concept par).
    * **Figma Styles & Components:** (Yeh Figma ke tools hain is concept ko laagu karne ke liye. Module 5 & 6 mein aa rahe hain).

---

Yeh tha hamara Module 2! ğŸ§  Humne seekha ki design shuru karne se pehle *socha* kaise jaata haiâ€”FigJam mein brainstorming se lekar, User Flows, Wireframes, aur Atomic Design ki philosophy tak.

Aapka foundation ab bohot strong ho raha hai.

Jab aap ready hon, bas **"Module 3 shuru karo"** likh dena, aur hum design ke core tools (Images, Pen Tool, Masking) mein dive karenge!


=============================================================

Chalo bhai, shuru karte hain aapke Figma (Beginner-to-Job-Ready) notes ka Module 4!

WARNING: Yeh poore course ka **sabse zaroori module** hai ğŸš€. Yahi woh skills hain jo ek "Beginner" ko "Professional" designer se alag karti hain. Yahan hum seekhenge ki designs ko *flexible*, *responsive* (har screen size par chalne wala), aur *scalable* (aasaani se update hone wala) kaise banate hain.

Auto Layout, Grids, aur Constraints par poora dhyaan dena. Let's go!

---

### 4.1: Layout Grids (Columns)

**(Yeh ek CORE Foundational topic hai. Poora dhyaan dein.)**

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Layout Grids (Columns) ğŸ“ (Apne design ko organize karne ka framework).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Layout Grid ek visual guide (guide) hai jise aap apne 'Frame' ke upar lagate hain, taaki aap apne content (text, images, buttons) ko ek clean, organized, aur consistent tareeke se align kar sakein. Sabse common grid '12-Column Grid' hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yeh aapke design ko "professional look" deta hai. Iske bina, aapke elements (button, text) canvas par idhar-udhar "tairte" (floating) hue lagenge. Developers ke liye grid-based design ko code karna (e.g., Bootstrap, Tailwind CSS) 10 guna aasan hota hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** **Frame (screen) banate hi, design shuru karne se pehle.** Sabse pehla kadam. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh "Yeh button thoda left mein hona chahiye ya right mein?" waali problem ko solve karta hai. Grid aapko batata hai ki cheezon ko *kahan* rakhna hai. Har website aur app (desktop ya mobile) design karte waqt.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka design bohot messy (ganda) aur inconsistent lagega. Ek screen par heading left se 20px door hogi, doosri par 25px. Elements aligned nahi honge. Aapka design "amateur" lagega. Developers aapse nafrat karenge kyunki aapke design mein koi logic ya structure nahi hoga.
6.  **ğŸ§‘_ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**_
    * **Frame select karein:** Grid hamesha 'Frame' par lagta hai.
    * **Right Panel:** 'Layout Grid' section mein `+` icon dabayein.
    * **Grid vs Columns vs Rows:** Default 'Grid' (graph paper jaisa) aayega. Uske icon par click karke 'Columns' chunein.
    * **Count:** Kitne columns chahiye (e.g., Desktop ke liye `12`, Mobile ke liye `4` ya `6`).
    * **Gutter:** Columns ke beech ki khaali jagah (spacing) (e.g., `20px`).
    * **Margin:** Screen ke left aur right side mein khaali jagah (e.g., `24px` ya `100px`).
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek 'Desktop' (1440px) Frame par standard 12-column grid lagana.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  `F` daba kar ek Frame banayein. Right panel se 'Desktop' -> 'Desktop 1440' chunein.
        2.  Frame selected rakhein. Right Panel mein 'Layout Grid' par `+` dabayein.
        3.  Default 'Grid: 10px' aayega. Uske icon (grid jaisa) par click karein.
        4.  Dropdown se `Columns` chunein.
        5.  `Count` ko `12` karein. (Yeh 12 columns banayega).
        6.  `Type` ko `Stretch` hi rehne dein (taaki woh 1440px mein automatically adjust ho).
        7.  `Gutter` ko `24` karein (columns ke beech 24px space).
        8.  `Margin` ko `100` karein (left/right se 100px chhod kar grid shuru hoga).
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapke 1440px Frame par 12 laal (default color) columns ka ek grid aa jayega, jo aapko align karne mein help karega. Grid ko hide/show karne ka shortcut: `Ctrl+G` (Mac: `Cmd+G`).
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Grid ka istemaal hi na karna. (Sabse badi galti).
    * Har Frame (Mobile, Desktop) ke liye *ek hi* grid (e.g., 12-column) use karna. (Galat! Mobile ke liye 4 ya 6-column grid behtar hai).
    * Grid *banane* ke baad, elements ko usse align *na* karna.
    * 'Gutter' (beech ki space) aur 'Margin' (side ki space) mein confuse hona.
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main toh bas ek choti mobile app bana raha hoon, mujhe grid ki kya zaroorat hai? Main haath se (manually) align kar lunga."
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Manual alignment hamesha inconsistent hota hai. Ek student 4-column grid (Mobile ke liye) banata hai. Isse usse pata chalta hai ki saare elements ya toh 1st column se shuru honge, ya 2nd. Saari screens ek jaisi dikhti hain. Yeh consistency hi professional design hai.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Ek team project shuru karne se pehle hi 'Grid System' define karti hai. (e.g., "Desktop: 12-col, 24px gutter, 120px margin. Mobile: 4-col, 16px gutter, 20px margin"). Yeh unke 'Design System' ka part hota hai. Har designer *usi* grid ko follow karta hai.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek news website ka homepage dekhein. Saari story cards, ads, aur text perfectly columns mein aligned hote hain. Woh '12-column grid' use kar rahe hote hain. Ek article 8 column le sakta hai, aur side-bar 4 column le sakta hai (Total 12).
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Desktop ke liye 12-column grid use karein (kyunki 12 ko 2, 3, 4, 6 se divide kar sakte hain).
    * Mobile ke liye 4-column ya 6-column grid use karein.
    * Grid ko hide/show karne ke liye `Ctrl+G` (ya `Cmd+G`) ka istemaal karein.
    * Apne 'Layout Grid' ko ek 'Style' (style) bana lein (hum Module 5 mein sikhenge) taaki aap use har naye Frame par ek click mein laga sakein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Grid ka color (laal) kaise badlein?** 'Layout Grid' settings mein 'Color' property se.
    * **Kya main Gutter (beech ki space) mein design kar sakta hoon?** Nahi! Gutter ka matlab hi hai 'khaali jagah'. Elements hamesha *columns ke andar* hone chahiye, gutter ke upar nahi.
    * **12 columns hi kyun? 8 ya 10 kyun nahi?** Kyunki 12 sabse flexible number hai. Aap screen ko 50/50 (6+6), 33/33/33 (4+4+4), ya 25/75 (3+9) mein aasaani se baant sakte hain. 10-column mein yeh mushkil hai.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. Ek 'Mobile' (iPhone 14) Frame banayein aur uspar ek 4-column grid (Gutter: 16px, Margin: 20px) lagayein.
    * 2. Ek 'Desktop' (1440px) Frame banayein aur uspar 12-column grid (Gutter: 24px, Margin: 100px) lagayein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Bootstrap Grid System:** Google par search karein. Yeh web development ka sabse popular 12-column grid hai, jise Figma designers follow karte hain.

---

### 4.2: The 8-Point Grid (Spacing Philosophy)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** The 8-Point Grid ğŸ“ (Consistent spacing ke liye 'magic number').
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh ek design *philosophy* (sochne ka tareeka) ya 'system' hai, tool nahi. Yeh kehta hai ki aap apne design mein saari spacing, padding, aur element sizes ko **8 ke multiples** (gunank) mein rakhein (e.g., 8px, 16px, 24px, 32px, 40px...).
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Consistency! Isse aapke design mein ek visual rhythm (taal) aata hai. Yeh "decision fatigue" (sochne ki thakaan) ko khatam kar deta hai. Aapko yeh nahi sochna padta ki "Button ke neeche 20px space doon ya 22px?" Jawaab hamesha 8 ka multiple hoga (e.g., 16px ya 24px).
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Poore design process mein. Jab aap elements ke beech 'padding' (andar ki space) ya 'margin' (baahar ki space) de rahe hon. Jab aap element ka size (e.g., button height) define kar rahe hon. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh 'random spacing' (kahin 13px, kahin 15px, kahin 19px) ki problem ko solve karta hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka design inconsistent lagega. Aapke paas spacing values ka "zoo" hoga (11px, 17px, 23px...). Developers ko har element ke liye alag CSS value likhni padegi. Design scalable nahi hoga.
6.  **ğŸ§‘_ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**_
    * **Base Unit:** `8px` hamara base unit hai.
    * **Spacing Scale (Aapka Spacing System):**
        * `xs` (extra small) = 8px (e.g., ek icon aur text ke beech)
        * `s` (small) = 16px (e.g., ek input field ke andar padding)
        * `m` (medium) = 24px (e.g., form fields ke beech)
        * `l` (large) = 32px (e.g., related items ke beech)
        * `xl` (extra large) = 48px ya 64px (e.g., sections ke beech)
    * **Component Sizes:** Button ki height `40px` (8x5) ya `48px` (8x6). Input field ki height `48px`.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek 'Button' design karna 8-point grid se.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  `T` daba kar "Click Me" likhein.
        2.  Is text ko select karke `Shift+A` dabayein (Auto Layout, hum aage padhenge). Ek Frame ban jayega.
        3.  Right Panel (Auto Layout section) mein jaayein:
        4.  `Horizontal padding` (left/right) ko `24px` (8x3) set karein.
        5.  `Vertical padding` (top/bottom) ko `16px` (8x2) set karein.
        6.  Frame ko 'Fill' (background color) dein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapke paas ek perfect button hai jiski saari internal spacing 8 ke multiples mein hai.
    * **Tip (Figma 'Nudge'):** `Shift + Arrow Keys` se element 10px move hota hai. Ise 8px karne ke liye: Figma Menu (`F`) -> Preferences -> Nudge Amount -> Big Nudge ko `8` set kar dein. Ab `Shift + Arrow` se element 8px move hoga!
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Is rule ko bohot strictly follow karna (e.g., Font size). (Rule: Font size 8 ka multiple hona zaroori nahi hai. Standard font sizes 14px, 16px, 18px, 20px... theek hain. Yeh rule *spacing* ke liye hai).
    * Sochna ki 4px-grid galat hai. (Kuch log 4-point grid bhi use karte hain, jo 8-point ka hi hissa hai. 4px, 8px, 12px, 16px...).
    * 'Big Nudge' ko 8px set na karna aur manually 8px move karne ki koshish karna.
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "8 hi kyun? 10 (decimal system) aasan nahi hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** 10 achha number nahi hai kyunki 10 ko 2 aur 5 se hi divide kar sakte hain. 8 ko 2 aur 4 se kar sakte hain. Saath hi, 8-point grid iOS aur Android dono ke guidelines se match karta hai. Ek student apna 'Big Nudge' 8px set karke design banata hai, uski spacing hamesha clean aati hai.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Poora 'Design System' 8-point grid par bana hota hai. Unke paas 'spacing variables' (Token) hote hain (jaise `$space-01: 8px`, `$space-02: 16px`). Designers ko number use karne ki bhi zaroorat nahi hoti, woh bas token select karte hain.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Google ka 'Material Design' 8dp (density-independent pixel) grid par (mobile ke liye 4dp) bana hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Apna 'Big Nudge' amount `8px` set karein.
    * Spacing (Padding, Margin) ke liye 8 ke multiples (8, 16, 24, 32...) use karein.
    * Component sizes (Button height) ko 8 ke multiples (40, 48, 56...) mein rakhne ki koshish karein.
    * Font sizes ke liye yeh rule zaroori nahi hai.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **'Big Nudge' kahan se set karein?** Figma Icon (Menu) -> Preferences -> Nudge Amount -> Big Nudge.
    * **Agar 8px bohot zyada lage toh?** 4px use kar sakte hain. (Yeh 4-point grid system kehlata hai).
    * **Kya mujhe har cheez 8 se measure karni hai?** Nahi, yeh philosophy hai. Agar kahin 18px (jo 8 ka multiple nahi hai) behtar lag raha hai, toh use karein. Par koshish 16px ya 24px ki karein. Consistency > Strict Rules.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. Figma mein 'Big Nudge' ko 8px set karein.
    * 2. Ek Rectangle banayein. Use `Shift + Right Arrow` se move karke dekhein (woh 8px move hoga).
    * 3. Ek 'Profile Card' (Image + Text) banayein aur uske beech ki saari spacing 8px, 16px, ya 24px rakhne ki koshish karein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * Google 'Material Design 8pt Grid' - Is concept par sabse achha article.

---

### 4.3: Alignment aur Spacing Options

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Alignment & Spacing Options (Cheezon ko line mein lagana).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh **Right Panel ke top** par chote icons hote hain jo tab dikhte hain jab aap 2 ya 2 se zyada elements select karte hain. Yeh aapko elements ko ek doosre se (ya unke parent Frame se) perfectly align (left, right, center) karne dete hain.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Speed aur Precision (sateekta). Aap kabhi bhi 'haath se' (manually) do cheezon ko perfectly center align nahi kar sakte. Yeh tools 1-click mein kar dete hain. Clean design = Aligned design.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Hamesha. Jab bhi aapko 2 ya 2 se zyada cheezon ko line mein laana ho (e.g., 3 buttons ko vertically align karna). Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh 'pixel-perfect' alignment ki problem ko solve karta hai, jo manually karna impossible hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapke elements 1-2 pixel upar-neeche honge. Aapka design "thoda off" (ajeeb) lagega, bhale hi user bata na paaye ki kyun. Aapka bohot time waste hoga cheezon ko manually align karne mein.
6.  **ğŸ§‘_ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**_
    * **Alignment Tools (6 icons):**
        * Align Left, Align Horizontal Centers, Align Right
        * Align Top, Align Vertical Centers, Align Bottom
    * **Distribution Tools (2 icons):**
        * `Distribute Horizontal Spacing:` 3 ya 3+ elements ke beech *horizontal* (X-axis) space barabar kar deta hai.
        * `Distribute Vertical Spacing:` 3 ya 3+ elements ke beech *vertical* (Y-axis) space barabar kar deta hai.
    * **Tidy Up (Cleanup):** Yeh 'Distribution' ka smart version hai. Yeh elements ko grid mein arrange karta hai aur unke beech ki space ko barabar kar deta hai (jise aap manually adjust kar sakte hain).
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task 1:** Ek 'Rectangle' ko 'Frame' ke beech mein laana.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Ek Frame banayein. Uske andar ek chota Rectangle banayein (kahin bhi).
        2.  *Sirf Rectangle* ko select karein.
        3.  Right Panel (top) mein `Align Horizontal Centers` icon par click karein.
        4.  Phir `Align Vertical Centers` icon par click karein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Rectangle apne parent Frame ke bilkul beech (center) mein aa jayega.
    * **Task 2:** 3 rectangles ke beech ki space barabar karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  3 Rectangles banayein (alag-alag vertical spacing ke saath).
        2.  Teeno ko select karein.
        3.  Right Panel mein 'Distribution' section mein (ya Alignment icons ke neeche `...` menu mein) `Distribute Vertical Spacing` par click karein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Teeno rectangles ke beech ki vertical space automatically barabar ho jayegi.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * In tools ka istemaal hi na karna.
    * 'Align Horizontal Centers' (ek doosre ke upar center karna) aur 'Align Vertical Centers' (ek doosre ke side-by-side center karna) mein confuse hona.
    * 'Align Top' (sabko sabse upar waale element se align karna) aur 'Align to Top of Frame' (sabko Frame ke top se align karna) mein confuse hona.
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main 'Smart Guides' (pink lines) se align kar sakta hoon. In tools ki kya zaroorat hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Smart Guides 2 cheezon ke liye achhe hain. Lekin jab 5 cheezein (e.g., ek navigation bar mein 5 text links) ko align karna ho, toh Smart Guides fail ho jaate hain. Tab 'Align Vertical Centers' aur 'Distribute Horizontal Spacing' 1 second mein kaam kar dete hain.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Professionals *kabhi bhi* manually align nahi karte. Woh hamesha in tools par depend karte hain. Ya (jo hum aage seekhenge) woh 'Auto Layout' ka istemaal karte hain, jo alignment ko automatic kar deta hai.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek e-commerce 'Product Grid' mein 4 cards hain. Un sabko select karke 'Align Top' (taaki sab upar se line mein aa jaayein) aur 'Distribute Horizontal Spacing' (taaki unke beech ki jagah barabar ho) karna.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Alignment tools ko use karne ki aadat daalein.
    * Jab *ek* element select hota hai, toh woh 'Parent Frame' se align hota hai.
    * Jab *do ya do se zyada* element select hote hain, toh woh 'ek doosre se' align hote hain.
    * 3+ elements ke beech space barabar karne ke liye 'Distribute' ya 'Tidy Up' use karein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **'Tidy Up' kab use karein?** Jab aapke paas grid jaisa layout (e.g., 3x3 cards) ho aur aapko horizontal aur vertical, dono spacing ek saath theek karni ho.
    * **Spacing adjust kaise karein 'Tidy Up' ke baad?** Jab elements 'Tidy' ho jaate hain, unke beech mein pink lines aati hain. Aap un lines ko (ya space ko) click karke drag kar sakte hain, ya right panel mein number daal sakte hain (e.g., 16px).
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. Ek Frame ke andar 3 Circle banayein (alag-alag jagah). Teeno ko select karein aur unhe horizontally align karein ('Align Vertical Centers') aur unke beech ki space barabar karein ('Distribute Horizontal Spacing').
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Auto Layout:** Yeh (Topic 4.4) alignment aur spacing ka "automatic" version hai aur in manual tools se 100 guna behtar hai.

---

### 4.4: Auto Layout (Introduction)

**(Yeh Figma ka sabse POWERFUL aur CORE Foundational topic hai. Poora dhyaan dein.)**

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Auto Layout (Introduction) ğŸ§© (Content ke hisaab se badalne wala Frame).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Auto Layout ek 'Frame' property hai jo aapke elements ko *automatically* align karti hai aur unke beech ki spacing ko maintain rakhti hai. Jab content (e.g., text) badalta hai, toh Frame (e.g., button) ka size bhi apne aap badal jaata hai. Yeh "CSS Flexbox" jaisa hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yeh aapka **90% time bachata hai**. Iske bina, agar aapne ek button (Rectangle + Text) banaya aur text "Buy" se "Add to Cart" kiya, toh aapko Rectangle (background) ko manually (haath se) bada karna padega. Auto Layout mein, button *apne aap* bada ho jaata hai. Yeh 'Responsive Design' ki neenv (foundation) hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** **Har us cheez ke liye jo ek container hai.** Buttons, Lists, Navigation Bars, Product Cards, Comment sections, poore-poore screens... *sab kuch* Auto Layout se banta hai. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh 'manual resizing' aur 'inconsistent spacing' ki problem ko solve karta hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka workflow 10 guna slow ho jayega. Aapka design 'static' (fixed) hoga, 'dynamic' (badalne wala) nahi. Agar text badla, toh aapka poora design toot jayega. Aapko har chote change ke liye poora layout haath se adjust karna padega. Aapko "Job-Ready" nahi maana jayega agar aapko Auto Layout nahi aata.
6.  **ğŸ§‘_ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown (Right Panel):**_
    * **Shortcut:** Element(s) select karke `Shift + A`.
    * **Direction (Flow):** Elements vertical (neeche ki taraf) align honge ya horizontal (side mein).
    * **Spacing between items:** Elements ke *beech* ki jagah (e.g., 8px).
    * **Padding (around items):** Frame ke *andar*, content ke chaaron taraf ki jagah (e.g., 16px padding).
    * **Alignment (Box):** Content ko Frame ke andar kahan rakhein (e.g., Top-Left, Center, Bottom-Right).
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek 'Dynamic Button' banana (jo text ke saath grow kare).
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  `T` daba kar "Sign Up" likhein.
        2.  *Sirf text ko* select rakhein aur keyboard par `Shift + A` dabayein.
        3.  **ğŸš€ Quick run (Output):** Text ke chaaron taraf ek 'Frame' ban jayega. Yeh ek Auto Layout Frame hai.
        4.  Right Panel (Auto Layout section) mein jaayein:
        5.  `Horizontal padding` ko `24` set karein.
        6.  `Vertical padding` ko `16` set karein.
        7.  Is Frame (Frame 1) ko select karein aur Right Panel (Fill section) mein `+` daba kar ek color (e.g., Blue) add karein.
        8.  **Test:** Text par double-click karein aur "Sign Up" ko badal kar "Sign Up for Free" likhein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run (Final Output):** Jaise hi aapne type kiya, Blue button (background Frame) apne aap bada ho gaya, text ke size ke hisaab se, aur padding (16px top/bottom, 24px left/right) maintain rahi! Aapne ab ek 'responsive' button bana liya hai.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * **Auto Layout ka istemaal hi na karna** (darr ke maare). Yeh sabse badi galti hai.
    * Ek Rectangle `(R)` aur Text `(T)` ko select karke `Shift+A` dabana. (Aap kar sakte hain, par behtar tareeka text se shuru karna hai, jaisa example mein hai).
    * 'Padding' (andar ki space) aur 'Spacing between items' (beech ki space) mein confuse hona.
    * Sochna ki Auto Layout lagane ke baad aap cheezon ko haath se (manually) drag karke move kar sakte hain. (Nahi! Ab spacing aur alignment sirf Right Panel se control honge. Yahi iska fayda hai).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main toh bas ek choti website bana raha hoon, mujhe 'Auto Layout' ki kya zaroorat hai? Main Group (Ctrl+G) karke haath se align kar lunga."
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Manual alignment mein 1 ghanta lagega, Auto Layout mein 5 minute. Student ek 'List Item' (Icon + Text) ko Auto Layout (horizontal) se banata hai. Phir 3 list items ko select karke unhe ek naye Auto Layout (vertical) Frame mein daal deta hai. Ab poori list responsive hai. Agar ek item ka text 2 line ka ho gaya, baaki items apne aap neeche shift ho jayenge.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** **Professionals 'Group' (Ctrl+G) ka istemaal *nahi* karte. Woh har cheez ke liye Auto Layout (Shift+A) ka istemaal karte hain.** Poori screen (Header, Body, Footer) ek bada 'Vertical Auto Layout' Frame hota hai. Header khud ek 'Horizontal Auto Layout' Frame hota hai. Yeh "Nesting" (Auto Layout ke andar Auto Layout) kehlata hai.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek "Comment Section". Har comment (Profile Pic + Name + Text) ek Auto Layout Frame hai. Poori comment list ek bada 'Vertical Auto Layout' Frame hai. Jab aap naya comment add karte hain, list apne aap grow karti hai aur sabke beech 24px ki 'spacing' maintain rehti hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * `Shift + A` ko apna best friend bana lein.
    * Groups (`Ctrl+G`) ki jagah Auto Layout (`Shift+A`) use karein.
    * Chota shuru karein (Button). Phir Auto Layout Frames ko 'nest' (ek ke andar ek) karna seekhein (Card). Phir poori screen banayein.
    * Padding (andar) aur Spacing (beech) ka fark samjhein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Auto Layout Frame mein elements ko re-order (upar-neeche) kaise karein?** Layers Panel mein drag-drop karein, ya element select karke keyboard par 'Up/Down arrow keys' use karein.
    * **Auto Layout lagane ke baad ek element ko 'beech' mein kaise rakhein?** Auto Layout Frame ko select karein aur Right Panel mein 'Alignment' box se 'Center' chunein.
    * **Auto Layout vs Group?** Group = Ek dumb folder (sirf saath move karne ke liye). Auto Layout = Ek smart container (jo spacing, padding, aur responsiveness handle karta hai). **Hamesha Auto Layout jeetega.**
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. "Button" waali exercise (Task) ko dobara karein.
    * 2. Ek 'Icon' (Circle `O`) aur 'Text' (`T`) banayein. Dono ko select karke `Shift+A` dabayein. Unke beech ki 'Spacing between items' ko `8px` set karein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Figma's Auto Layout Playground:** Figma community par ek interactive file hai jo aapko Auto Layout seekhne mein help karti hai.

---

### 4.5: Advanced Auto Layout (Spacing & Resizing)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Advanced Auto Layout âš™ï¸ (Elements ko stretch aur grow karana).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh Auto Layout ki 'Resizing' properties hain. Yeh define karti hain ki jab Parent Frame (container) bada ya chota hota hai, toh uske *andar* ke elements (children) kaise behave (react) karenge.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yahi asli 'Responsive Design' hai. Isse aap define karte hain ki 'Navbar' (parent) ko 300px (Mobile) se 1440px (Desktop) stretch karne par, 'Logo' left mein rahega, 'Links' beech mein aa jayenge, aur 'Button' right mein chala jayega.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Jab aapne ek Auto Layout Frame (jaise Navbar ya Card) bana liya ho, aur ab aap use responsive banana chahte hain. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh us problem ko solve karta hai jahan aap mobile design ko bada karke desktop banate hain aur saare elements left mein hi chipke reh jaate hain.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka Auto Layout Frame "responsive" nahi hoga. Woh bas content ke hisaab se grow (bada) hoga, lekin parent ke hisaab se stretch nahi hoga. Aapka design har screen size ke liye 'toota hua' (broken) lagega.
6.  **ğŸ§‘_ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown (Right Panel 'Resizing'):**_
    * Yeh properties aapko *child element* (jo Auto Layout ke andar hai) par milti hain.
    * **Horizontal Resizing (Width):**
        * `Hug Contents (Default):` Element ki width uske andar ke content (e.g., text) jitni hogi. (Button ke liye best).
        * `Fill Container:` Element *stretch* hokar parent container ki poori available width le lega. (Responsive design ke liye sabse zaroori).
        * `Fixed Width:` Element ki width fixed rahegi (e.g., 100px), chahe kuch bhi ho.
    * **Vertical Resizing (Height):** Same options (Hug, Fill, Fixed).
    * **Spacing Mode (Parent par):**
        * `Packed (Default):` Saare elements ek saath (e.g., left mein) rehte hain.
        * `Space between (Auto):` Yeh 'magic' property hai. Yeh pehle element ko left, aakhiri ko right, aur baaki sabke beech mein space barabar distribute kar deti hai. (Navbar ke liye perfect).
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek 'Responsive Navbar' banana (Logo left, Button right).
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Ek 'Text' (Logo) aur ek 'Button' (jo aapne 4.4 mein banaya) banayein.
        2.  Dono ko select karke `Shift+A` (Auto Layout) dabayein. Direction `Horizontal` set karein. Is Frame ko "Navbar" naam dein.
        3.  "Navbar" Frame ko select karein aur Right Panel (Frame section) mein Width ko `1440px` (Fixed Width) kar dein (taaki yeh poori screen jitna ho). Use 'Fill' (color) dein taaki dikhe.
