        * **Style Guide:** Sirf 'visuals' (Colors, Fonts). (DS ka chota hissa).
        * **UI Kit:** Styles + Components (Figma file). (DS ka Figma hissa).
        * **Design System:** UI Kit + Documentation + Guidelines + Code. (Poora package).
    * **Yeh developers ke liye kaise kaam karta hai?** Designer 'Button' component (Figma) use karta hai. Developer 'Button' component (React code) use karta hai. Dono ka naam (`Button/Primary`) aur properties (`State=Hover`) *same* hote hain. Isse 'Design-to-Dev' handoff super-smooth ho jaata hai.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. (Mental Exercise) Apne Module 5 (Styles) aur Module 6 (Components) ke banaye hue assets ko dekhein. Yeh aapke personal 'UI Kit' ki shuruaat hai.
    * 2. Google "Material Design" aur unki 'Button' component ki documentation website dekhein (unke Do's and Don'ts padhein).
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Material Design (Google):** Sabse famous DS.
    * **Atlassian Design System:** B2B (business) products ke liye best example.
    * **Zeroheight, Storybook:** DS ki documentation (website) banane ke popular tools.

---

### 7.2: Figma Variables (for Theming)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Figma Variables ğŸ¨ğŸ”„ (Styles ka naya, super-powerful version).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Variables 'design tokens' (raw values) ko store karne ka ek naya tareeka hai. Yeh 'Styles' (Module 5) se zyada advanced hain. Style (e.g., `Brand-Primary` color) ek 'semantic' (matlab wala) naam tha. Variable ek 'raw' (kacchi) value (jaise color ka hex code `#0D99FF` ya spacing ka number `16`) ko ek naam (e.g., `color-blue-500` ya `spacing-4`) ke peeche save karta hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Inki sabse badi power hai **'Modes' (avasthaayein)**. Variables se aap *ek hi* design ko alag-alag 'Modes' (jaise `Light Mode` / `Dark Mode`) mein automatically switch kar sakte hain. Aap spacing ke liye bhi variables (`space-16px`) bana sakte hain.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Jab bhi aapko 'Theming' (jaise Light/Dark Mode, ya alag-alag brands ke liye alag color themes) implement karna ho. Jab aap ek bohot advanced Design System (jo seedha code se link ho) bana rahe hon. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh 'Light Mode' aur 'Dark Mode' ke liye **do alag-alag design file** (ya 2 alag Style sets) maintain karne ki problem ko solve karta hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Agar aapko 'Dark Mode' banana hai, toh aapko *saare* Color Styles (Module 5) ko 'duplicate' karna padega (e.g., `Text/Primary-Light`, `Text/Primary-Dark`). Yeh bohot manual kaam hai aur inconsistent ho sakta hai. Variables ke bina 'Modes' achieve karna bohot mushkil hai.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
    * **Variables Panel:** Canvas par (kuch bhi select na karke) Right Panel mein "Local Variables" par click karke khola jaata hai.
    * **Collection (Group):** Variables ka group (e.g., "Colors", "Spacing").
    * **Variable (Token):** Asli value (e.g., `colors/brand/blue-500` = `#0D99FF`).
    * **Modes (The Superpower):** Ek hi 'Collection' (e.g., "Theme") ke alag-alag columns (e.g., `Light Mode`, `Dark Mode`).
    * **Semantic Token:** Aap ek variable (e.g., `color/background`) ko doosre variable (e.g., `color/white`) se link kar sakte hain.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek 'Frame' ko 'Light Mode' se 'Dark Mode' mein switch karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Canvas par deselect karein. Right Panel mein 'Local Variables' par click karein.
        2.  `Create Variable` -> `Color` chunein. Naam dein `color/background`. Value (Mode 1) ko `#FFFFFF` (White) rakhein.
        3.  Ek aur variable banayein: `color/text`. Value (Mode 1) ko `#000000` (Black) rakhein.
        4.  Ab 'Collection 1' (default naam) ke naam par click karein. Column header (jahan 'Mode 1' likha hai) ke paas `+` icon dabayein. Ek naya 'Mode 2' ban jayega.
        5.  'Mode 1' ka naam badal kar `Light` rakhein. 'Mode 2' ka naam `Dark` rakhein.
        6.  Ab 'Dark' column mein jaayein: `color/background` ki value ko `#000000` (Black) karein. `color/text` ki value ko `#FFFFFF` (White) karein. Panel band karein.
        7.  `F` daba kar ek Frame banayein.
        8.  Frame ko select karke, Right Panel mein 'Fill' ke 4-dot âˆ· icon par click karein aur apne `color/background` variable ko chunein.
        9.  Frame ke andar `T` daba kar text likhein. Text ka 'Fill' âˆ· `color/text` variable se link karein.
        10. **Magic Step:** Frame ko select rakhein. Right Panel mein 'Layer' section (jahan Opacity hai) ke paas 'Variables' (mode icon) par click karein. 'Change Variable Mode' -> 'Dark' chunein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapka Frame (aur uske andar ka text) *automatically* Light Mode se Dark Mode mein switch ho jayega (Background black, text white).
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * 'Variables' (raw tokens) aur 'Styles' (semantic use) mein confuse hona. (Rule: Naye workflow mein, Variables (e.g., `blue-500`) ko 'Styles' (e.g., `Brand-Primary`) se link kiya jaata hai).
    * 'Number' variables (spacing ke liye) aur 'Color' variables ko ek hi Collection mein daal dena. (Alag-alag 'Collections' banayein: "Colors", "Spacing", "Radius").
    * 'Modes' ka feature hi na dhoondh paana.
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main 'Styles' (Module 5) seekh chuka hoon. Kya mujhe 'Variables' bhi seekhne ki zaroorat hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Agar aapko 'Theming' (Light/Dark Mode) *nahi* banana hai, toh aap abhi 'Styles' ke saath kaam chala sakte hain. Par agar aapko Theming chahiye, toh 'Variables' zaroori hain.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Poore Design Systems ab 'Variables' par shift ho rahe hain. Inhe 'Design Tokens' bhi kehte hain. Yeh developers ke saath link karna aasan hota hai. 'Spacing' (padding, margin) ke liye 'Number' variables (`space-4` = 16px) banana ab standard practice hai.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek 'Frame' (poori screen) ka 'Mode' `Light` se `Dark` karne par, uske andar ke *saare* components (Buttons, Cards, Text) jo variables se jude hain, automatically dark mode mein switch ho jaate hain.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Variables = Raw Tokens (e.g., `blue-500`, `space-8`).
    * Modes = Theming (Light/Dark).
    * Aap 'Styles' (Module 5) ko 'Variables' se link kar sakte hain. (Best of both worlds).
    * Spacing (Number), Radius (Number), aur Colors (Color) ke liye alag-alag 'Collections' banayein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Kya Variables free plan mein hain?** Free plan mein 'Local Variables' (limited) available hain, par 'Modes' (Light/Dark) ki limitation ho sakti hai (e.g., 1 mode).
    * **Spacing (Number) variables ka kya fayda?** Aap ek 'Collection' (e.g., "Spacing") banate hain. Uske 2 modes banate hain: `Default` aur `Compact`. `Default` mein `space-medium` = `16px` ho sakta hai. `Compact` mein `space-medium` = `8px` ho sakta hai. Ab aap poora layout 1-click mein 'Compact' bana sakte hain.
    * **String variables?** Yeh text content (e.g., "Submit" button ka text) ko variable banane ke liye hai (e.g., alag-alag 'Languages' ke modes ke liye).
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. 'Light/Dark Mode' waali exercise (Task) ko poora try karein.
    * 2. Ek 'Number' variable banayein (`spacing/medium` = `16px`) aur use ek Auto Layout component (Button) ki 'Padding' se link karein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Design Tokens:** Yeh 'Variables' ke peeche ka main concept hai. Iske baare mein zaroor padhein.
    * **Figma Variables Documentation:** (Figma ke official guides).

---

### 7.3: Advanced Team Libraries (Publishing & Consuming)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Advanced Team Libraries (Publishing & Consuming) ğŸ“š (Apne DS ko team se share karna).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh Figma ka **paid feature** hai jo aapko apni *ek* file (jismein saare Master Components â– aur Styles âˆ· hain) ko 'Publish' (prakaashit) karne deta hai. Ek baar publish hone ke baad, aapki team ke *baaki sab log* us 'Library' ko apni-apni files mein 'Consume' (use) kar sakte hain.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yahi hai 'Single Source of Truth' (SSOT) in action. Poori team (100 log) *ek hi* central 'Master Button' component ko use karti hai. Jab 'Design System file' mein woh button update hota hai, toh baaki 100 logon ko apni files mein 'update' ka notification milta hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** **Hamesha, jab aap ek team (2 ya 2+ log) mein kaam kar rahe hon.** Ek file 'Design System Library' ban jaati hai. Baaki saari files (e.g., "iOS App", "Website") us library ko 'consume' (use) karti hain. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh components ko copy-paste karne ki problem ko solve karta hai. Yeh ensure karta hai ki poori team hamesha 'latest' (sabse naye) design components par kaam kar rahi hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** **Chaos (Arajakta).** Agar aapne component file (DS) se 'Button' copy karke apni 'Product' file mein paste kiya, toh unka 'link' (connection) *toot* jaata hai (ya local rehta hai). Jab 'DS' file mein 'Master Button' update hoga, aapki 'Product' file mein button update *nahi* hoga. Aapki poori team 'out of sync' (sync se baahar) ho jayegi.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
    * **File 1: Design System (DS) File:**
        * Is file ko 'Drafts' se nikaal kar ek 'Project' mein move karna zaroori hai (paid feature).
        * `Assets` panel -> 'Library' (kitaab ğŸ“š) icon -> `Publish` button.
    * **File 2: Product File (e.g., iOS App):**
        * Is file mein, `Assets` panel -> 'Library' (kitaab ğŸ“š) icon.
        * Aapko list mein aapki 'Design System' file dikhegi. Uska 'switch' (toggle) `On` karein.
    * **The Workflow (Updating):**
        1.  Designer A 'DS' file mein jaakar 'Button' ka color 'Red' karta hai aur `Publish` karta hai.
        2.  Designer B (jo 'Product' file mein kaam kar raha hai) ko screen ke bottom-right mein ek notification aata hai: "Updates available".
        3.  Designer B 'Review' karke 'Accept' (sveekaar) karta hai.
        4.  Uski file ke saare 'Button' instances automatically 'Red' ho jaate hain.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Apni component file (UI Kit) ko publish karna (Yeh paid plan feature hai).
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Apni file (jismein `ğŸ§© Components` page hai) ko 'Drafts' se nikaal kar ek 'Shared Project' mein move karein.
        2.  File ke andar, 'Assets' panel par jaayein.
        3.  Top par 'Library' (kitaab ğŸ“š) icon par click karein.
        4.  Ek modal (popup) khulega. Bada sa `Publish` button dabayein. (Aap likh sakte hain ki aapne kya change kiya, e.g., "Updated button colors").
        5.  **Ab, ek dum *nayi* (New) Figma file kholein** (Yeh aapki 'Product' file hogi).
        6.  Is nayi file mein, 'Assets' panel -> 'Library' (kitaab ğŸ“š) icon par jaayein.
        7.  Aapko list mein aapki 'Design System' file ka naam dikhega. Uska 'switch' `On` karein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Ab is *nayi* file ke 'Assets' panel mein, aapko apni *puraani* file ke saare components (Button, Card) dikhne lagenge. Aap unhe yahan drag-and-drop karke use kar sakte hain.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Yeh sochna ki yeh 'Free' plan mein hai. (Library 'publishing' paid plan feature hai. 'Consuming' (use karna) free hai, jaise community files se).
    * File ko 'Drafts' (aapka personal folder) mein rakhe-rakhe 'Publish' karne ki koshish karna. (File hamesha 'Team Project' mein honi chahiye).
    * Updates ko 'Accept' na karna aur puraane components par kaam karte rehna.
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main akela freelancer hoon. Kya mujhe yeh paid feature chahiye?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** **Nahi.** Agar aap akele kaam kar rahe hain, toh aapke 'Local Components' (jo usi file mein 'Assets' panel mein dikhte hain) aapke liye kaafi hain. Aapko 'Publish' karne ki zaroorat nahi hai.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** **Yeh feature ek Professional Team ke liye *sab kuch* hai.** Iske bina team mein kaam karna (scalability) impossible hai. Ek 'DS Team' (5 log) 'DS Library' file ko manage aur publish karti hai. 100 'Product Designers' (jo alag-alag features par kaam kar rahe hain) us library ko 'consume' (use) karte hain.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** 'Airbnb' ki 'DS Team' ne 'Date Picker' component mein ek bug fix kiya. Unhone change ko `Publish` kiya. Agle din, poori duniya mein Airbnb ke 50 designers (jo alag-alag files mein kaam kar rahe the) ko 'Update' notification mila, aur sabka 'Date Picker' 1-click mein fix ho gaya.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * **DS File:** 'Team Project' mein rakhein (Paid plan).
    * **Publish:** 'Assets' -> 'Library' -> `Publish`.
    * **Product File:** 'Assets' -> 'Library' -> 'Switch On' (consume).
    * Hamesha 'Updates' ko review aur accept karein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Kya main library se component ko edit kar sakta hoon?** Nahi. Aap 'Instance' (â™¢) ko 'override' (text badalna) kar sakte hain, par 'Master' (â–) ko edit karne ke liye aapko 'DS file' mein hi jaana padega (Instance par right-click -> 'Go to Main Component').
    * **Agar main 'Update' accept na karun toh?** Aap puraane (outdated) component par kaam karte rahenge, jo bura hai.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. (Agar paid plan hai) 'Task' waali exercise ko poora karein.
    * 2. (Agar free plan hai) 'Community' (Topic 7.4) se koi 'UI Kit' (jaise "Material Design 3 Kit") ko 'enable' (switch on) karein aur uske components ko 'Assets' panel mein dekhein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * Figma Libraries (Official Documentation).

---

### 7.4: Figma Community (Templates & Icons)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Figma Community ğŸ¤ (Free design files, plugins, aur icons ka khazaana).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Figma Community ek 'public platform' (saarvajanik manch) hai (Figma ke andar hi) jahan poori duniya ke designers aur companies (jaise Google, Microsoft) apne banaye hue resourcesâ€”**Files (UI Kits, Templates)**, **Plugins (Tools)**, aur **Widgets (FigJam ke liye)**â€”doosron ke use ke liye (aksar free mein) share karte hain.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** **Aapko har cheez zero se shuru karne ki zaroorat nahi hai.** Aapko ek achha 'Icon Set' chahiye? Community se 'Duplicate' kar lo. Aapko dummy images (nakli photos) chahiye? 'Unsplash' (Plugin) install kar lo. Yeh aapka workflow 100 guna tez (fast) kar deta hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** **Roz!** Jab aapko koi 'Plugin' (extra tool) install karna ho. Jab aapko 'inspiration' (prerna) ke liye dekhna ho ki doosre log professional files kaise banate hain. Jab aapko 'assets' (jaise icons, illustrations) ki zaroorat ho. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh 'resource dhoondhne' aur 'manual kaam' (jaise 100 photos import karna) ki problem ko solve karta hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aap bohot *dheeme* (slow) designer honge. Aap icon dhoondhne ke liye Google par jayenge, `.svg` download karenge, use Figma mein drag-and-drop (import) karenge. Jabki Community user, 'Iconify' (plugin) se 5 second mein Figma ke andar hi icon search karke daal dega.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
    * **Location:** Figma 'Home' (Dashboard) screen par, left-side mein 'Community' ğŸ¤ tab hota hai.
    * **Files (Templates, UI Kits):** Inhe aap 'Duplicate' (copy) karte hain. Yeh aapke 'Drafts' folder mein ek nayi, editable file ban jaati hai.
    * **Plugins (Tools):** Inhe aap 'Install' (ya 'Try it out') karte hain. Yeh aapke Figma editor ke andar (Right-click -> Plugins) menu mein 'tools' ki tarah add ho jaate hain.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task 1:** Ek 'Icon Set' (Feather Icons) ko copy karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Figma Home (Dashboard) par jaayein -> Left mein 'Community' ğŸ¤ par click karein.
        2.  Upar 'Search bar' mein "Feather Icons" type karein.
        3.  Search results mein 'Files' tab par click karein.
        4.  'Feather Icons' file (jo official dikhe) par click karein.
        5.  Top-right corner mein `Duplicate` button dabayein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run (Output 1):** Yeh file *aapke* 'Drafts' folder mein copy ho jayegi. Ab aap is file se icons ko copy karke apne design mein paste kar sakte hain. (Best tareeka: Inhe component banakar apni library mein daalna).
    * **Task 2:** Ek 'Plugin' (Unsplash) install karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  'Community' mein waapas jaayein. "Unsplash" search karein.
        2.  'Plugins' tab par click karein.
        3.  'Unsplash' (jo official dikhe) par click karein.
        4.  Top-right mein `Install` (ya `Try it out`) button dabayein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run (Output 2):** Plugin install ho gaya. Ab apni *design file* mein jaayein -> Canvas par Right-click -> Plugins -> 'Unsplash'. Plugin khul jayega.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Community se *poora design* (e.g., ek poori app) 'Duplicate' karke use apne 'Portfolio' mein "apna kaam" (my work) bolkar dikhana. (Yeh 'plagiarism' (chori) hai! Community ko *seekhne* (learning), *inspiration* (prerna), aur *assets* (icons/plugins) ke liye use karein, copy karne ke liye nahi).
    * Bahut saare (100+) plugins install kar lena, jisse Figma slow ho sakta hai. (Sirf zaroori waale rakhein).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Kya professional designers bhi Community ka istemaal karte hain?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** **Roz!** Student 'Community' se 'Mobile App Templates' duplicate karke unhe 'reverse-engineer' (tod-fod karke seekhna) karte hain ki Auto Layout aur Variants kaise bane hain.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** **Roz!** Professional teams 'Plugins' par bohot zyada depend karti hain.
        * `Unsplash` / `Content Reel` (Dummy data ke liye).
        * `Stark` / `Contrast` (Accessibility [9.2] check karne ke liye).
        * `Autoflow` (User flow diagrams [2.2] banane ke liye).
        * `Iconify` / `Feather Icons` (Icons laane ke liye).
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek designer ko 20 'Product Cards' mein dummy data (photo, title, price) daalna hai. Woh `Content Reel` (Plugin) install karta hai, 20 cards select karta hai, aur 1-click mein sab mein alag-alag dummy data bhar deta hai. (Kaam 10 minute ki jagah 10 second mein ho gaya).
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * **Files (Templates):** 'Duplicate' karein (seekhne aur inspiration ke liye).
    * **Plugins (Tools):** 'Install' karein (workflow tez karne ke liye).
    * Hamesha credible (bharosemand) publishers (jaise 'Figma', 'Google', 'Microsoft') ke resources ko pehle dekhein.
    * Apna "Must-Have" plugin set banayein (Unsplash, Iconify, Content Reel).
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Kya yeh sab free hai?** 95% resources (files, plugins) free hain. Kuch bohot advanced plugins ya UI Kits 'paid' (premium) ho sakte hain.
    * **Kya main bhi Community par publish kar sakta hoon?** Haan! Aap apni banayi hui file (e.g., ek Icon Set) ya Plugin ko Community par 'Publish' (share) kar sakte hain.
    * **Mera plugin kahan milenga?** Install karne ke baad, apni design file mein, Canvas par Right-Click -> 'Plugins' -> [Aapka Plugin].
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. 'Unsplash' plugin install karein (Task 2). Ek Rectangle banayein, use select karein, plugin run karein aur usmein ek "Nature" ki photo daalein.
    * 2. 'Iconify' (ya 'Feather Icons') plugin install karein aur apne design mein ek 'Home' icon add karein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Content Reel:** Dummy text, images, avatars ke liye.
    * **Iconify:** Hazaron icons (Material, Feather, etc.) ka ek hi plugin.
    * **Stark:** Accessibility (color contrast) check karne ke liye.

---

Yeh tha hamara Module 7! ğŸ‰ Aapne 'Design System' ki theory, 'Variables' (Light/Dark mode), 'Team Libraries' (Publishing), aur 'Community' (Plugins) ke baare mein seekh liya hai.

Aapka professional workflow ab lagbhag poora ho gaya hai.

Jab aap ready hon, bas **"Module 8 shuru karo"** likh dena, aur hum design ko 'clickable' (interactive) banana seekhengeâ€”yaani **Prototyping**!

=============================================================

Chalo bhai, shuru karte hain aapke Figma (Beginner-to-Job-Ready) notes ka Module 8!

Yeh module bohot mazedaar hai. Humne design 'banana' (banana) seekh liya, ab hum use 'zinda' (live) karna seekhenge. Hum apne designs ko **clickable (interactive)** banayenge taaki woh ek asli app ya website jaisa feel dein. Yahi 'Prototyping' hai.

---

### 8.1: Prototyping Basics (Connecting Frames)

**(Yeh ek CORE Foundational topic hai. Poora dhyaan dein.)**

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Prototyping Basics ğŸ”— (Screens ko aapas mein jodna).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Prototyping ek "clickable" (interactive) mock-up banana hai. Ismein aap 'hotspots' (clickable areas) banate hain (jaise ek 'Login' button) aur unhe doosri 'Frames' (screens) se jodte hain (jaise 'Home Page').
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Kyunki client ya user 'static' (ruki hui) image dekh kar poora 'flow' (raasta) nahi samajh paate. Ek clickable prototype unhe *experience* karne deta hai ki "Login button dabane se kya hoga." Yeh design ko 'test' (jaanch) karne aur developers ko 'user flow' samjhane ke liye sabse zaroori hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Jab aapke paas kam se kam 2 screens (Frames) design ho chuki hon. **Hamesha,** design ko present (dikhaane) karne se pehle. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh us problem ko solve karta hai jahan aap client ko 20 alag-alag JPEG/PNG files bhejte hain aur fir call par samjhate hain, "Sir, is button ko dabane se woh waali screen khulegi." Prototype mein woh *khud* daba kar dekh sakte hain.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka design 'be-jaan' (lifeless) lagega. Aap user ka 'experience' (anubhav) nahi, balkin sirf 'visuals' (dikhavat) dikha payenge. User feedback (jaise "Yeh button kahan le jaata hai?") clear nahi hoga. Developers ko 'flow' (raasta) samjhane mein bohot mushkil hogi. Aap usability testing (jaanch) nahi kar payenge.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
    * **Prototype Tab:** Saara prototyping ka kaam **Right Panel** ke `Prototype` tab (Module 1.5) mein hota hai.
    * **Hotspot (Noodle):** Jab aap 'Prototype' tab mein hote hain, kisi bhi element (jaise Button) ko select karne par uske side mein ek 'plus' `+` (circle) dikhta hai. Isse 'noodle' (taar) kehte hain.
    * **Connecting:** Aap is `+` (noodle) ko kheench (drag) kar doosre 'Frame' (screen) par 'drop' (chhod) dete hain. Ek 'connection' (link) ban jaata hai.
    * **Starting Point:** Aapko batana padta hai ki prototype *shuru* kahan se hoga. Ise 'Flow starting point' kehte hain.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek 'Login' screen ko 'Home' screen se jodna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Aapke paas 2 Frames hone chahiye: "Frame 1: Login Screen" aur "Frame 2: Home Screen".
        2.  "Login Screen" Frame ke andar ek 'Login Button' (component/frame) hona chahiye.
        3.  Sabse pehle, **Right Panel** mein `Design` tab se `Prototype` tab par switch karein.
        4.  Apne "Login Button" ko select karein.
        5.  Aapko button ke right side par ek blue `+` circle dikhega.
        6.  Us `+` ko click karein aur mouse ko (drag) kheench kar "Frame 2: Home Screen" par le jaakar chhod dein.
        7.  **ğŸš€ Quick run (Output 1):** Ek 'Interaction details' (popup) khulega.
        8.  **âœï¸ Options:**
            * `Trigger:` `On click` (Jab user click kare). (Default yahi rakhein).
            * `Action:` `Maps to` (Le jaao).
            * `Destination:` `Home Screen` (Figma ne automatically select kar liya).
        9.  Popup ko band kar dein.
        10. Ab, "Frame 1: Login Screen" ko select karein. `Prototype` tab mein (Right Panel), 'Flow starting point' ke paas `+` icon par click karein. (Isse Figma ko pata chalta hai ki app yahan se shuru hogi).
        11. **Test:** Toolbar (top-right) mein `Present` (Play â–¶) icon par click karein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run (Final Output):** Ek nayi 'Presentation' tab khulegi. Aapko 'Login Screen' dikhegi. Jab aap 'Login Button' par click karenge, toh screen 'Home Screen' par change ho jayegi. Aapne apna pehla prototype bana liya!
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * **`Design` tab mein rehkar `+` (noodle) dhoondhna.** (Yaad rakhein: Prototyping ke saare options `Prototype` tab mein hain).
    * Poore 'Frame' (screen) ko 'Frame' se link kar dena. (Aisa na karein). Hamesha *ek specific element* (jaise 'Button') ko 'Frame' se link karein.
    * 'Flow starting point' ğŸ“ set karna bhool jaana. (Iske bina, 'Play' (â–¶) button kaam nahi karega).
    * Link ko 'Frame' (screen) ki jagah 'Rectangle' (shape) se jod dena. (Hamesha poore 'Frame' se jodein).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main 'User Flow' (Module 2.2) FigJam mein bana chuka hoon. Phir iski kya zaroorat hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** 'User Flow' (FigJam) sirf 'planning' (yojana) thi. 'Prototype' (Figma) us planning ka 'asli' (actual), clickable, high-fidelity (sundar) version hai. Student apne Lo-Fi wireframes (Module 2.3) ko hi pehle prototype (link) karke 'flow' (raasta) test kar leta hai, taaki Hi-Fi (sundar) design banane se pehle hi galtiyan pakdi jaayein.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Designers pehle 'happy path' (main flow, e.g., Login -> Home -> Product -> Buy) prototype karte hain. Phir woh is prototype ka 'link' (share button se) Product Managers aur Engineers ko bhejte hain (feedback ke liye). Phir is prototype ko 'Usability Testing' (Module 10.6) ke liye real users ko diya jaata hai.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek company 'Sign Up' process ko aasan banana chahti hai. Designer 3 alag-alag 'flows' (versions) ko prototype karta hai. Phir A/B testing (ya user testing) se dekha jaata hai ki kaun sa prototype (flow) user sabse jaldi poora kar paata hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * `Prototype` tab mein switch karein.
    * Hamesha 'element' (Button) ko 'Frame' (Screen) se jodein.
    * `Flow starting point` ğŸ“ set karna na bhoolein.
    * Apne links ko organize rakhein. Gande (messy) noodles aapki file ko slow kar sakte hain.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Main 'Back' button kaise banaun?** Aasaan! 'Home Screen' ke 'Back' button (element) ko select karein -> `+` noodle ko kheench kar 'Login Screen' (Frame) se jodein. Action `Maps to` hoga. Ya phir, Action mein `Back` (Previous screen) chunein.
    * **Mera 'Play' (Present) button grey (disabled) kyun hai?** Kyunki aapne 'Flow starting point' ğŸ“ set nahi kiya hai. Ek Frame select karke 'Flow starting point' add karein.
    * **Main ek link (noodle) ko delete kaise karun?** Bas us 'noodle' (taar) par click karein aur 'Delete' (keyboard) dabayein.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. 'Login' -> 'Home' waali exercise (Task) ko poora karein.
    * 2. 'Home' screen par ek 'Profile' icon banayein aur use ek nayi 'Profile' (Frame) screen se link karein. Phir 'Profile' screen se 'Back' button ko waapas 'Home' screen se link karein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Smart Animate (Topic 8.2):** Prototyping ki agli superpower.

---

### 8.2: Triggers & Animations (Smart Animate)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Triggers & Animations ğŸª„ (Clickable se 'Smooth' banana).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):**
    * **Triggers (Kab shuru ho):** Yeh batata hai ki 'action' (link) *kab* shuru hoga. (e.g., `On click`, `On hover`, `After delay`).
    * **Animations (Kaise dikhe):** Yeh batata hai ki ek screen se doosri screen par jaate waqt 'transition' (badlaav) kaisa dikhega. (e.g., `Instant`, `Dissolve` (fade hona), `Move In` (slide hona)).
    * **Smart Animate (Jaadu):** Yeh Figma ka sabse powerful animation hai. Agar 2 Frames mein *ek hi layer* (same naam waala) hai, par uski 'position' (jagah) ya 'style' (color/size) alag hai, toh 'Smart Animate' uske beech ke steps ko *khud* (automatically) calculate karke ek 'smooth' (makhan jaisa) animation bana deta hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yeh aapke prototype ko 'static' (ruka hua) se 'dynamic' (zinda) bana deta hai. Ek 'Instant' (turant) badlaav ajeeb lagta hai. Ek 'Slide-in' (slide hokar aana) ya 'Smart Animate' (smoothly badalna) user ko 'context' (sandarbh) deta hai ki woh app mein kahan jaa rahe hain. Yeh aapke design ko 'polished' (professional) feel deta hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Har prototype connection (link) mein.
    * **Triggers:** `On click` (90% time), `On hover` (Desktop dropdown menu/tooltips), `After delay` (Splash screen se Home screen par automatically jaana).
    * **Smart Animate:** **Jab bhi** do screens ke beech 'common' (ek jaise naam waale) elements hon. (e.g., Ek 'Profile Pic' par click karke 'Profile Screen' par jaana, jahan wahi 'Profile Pic' badi ho jaati hai).
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka prototype 'click' toh hoga, par 'real' (asli) app jaisa *feel* nahi hoga. Har cheez 'Instant' (jhatke se) badlegi, jo user ke liye ajeeb (jarring) ho sakta hai. Aap advanced micro-interactions (chote animations) nahi bana payenge.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
    * Jab aap (8.1 ki tarah) ek link banate hain, toh 'Interaction details' popup khulta hai.
    * **Trigger:**
        * `On click:` User ke click karne par.
        * `On drag:` User ke element ko drag (kheenchne) par.
        * `While hovering:` Jab tak mouse uspar hai (e.g., 'Hover' state dikhana).
        * `After delay:` Kuch milliseconds (e.g., 800ms) ke baad *apne aap* chalna.
    * **Animation:**
        * `Instant:` Turant (koi animation nahi).
        * `Dissolve:` Ek screen fade-out, doosri fade-in.
        * `Move In / Move Out / Push / Slide:` Screen alag-alag disha (direction) se slide hoti hai.
        * `Smart Animate:` (Sabse zaroori).
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek 'Toggle Switch' (On/Off) ko 'Smart Animate' karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Do Frames banayein: "Frame 1: Toggle Off" aur "Frame 2: Toggle On".
        2.  **Zaroori Layer Naming:**
            * "Toggle Off" Frame mein ek 'grey' Rectangle (background) banayein. Naam rakhein `Toggle BG`.
            * Uske andar ek 'white' Circle (handle) banayein. Naam rakhein `Toggle Handle`. Circle ko left mein rakhein.
            * "Toggle On" Frame mein, inhi dono layers ko copy-paste karein. `Toggle BG` ka color 'Green' kar dein. `Toggle Handle` ko 'right' side par move kar dein.
        3.  **Layers Panel Check:** Dono Frames mein `Toggle BG` aur `Toggle Handle` naam ki layers *honi* chahiye. Naam *bilkul same* hone chahiye!
        4.  `Prototype` tab mein jaayein.
        5.  "Toggle Off" Frame (poore frame) ko select karein aur `+` noodle ko "Toggle On" Frame se jodein.
        6.  **Interaction details:**
            * `Trigger:` `On click`.
            * `Animation:` `Smart Animate`. (Figma ne layers match kar li hain).
        7.  Ab "Toggle On" Frame ko select karke waapas "Toggle Off" Frame se jodein (Trigger: `On click`, Animation: `Smart Animate`).
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Prototype 'Play' (â–¶) karein. Jab aap (kahin bhi) click karenge, toh grey toggle 'smoothly' green mein badlega aur white circle 'smoothly' right side par slide hoga. Yeh 'Smart Animate' hai.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * **Smart Animate ke liye layer ka naam (naming) same na rakhna.** (e.g., ek frame mein "Rectangle 1", doosre mein "Rectangle 2"). Agar naam same nahi hoga, toh Smart Animate *kaam nahi karega* aur 'Dissolve' (fade) jaisa dikhega.
    * 'After delay' ko bohot kam (e.g., 1ms) ya bohot zyada (e.g., 5000ms) rakhna.
    * Har cheez par 'Smart Animate' lagane ki koshish karna. (Agar layers common nahi hain, toh 'Move In' ya 'Dissolve' behtar hai).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main 'Smart Animate' kab use karun aur 'Move In' kab?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:**
        * `Move In / Slide In:` Jab ek *poori nayi* screen aa rahi ho (e.g., Login se Home).
        * `Smart Animate:` Jab *usi* screen ke elements apni jagah/style badal rahe hon (e.g., Toggle switch, ek image par click karke use full-screen bada karna, ek list item ko expand (kholna)).
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** 'Smart Animate' ka use 'micro-interactions' (chote animations) ko dikhane ke liye hota hai, jisse developers ko pata chalta hai ki element ka 'transition' (badlaav) kaisa hona chahiye (e.g., Easing curve, duration).
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek 'Photo Gallery' (jismein 10 choti photos hain). Aap ek photo par click karte hain. Woh photo 'smoothly' (Smart Animate se) full-screen ho jaati hai. Yeh tabhi mumkin hai jab 'Gallery' Frame aur 'Full Screen' Frame, dono mein us image ka layer naam `image-01` (same) ho.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * **Smart Animate = Same Layer Names.** Yeh sabse bada rule hai.
    * Apne animations ko 'subtle' (halka) aur 'fast' (tez) rakhein (e.g., 300ms, 'Ease Out'). Bohat slow animation user ko frustrate karta hai.
    * `After delay` ka use 'Splash Screens' (Welcome screen jo 2 second baad hatt jaati hai) ke liye karein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Smart Animate kaam nahi kar raha!** 99% chance hai ki aapki dono frames mein layers ke 'naam' (naming) alag-alag hain. Layers Panel (Left) mein check karein.
    * **'Easing' (Ease In, Ease Out) kya hai?** Yeh animation ki 'speed curve' hai. `Ease Out` (default, shuru mein tez, aakhir mein slow) sabse natural (praakritik) lagta hai.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. 'Toggle Switch' (Task) waali exercise poori karein.
    * 2. Ek 'Splash Screen' (Frame 1) banayein. Use 'Home Screen' (Frame 2) se jodein. Trigger: `After delay`, Time: `1000ms`. Animation: `Dissolve`.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Interactive Components (Topic 8.4):** Smart Animate ko variants ke saath jodna.

---

### 8.3: Advanced Prototyping (Overlays, Modals, Sidebars)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Advanced Prototyping ğŸ–¼ï¸ (Screens ke upar screens dikhana).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh 'Prototype Action' (kriya) ka ek type hai. `Maps to` (jo humne 8.1 mein seekha) poori screen ko badal deta hai. `Open Overlay` (naya action) aapki *current screen* (maujooda screen) ke *upar* ek doosra 'Frame' (jaise Pop-up ya Sidebar) kholta hai, bina peeche waali screen ko hataye.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Kyunki modern apps mein har cheez poori screen nahi badalti. Aapko 'Modals' (pop-up box), 'Sidebars' (menu), 'Tooltips' (choti info), ya 'Keyboards' dikhane ki zaroorat padti hai, jo current screen ke *upar* aate hain.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):**
    * `Open Overlay:` Jab aapko ek 'Menu' button se 'Sidebar' (Side Menu) kholna ho. Jab aapko 'Warning' button se 'Confirm?' (Modal / Pop-up) dikhana ho. Jab aapko 'Info' icon se 'Tooltip' dikhana ho.
    * Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh 'context' (sandarbh) banaye rakhne ki problem ko solve karta hai. User ko pata rehta hai ki woh abhi bhi 'Home Screen' par hai, bas uske upar ek 'Menu' khula hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapko 'Sidebar' (menu) dikhane ke liye ek *poori nayi screen* ("Home Screen with Sidebar Open") design karni padegi. Yeh bohot inefficient (slow) hai. Agar aapke paas 10 screens hain, toh aapko 10 *aur* screens (sidebar ke saath) banani padengi. 'Overlay' ke saath, aapko *sirf 1* 'Sidebar' Frame banana padta hai, aur aap use kisi bhi screen ke upar 'overlay' (dikha) sakte hain.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
    * Jab aap ek link (noodle) banate hain, 'Interaction details' popup mein 'Action' ko `Maps to` se `Open Overlay` mein badlein.
    * **Overlay Settings (Nayi settings):**
        * `Destination:` Woh Frame jo aapko 'upar' dikhana hai (e.g., "My Sidebar Frame").
        * `Position:` Overlay kahan dikhega? (`Center` (Modal ke liye), `Top Left`, `Top Right`, `Bottom Center`... ya `Manual` (haath se set karein)).
        * `Close when clicking outside:` (Check karein) Jab user overlay ke baahar (grey area) click kare, toh overlay band ho jaaye.
        * `Add background behind overlay:` (Check karein) Peeche waali screen par ek 'kala/grey' (dark) tint daal deta hai (Modal ke liye zaroori).
        * `Animation:` `Move In` (Sidebar ke liye best), `Dissolve` (Modal ke liye best).
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek 'Menu' (Hamburger â˜°) icon se 'Sidebar' (Left Menu) kholna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Aapke paas ek 'Home Screen' (Frame) hai, jispar ek 'Menu' (â˜°) icon hai.
        2.  **Alag se,** canvas par ek chota 'Sidebar' (Frame) design karein (e.g., 300px width). Is Frame ka naam `Sidebar Menu` rakhein. (Yeh poori screen nahi hai, bas sidebar hai).
        3.  `Prototype` tab mein jaayein.
        4.  'Home Screen' ke 'Menu' (â˜°) icon ko select karein.
        5.  `+` noodle ko kheench kar `Sidebar Menu` (Frame) se jodein.
        6.  **Interaction details:**
            * `Trigger:` `On click`.
            * `Action:` `Maps to` ki jagah `Open Overlay` chunein.
            * `Destination:` `Sidebar Menu`.
            * `Position:` `Top Left` chunein (taaki woh top-left se khule).
            * (Optional) `Add background...` (50% Black) check karein.
            * `Animation:` `Move In` chunein aur direction â¬…ï¸ (left se) set karein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Prototype 'Play' (â–¶) karein. Jab aap 'Menu' (â˜°) icon par click karenge, toh 'Sidebar Menu' (Frame) `Move In` (slide) hokar left se aayega, aur peeche 'Home Screen' (halki dark tint ke saath) dikhti rahegi.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * 'Overlay' (e.g., Sidebar) ko *poori screen* (Frame) ke size ka bana dena. (Galat! Overlay Frame utna hi bada hona chahiye jitna pop-up ya sidebar dikhana hai).
    * 'Position' galat set karna. (Modal (pop-up) ke liye `Center` best hai).
    * `Close when clicking outside` ko check *na* karna, jisse user overlay (pop-up) ko band hi nahi kar paata (bina 'Close' X button ke).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main 'Modal' (pop-up) ko 'Navigate to' (doosri screen) se bhi toh dikha sakta hoon?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Aap dikha sakte hain, par `Open Overlay` 2 fayde deta hai: (1) Peeche waali screen (context) dikhti rehti hai. (2) Aapko `Close` (band) karne ke liye alag se link nahi banana padta; `Close when clicking outside` se kaam ho jaata hai.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** 'Overlay' ka use har us interaction ke liye hota hai jo 'destructive' (delete karna) ya 'confirm' (poochhna) waala ho. Jaise "Are you sure you want to delete?" (Yeh `Open Overlay` se 'Modal' (pop-up) aata hai).
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek E-commerce app mein 'Filter' button par click karna. `Open Overlay` se 'Filter Options' (Frame) neeche se (`Bottom Center` position se) slide hokar `Move In` karta hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * `Modals (Pop-ups)` ke liye: `Open Overlay` + `Center` + `Add background...` + `Dissolve`.
    * `Sidebars (Menus)` ke liye: `Open Overlay` + `Top Left` (ya `Top Right`) + `Move In`.
    * `Tooltips` ke liye: `Open Overlay` + `Manual` (position set karein) + `While hovering` (Trigger).
    * Overlay Frame ka size utna hi rakhein jitna zaroori hai.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Overlay ko band (Close) kaise karein?** 2 tareeke: (1) `Close when clicking outside` (setting) check karein. (2) Overlay Frame (e.g., 'Sidebar') ke andar ek 'Close' (X) icon banayein. Us icon ko select karein -> `Prototype` tab -> `+` noodle ko kahin mat jodein. 'Interaction details' mein Action: `Close Overlay` chunein.
    * **Keyboard (mobile) kaise dikhayein?** Ek 'Keyboard' (Frame) design karein. Input field (element) ko us 'Keyboard' (Frame) se `Open Overlay` (`Bottom Center`) se link kar dein.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. 'Sidebar' (Task) waali exercise poori karein.
    * 2. Ek 'Delete' button banayein. Ek chota 'Confirm Delete?' (Modal/Pop-up) Frame banayein. 'Delete' button ko 'Modal' Frame se `Open Overlay` (Position: `Center`) se link karein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * (Yeh Figma ka core feature hai. Practice hi key hai).

---

### 8.4: Interactive Components

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Interactive Components ğŸš€ (Clickable Variants banana).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh 'Components' (Module 6) aur 'Prototyping' (Module 8) ka sabse powerful combination hai. Yeh aapko *ek component set ke andar* (jaise 'Button' variants ke beech) prototype link banane deta hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** **Yeh aapka 90% prototyping time bachata hai.** Iske bina, agar aapko ek 'Button' (jo 100 screens par use hua hai) ka 'Hover' effect dikhana hai, toh aapko **100 alag screens** (hover state waali) banani padengi aur 100 link jodne padenge. 'Interactive Components' ke saath, aap *sirf 1 baar* 'Master Component' (â–) ke andar (`Default` variant se `Hover` variant tak) link banate hain. Ab woh 'Hover' effect aapki *saari* 100 instances (copies) par *automatically* kaam karega.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** **Har us component ke liye jiske 'states' (avasthaayein) hon.** Jaise:
    * `Button` (Default -> Hover)
    * `Toggle Switch` (Off -> On)
    * `Checkbox` (Unchecked -> Checked)
    * `Dropdown Menu` (Closed -> Open)
    * Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh 'screen explosion' (100 screens banane) ki problem ko solve karta hai aur aapke prototype ko 'high-fidelity' (asli jaisa) banata hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aap 'Hover' effects, 'Toggle' switches, ya 'Checkboxes' ko *asli* (real) tareeke se prototype nahi kar payenge. Aap ya toh yeh interactions (effects) dikha hi nahi payenge, ya phir aapko har interaction ke liye *poori poori screen* (Frame) duplicate karni padegi (e.g., "Screen with Toggle Off", "Screen with Toggle On"), jo bohot hi inefficient (slow) workflow hai.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
    * Aapko 'Component Set' (Module 6.2) (purple dotted box) ki zaroorat padegi.
    * Aap 'Prototype' tab mein jaate hain.
    * Aap 'Component Set' ke *andar* hi ek variant (e.g., `State=Default` waala button) ko doosre variant (e.g., `State=Hover` waala button) se 'noodle' (link) se jodte hain.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek 'Button' component (jo 2 variants: `Default`, `Hover` rakhta hai) ko 'interactive' banana.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Apne 'ğŸ§© Components' page par jaayein. Aapke paas 'Button' ka 'Component Set' â– (purple box) hona chahiye, jismein 2 variants (Default aur Hover) hon (jaisa 6.2 mein banaya tha).
        2.  **`Prototype` tab** mein switch karein. (Aap Component Set ke *andar* kaam kar rahe hain).
        3.  `Default` waale variant (button) ko select karein.
        4.  Uske `+` noodle ko kheench kar `Hover` waale variant (button) se jodein.
        5.  **Interaction details:**
            * `Trigger:` `On click` ki jagah `While hovering` chunein.
            * `Action:` `Change to` (Figma ne automatically chun liya).
            * `Destination:` `Button, State=Hover`.
            * `Animation:` `Dissolve` (ya `Smart Animate` agar `Default` aur `Hover` ke naam same hain).
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapne *Master* component ko interactive bana diya hai.
    * **Test:** Ab apni 'Design' (High-Fidelity) page par jaayein. 'Assets' panel se is 'Button' ki ek 'Instance' (â™¢) ko apne 'iPhone' Frame mein daalein.
    * **Play (â–¶) karein:** Ab prototype mein, jab aap mouse is button (Instance) ke *upar* le jaayenge, woh *apne aap* 'Hover' state mein badal jayega. Aapko 100 screens nahi banani padin!
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * **Component Set (Variants) ke bina** ise try karna. (Yeh feature *sirf* variants ke beech kaam karta hai).
    * Link (noodle) ko component ke *bahar* kisi 'Frame' se jod dena. (Nahi! Link ko *variant se variant tak* (andar hi andar) jodna hai).
    * 'Trigger' galat set karna. (Hover effects ke liye `While hovering`. Toggle switch (On/Off) ke liye `On click`).
    * Smart Animate (8.2) aur Interactive Components (8.4) ko confuse karna. (Smart Animate 2 *Frames* ke beech hota hai. Interactive Components 2 *Variants* ke beech hota hai).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Yeh Smart Animate (Toggle waala example) jaisa hi lag raha hai. Fark kya hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** 8.2 (Smart Animate) waale example mein, aapko 'Toggle Off' aur 'Toggle On' ke liye **2 poori screens (Frames)** banani padin. Is (8.4) waale tareeke mein, aap *sirf 1 'Toggle' component* banate hain (Off/On variants ke saath). Phir aap us *ek* component ko apni 'Home Screen' (Frame) par rakhte hain. Prototype mein 'Toggle' usi screen par (bina screen change kiye) On/Off hoga.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Design System mein *saare* components (Buttons, Toggles, Checkboxes, Dropdowns) 'Interactive Components' hote hain. Isse designer jab 'Design' (High-Fidelity) file mein prototype banata hai, toh 90% interactions (hover, click) *automatically* kaam karte hain, use kuch link nahi karna padta.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek 'Checkbox' component (Checked/Unchecked variants). Designer 'Unchecked' variant ko 'Checked' se `On click` -> `Change to` se link karta hai. (Aur 'Checked' ko waapas 'Unchecked' se). Ab prototype mein user us checkbox ko *asli* (real) ki tarah check/uncheck kar sakta hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Yeh feature = Variants + Prototyping.
    * Link hamesha *variant se variant* tak (Component Set ke andar) banayein.
    * `Hover` effects ke liye: `While hovering` trigger use karein.
    * `Toggles/Checkboxes` ke liye: `On click` trigger use karein.
    * `Dropdowns` ke liye: `On click` (Closed -> Open) aur `After delay` (Open -> Closed, agar mouse hatt jaaye) ka complex combination use hota hai.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Mera 'While hovering' kaam nahi kar raha!** Check karein ki (1) aapke paas 2 variants (Default, Hover) hain, aur (2) aapne link *Default se Hover* tak (Component Set ke andar) banaya hai.
    * **Kya main ek Interactive Component ko doosre se jod sakta hoon?** Haan! (e.g., 'Dropdown' (variant) ko `Open Overlay` (action) se 'Menu List' (frame) se jodna).
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. 'Button Hover' (Task) waali exercise poori karein.
    * 2. Ek 'Checkbox' component (2 variants: `Unchecked`, `Checked`) banayein. Unhe 'interactive' banayein taaki `On click` par woh 'Checked'/'Unchecked' hon.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * (Yeh Figma ka advanced core feature hai. Practice hi key hai).

---

### 8.5: Prototyping with Variables (Conditional Logic)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Prototyping with Variables (Prototype ko 'Smart' banana).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh prototyping ka sabse advanced feature hai. Yeh aapko 'Variables' (Module 7.2) ka istemaal karke **'Conditional Logic' (shartein)** (IF/THEN/ELSE) aur 'Formulas' (expressions) apne prototype mein daalne deta hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yeh aapke prototype ko 'static' (fixed flow) se 'dynamic' (badalne wala) bana deta hai. Isse aap *asli code jaisa* behavior (vyavhaar) bana sakte hain.
    * **Pehle:** 'Login' button hamesha 'Home' screen par jaata tha.
    * **Ab (Variables ke saath):** 'Login' button (Click) -> **IF** `password` (text variable) == "1234" **THEN** `Maps to` 'Home Screen' **ELSE** `Open Overlay` 'Error Message'.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Jab aapko 'high-fidelity' (asli) prototype banana ho jo 'data' (jaankari) ya 'states' (avastha) ko *yaad* (remember) rakh sake.
    * **Examples:** Ek 'Shopping Cart' (jismein total price update ho), ek 'Game' (jismein score badhe), ya ek 'Password' (jo check kare ki input sahi hai ya nahi).
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapke prototypes 'dumb' (bekaar) rahenge. Woh 'happy path' (sab sahi) toh dikha payenge, par 'sad path' (error states) ya 'dynamic data' (badalta content) nahi dikha payenge.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
    * **Set Variable (Action):** Yeh 'Prototype' interaction mein ek naya 'Action' (kriya) hai. `Maps to` ki jagah, aap `Set Variable` chunte hain. (e.g., `On click` -> `Set Variable` -> `Score` (variable) ko `Score + 1` (formula) kar do).
    * **Conditional (Logic):** Yeh `Interaction details` mein `+` daba kar add kiya jaata hai. Yeh ek 'IF' (agar) condition lagata hai. (e.g., `IF Score > 10` -> `Maps to` 'Winner Screen').
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek 'Add to Cart' button banana jo 'Cart Total' (Number Variable) ko update kare.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  'Local Variables' (Module 7.2) panel kholein. Ek 'Number' variable banayein. Naam: `CartTotal`. Value: `0`.
        2.  Apni screen (Frame) par ek 'Add' button banayein.
        3.  Ek 'Text' layer banayein (jahan total dikhega). Is text layer ko 'Text' (Right Panel) section mein 'Apply Variable' â“¥ icon se `CartTotal` variable se link kar dein. (Ab yeh '0' dikhayega).
        4.  `Prototype` tab mein jaayein.
        5.  'Add' button ko select karein. `+` (Interaction) par click karein.
        6.  **Interaction details:**
            * `Trigger:` `On click`.
            * `Action:` `Set Variable`.
            * `Target:` `CartTotal` (variable) ko `Set to:` `CartTotal + 1`.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Prototype 'Play' (â–¶) karein. Shuru mein text '0' dikhega. Jab aap 'Add' button par click karenge, text '1' ho jayega. Dobara click karenge, '2' ho jayega. Aapne 'state' (data) ko badalne wala prototype bana liya hai.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * 'Variables' (data) aur 'Variants' (visual states) mein confuse hona.
    * 'Expressions' (formulas) (jaise `Variable + 1`) ka syntax (likhne ka tareeka) galat likhna.
    * 'Conditional Logic' (IF/ELSE) ko set na kar paana (yeh '+' (add action) ke andar hota hai).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Yeh toh code jaisa lag raha hai. Kya mujhe iski zaroorat hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Shuruaat mein 90% zaroorat nahi hai. Simple `Maps to` aur `Smart Animate` kaafi hai. Yeh 'advanced' (bohot aage) ka topic hai, jo 'developer-level' prototypes ke liye hota hai.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Jo teams 'high-fidelity usability testing' (asli jaisi jaanch) karti hain, woh iska istemaal karti hain. Jaise, user ko ek 'asli' (real) form bharne ko dena aur check karna ki 'Error messages' (IF logic) sahi se kaam kar rahe hain ya nahi.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek 'E-commerce' prototype. `IF CartTotal == 0` (agar cart khaali hai), toh 'Checkout' button `Disabled` (variant) dikhe. `ELSE` (warna), 'Checkout' button `Enabled` (variant) dikhe.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Pehle 'Variables' (data) banayein (Local Variables panel mein).
    * Phir 'Elements' (text, layers) ko un variables se 'link' (jodein).
    * Phir 'Prototype' (action) mein `Set Variable` ya `Conditional` (IF/THEN) logic ka use karein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Kya yeh free plan mein hai?** 'Variables' (aur isliye yeh feature) 'Paid' plans par hi poori tarah se available hai.
    * **Main text input (e.g., password) kaise check karun?** Ek 'String' (text) variable banayein. Input field ko usse link karein. Phir button par `Conditional` logic lagayein: `IF MyTextVariable == "Password123"`.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. (Agar paid plan hai) 'Shopping Cart' (Task) waali exercise poori karein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Figma Advanced Prototyping (Official Docs):** (Yeh bohot naya aur advanced feature hai).

---

### 8.6: Live Device Preview

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Live Device Preview ğŸ“± (Apna design *asli phone* par dekhna).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh ek feature hai jo aapko **Figma Mirror** (mobile app) ka istemaal karke, apne computer par banaye gaye design ko *real-time* (usi samay) mein apne *asli* (real) phone (iOS ya Android) par dekhne deta hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Kyunki jo design computer (badi screen) par achha dikhta hai, woh zaroori nahi ki chote phone (asli device) par bhi achha dikhe. Font size (text) shayad bohot chota ho. 'Touch Targets' (Module 4.8) shayad bohot paas-paas hon. 'Live Preview' aapko design karte-karte *asli device* par check karne deta hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** **Hamesha,** jab aap 'Mobile' (phone) ke liye design kar rahe hon. Design process ke dauraan hi. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh "Looks good on my laptop, but... (laptop par achha dikh raha hai, par...)" waali problem ko solve karta hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aap galti se bohot chote fonts (e.g., 12px) ya chote 'touch targets' (e.g., 32px button) design kar denge, jo phone par padhne ya click karne laayak nahi honge. Aapka design 'unusable' (bekaar) ban sakta hai.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
    * **Computer (Figma):** Aap apni Figma file (jismein 'iPhone' Frame hai) kholein.
    * **Mobile (Phone):** 'App Store' / 'Play Store' se **"Figma Mirror"** app download karein.
    * **Login:** Dono jagah (computer aur phone app) *same* Figma account se login karein.
    * **Connect:** Apne computer par, 'iPhone' Frame ko *select* karein. Apne phone par 'Figma Mirror' app kholein. Woh automatically connect ho jayega.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Apne 'iPhone' design ko asli phone par 'mirror' (dekhna) karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Apne phone par 'Figma Mirror' app download aur login karein.
        2.  Apne computer par Figma file kholein.
        3.  Ek 'iPhone 14' Frame banayein aur usmein kuch text (e.g., 14px size) likhein.
        4.  Us 'iPhone 14' Frame ko computer par *select* karein.
        5.  Apne phone par 'Figma Mirror' app kholein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapke phone ki screen par aapka 'iPhone 14' Frame (text ke saath) *live* dikhne lagega.
    * **Live Test:** Ab computer par, text ka size 14px se 20px karein. Aap dekhenge ki *usi samay* (real-time) aapke phone par bhi text bada ho jayega.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Computer aur Phone app mein *alag-alag* account se login karna.
    * Computer par kisi 'Frame' ko select *na* karna. (Mirror app tabhi kaam karti hai jab computer par koi Frame select ho).
    * 'Figma' (main app) aur 'Figma Mirror' (mirror app) mein confuse hona. (Phone par 'Mirror' app chahiye).
    * USB se connect karne ki koshish karna. (Yeh Wi-Fi (ya same network) par (ya same account se) chalta hai).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main 'Present' (Play â–¶) karke bhi toh prototype dekh sakta hoon? Phone ki kya zaroorat hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** 'Present' (desktop par) aapko 'click' (mouse se) karne deta hai. 'Figma Mirror' (phone par) aapko 'tap' (ungli se) karne deta hai. Ek student 'Mirror' app se check karta hai ki uske banaye 'Touch Targets' (buttons) (Module 4.8) uski *ungli* ke liye aasan hain ya nahi.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Mobile designers ka *poora din* 'Figma Mirror' app unke phone par chalti rehti hai. Woh har 5 minute mein check karte hain ki unka design (color, spacing, font) asli device par kaisa lag raha hai.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek designer ko 'font size' (text) set karna hai. Woh 14px, 15px, 16px, 17px try karta hai, aur 'Mirror' app mein (phone ko door/paas karke) dekhta hai ki kaun sa size padhne (readability) mein sabse aasan hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * 'Figma Mirror' (iOS/Android) app download karein.
    * Dono devices par 'same account' se login karein.
    * Computer par 'Frame' (jo dekhna hai) ko select karein.
    * Hamesha 'Mobile design' ko 'asli Mobile' par test karein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Mera Mirror connect nahi ho raha!** Check karein: (1) Same account? (2) Same Wi-Fi network? (3) Computer par Frame selected hai?
    * **Kya main phone se prototype chala sakta hoon?** Haan! 'Figma Mirror' app aapke 'Flows' (Prototype links) ko bhi support karti hai. Aap phone par hi 'tap' (click) karke doosri screens par jaa sakte hain.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. 'Figma Mirror' app (Task) waali exercise poori karein aur real-time changes (font size badalna) karke dekhein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Figma Mirror (App Store / Play Store):** (Yeh hi tool hai).

Yeh tha hamara Module 8! ğŸ’¥ Aapne design ko 'zinda' karna seekh liyaâ€”basic linking se lekar, 'Smart Animate', 'Overlays', 'Interactive Components', aur 'Variables' tak.

Aapka skill set ab bohot 'job-ready' ke kareeb hai.

Jab aap ready hon, bas **"Module 9 shuru karo"** likh dena, aur hum 'Professional Polish' (design ko chamkana) aur 'Workflow' (kaam ko tez karna) seekhenge.

Chalo bhai, shuru karte hain aapke Figma (Beginner-to-Job-Ready) notes ka Module 9!

Module 8 mein humne design ko 'zinda' (live) bana diya. Ab Module 9 mein, hum seekhenge ki ek achhe design ko 'great' (shaandaar) design kaise banate hain. Hum 'Professional Polish' (design ko chamkana) aur 'Workflow' (kaam ko tez karna) par focus karenge.
