### 9.1: Advanced Typography (Variable Fonts, OpenType)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Advanced Typography âœï¸ (Fonts ko professional banana).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh aapke text (fonts) par 'fine-tuning' (baareek control) karne ke advanced features hain.
    * **Variable Fonts:** Yeh naye type ke fonts hain jo *ek hi* font file mein 'Weight' (motai), 'Slant' (tirchha-pan), etc. ke *saare* variations (roop) rakhte hain. Aapko 'Bold', 'Regular', 'Light' alag-alag nahi, balki ek 'slider' (slide karne waala) milta hai.
    * **OpenType Features:** Yeh font ke andar chhupe hue 'special rules' (khaas niyam) hote hain. Jaise 'Ligatures' (jo `f` aur `i` ko jodkar `ï¬` bana deta hai) ya 'Fractions' (jo `1/2` ko `Â½` jaisa sundar bana deta hai).
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yeh aapke design ko 'unique' (sabse alag) aur 'polished' (behtareen) look dete hain. 'Variable Fonts' designers ko 'perfect' weight (e.g., 'Medium' (500) aur 'SemiBold' (600) ke beech `550`) chunne ki azaadi dete hain. 'OpenType' features aapke text ko 'clean' aur 'readable' (padhne laayak) banate hain.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):**
    * **Variable Fonts:** Jab aapko font weight par poora control chahiye (e.g., ek heading ko perfect look dena).
    * **OpenType (Ligatures):** Hamesha 'on' rakhein (Body text ke liye).
    * **OpenType (Fractions):** Jab aap numbers (e.g., `1/2`, `3/4`) ya 'Price' (`$19.99`) likh rahe hon.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka text thoda 'unprofessional' (saada) lagega. "fi" (jaise 'financial' mein) jaise characters aapas mein 'clash' (takra) sakte hain. `1/2` ajeeb (1 / 2) dikhega. Aap standard font weights (400, 500, 600) tak hi seemit (limited) reh jayenge.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
    * Yeh saare options **Right Panel** -> **Text** section -> `...` (three-dot 'More') icon ke andar milte hain.
    * **Variable Tab:** Agar aapka font 'Variable' (jaise 'Inter' ya 'Roboto Flex') hai, toh aapko 'Variable' tab dikhega, jismein 'Weight', 'Slant', etc. ke *sliders* honge.
    * **Details Tab:** Yahan aapko 'OpenType' features milenge (jaise 'Ligatures', 'Fractions', 'Stylistic Sets').
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** 'Ligatures' (jo `fi` ko `ï¬` banata hai) ko 'On' karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Ek Text layer (`T`) banayein aur usmein "financial" ya "figure" likhein.
        2.  Text ko select rakhein.
        3.  Right Panel mein 'Text' section (jahan font ka naam hai) ke `...` (More) icon par click karein.
        4.  'Details' tab mein neeche scroll karein.
        5.  'OpenType features' section mein, 'Ligatures' (`fi` jaisa icon) par click karein (ya toggle on karein).
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aap dekhenge ki "fi" (alag-alag) judkar ek single, sundar "ï¬" (juda hua) character ban jayega.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * `...` (Text details) menu ko kabhi na kholna.
    * Yeh na samajhna ki 'Variable Font' kya hota hai. (Figma ka default font 'Inter' ek behtareen Variable Font hai).
    * Har font mein 'Variable' ya 'OpenType' features dhoondhna. (Yeh *font* par depend karta hai ki usmein yeh features hain ya nahi).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main toh 'Inter' font (default) se hi khush hoon. Yeh sab zaroori hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Haan! Kam se kam 'Ligatures' (jo `...` menu mein hai) hamesha 'on' rakhein. Yeh aapke paragraphs ko 'clean' look deta hai, jo ek chota sa 'professional polish' (chamkaan) hai.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Pro teams 'Variable Fonts' ka bohot istemaal karti hain, (1) Design mein fine-control ke liye, aur (2) (Developers ke liye) Web performance ke liye, kyunki 'Variable Font' ki *ek hi* file (jo 100KB ki ho) *saare* weights (Light se Black tak) provide kar deti hai, 10 alag-alag font files ki jagah.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek e-commerce site par price `$19.99` likhna. Designer `.99` (cents) ko select karta hai -> `...` (OpenType) -> 'Superscript' (ya 'Stylistic Set') use karke unhe chota aur upar (superscript) kar deta hai, jo zyada professional dikhta hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Hamesha 'Ligatures' (OpenType feature) ko 'on' rakhein.
    * `...` (Text details) menu ko zaroor explore karein.
    * Jab 'Google Fonts' (website) se font download karein, toh "Variable" waala filter check karein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Mera 'Variable' tab kyun nahi dikh raha?** Kyunki aapne jo font chuna hai (e.g., 'Arial'), woh 'Variable Font' nahi hai. 'Inter' chunein, tab dikhega.
    * **'Ligatures' kya hote hain?** Do ya teen characters (jaise f, i, l) ka ek 'joda' (glyph) jo unhe behtar dikhata hai (jaise `fi`, `ffl`).
    * **Yeh 'Stylistic Sets' kya hain?** Yeh font ke 'alternate' (doosre) designs hote hain (e.g., 'a' likhne ka doosra tareeka) jo font designer deta hai.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. 'Ligatures' (Task) waali exercise (text: "financial") ko poora karein.
    * 2. 'Inter' font (Variable font) chunein. 'Variable' tab (jo `...` menu mein hai) mein 'Weight' slider ko `400` se `900` tak dheere-dheere slide karke dekhein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Google Fonts (Website):** Wahan aap 'Variable' fonts ko filter aur test kar sakte hain.

---

### 9.2: Accessibility (Color Contrast, etc.)

**(Yeh ek CORE Foundational topic hai. Poora dhyaan dein.)**

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Accessibility (a11y) â™¿ (Sabke liye design banana).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Accessibility (jise 'a11y' bhi kehte hain) yeh sunishchit (ensure) karne ka process hai ki aapki website ya app ko **har koi** (bina kisi bhedbhaav) use kar sake. Ismein woh log bhi shaamil hain jinhe 'disabilities' (viklaangta) hain (jaise low vision, color blindness, ya jo keyboard se navigate karte hain).
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):**
    1.  **Ethical (Naitik):** Yeh sahi cheez hai. Internet sabke liye hai.
    2.  **Legal (Kanooni):** Bohot se deshon (jaise USA, Europe) mein yeh 'kanooni' (legal) zaroorat hai. Aapki company par 'case' (lawsuit) ho sakta hai agar aapka product accessible nahi hai.
    3.  **Business:** Yeh aapka 'user base' (logon ki sankhya) badhata hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** **Hamesha! Poore design process mein, shuru se aakhir tak.** Yeh koi 'final step' (aakhiri kadam) nahi hai, yeh ek 'mindset' (soch) hai. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh us problem ko solve karta hai jahan ek 'color blind' (rang-bhed na kar paane waala) user aapke 'Green' (Save) aur 'Red' (Delete) button mein fark nahi kar paata.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka product (app/website) aapke 15-20% potential users ko 'exclude' (baahar) kar dega. Aapki company par laakhon dollar ka 'kanooni' jurmaana lag sakta hai. Aap ek 'unethical' (anaitik) aur 'unprofessional' (gair-peshevar) designer maane jayenge.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown (Figma mein):**
    * **Color Contrast (Sabse Zaroori):** Aapke 'Text' (foreground) aur 'Background' ke beech rang (color) ka 'fark' (contrast) itna hona chahiye ki woh 'low vision' (kamzor nazar) waale logon ko bhi dikh jaaye.
    * **Font Size:** Text itna bada hona chahiye ki padha jaa sake. (Rule: Body text ke liye kam se kam `16px`).
    * **Touch Targets (Module 4.8):** Mobile par clickable area (Button, Icon) kam se kam `44px` by `44px` hona chahiye.
    * **Don't Rely on Color Alone:** Sirf 'rang' (color) se information na dein. (e.g., 'Error' (galti) dikhane ke liye, sirf 'Red' outline na banayein. Saath mein ek 'Icon' (âš ï¸) aur 'Text message' (e.g., "Invalid email") bhi dein).
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Apne 'Primary Button' (e.g., Blue background par White text) ka 'Color Contrast' (rang ka fark) check karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Sabse pehle, 'Community' (Module 7.4) se ek 'Accessibility' plugin install karein. Sabse popular hain: `Stark`, `Contrast`, ya `A11y - Color Contrast Checker`.
        2.  Maan lijiye humne `Stark` install kiya.
        3.  Apne 'Button' (Component ya Instance) ko select karein. (Aapko 2 layers select karni hai: 'Text' layer aur 'Background' (Frame/Rectangle) layer).
        4.  Right-click -> Plugins -> `Stark` -> `Contrast Checker`.
        5.  Plugin aapko ek 'Ratio' (anupaat) dega (e.g., `4.8:1`).
        6.  **WCAG Guidelines (Niyam):** Yeh international niyam hain.
            * `AA` (Minimum Pass): Ratio `4.5:1` (ya usse zyada) hona chahiye (Body text ke liye).
            * `AAA` (Enhanced Pass): Ratio `7:1` (ya usse zyada) hona chahiye.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Plugin aapko batayega ki aapka combination 'AA' aur 'AAA' level par `Pass` (safal) hai ya `Fail` (asafal). Agar 'Fail' hai, toh aapko apna color 'darker' (gehra) ya 'lighter' (halka) karna padega jab tak woh 'Pass' na ho jaaye.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * **Accessibility ko 'baad mein' (later) ya 'extra kaam' samajhna.** (Yeh sabse badi galti hai).
    * "Yeh 'sundar' (beautiful) lag raha hai, isliye theek hai." (Aapki aankhein 'Color Blind' user jaisi nahi hain. Hamesha 'Data' (plugin ratio) par bharosa karein, apni aankhon par nahi).
    * Body text ke liye `12px` ya `14px` font use karna (jo mobile par padhna bohot mushkil hai).
    * Sirf 'color' se 'error' (galti) ya 'success' (safalta) dikhana.
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Agar main accessible colors use karunga, toh mera design 'sundar' (vibrant) nahi, balki 'boring' (dull) ho jayega!"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Yeh ek 'myth' (galatfehmi) hai. Achha designer 'constraints' (seemao) ke andar hi sundar design banata hai. Ek student 'Stark' plugin ko apna 'best friend' banata hai. Har 'Color Style' (Module 5.1) ko save karne se *pehle* hi use check karta hai.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** **Design System (Module 7) mein *sirf* accessible components hi hote hain.** Team 'Color Styles' (e.g., `Brand-Primary-500`) ke saath 'Text Styles' (e.g., `Text-on-Primary`) ko 'jod' (pair) kar deti hai jinka contrast 'Pass' hota hai. Product Designer (jo DS use kar raha hai) ko sochna hi nahi padta. System hi 'accessible by default' (pehla se hi accessible) hota hai.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek 'Link' (hyperlink) ko 'underline' (neeche line) karna. Bohot se designer underline hata dete hain (kyunki woh 'sundar' nahi lagta). Lekin 'underline' zaroori hai, kyunki 'color blind' user ko (jo 'blue' color nahi dekh sakta) 'underline' se hi pata chalta hai ki woh 'text' nahi, balki ek 'link' hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * `Stark` ya `Contrast` plugin install karein aur *use* karein.
    * Text (Body) ke liye minimum `16px` font size rakhein.
    * Color ke alava hamesha 'dusra' indicator (jaise icon âš ï¸, text, ya underline) use karein.
    * Touch targets (Module 4.8) mobile par `44px` se kam na rakhein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **WCAG kya hai?** (Web Content Accessibility Guidelines). Yeh 'rules' (niyam) hain jinhe poori duniya follow karti hai.
    * **AA vs AAA?** `AA` 'must-have' (zaroori) hai. `AAA` 'nice-to-have' (behtareen) hai. Hamesha `AA` ko 'pass' karne ka target rakhein.
    * **'a11y' ka matlab kya hai?** Yeh 'Accessibility' ka shortcut hai. (Pehla 'A', aakhiri 'Y', aur beech mein 11 letters).
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. Ek 'light-grey' (`#E0E0E0`) background par 'medium-grey' (`#757575`) text likhein.
    * 2. `Stark` (ya `Contrast`) plugin install karein aur is combination ko check karein. (Yeh `Fail` hoga).
    * 3. Ab text ko 'dark' (gehra) karein jab tak woh `AA` 'Pass' na ho jaaye.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Plugins:** `Stark`, `Contrast`, `A11y - Color Contrast Checker`.
    * **Website:** "WCAG Guidelines" (W3C), "Material Design - Accessibility", "Apple HIG - Accessibility".

---

### 9.3: File Performance & Optimization

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** File Performance & Optimization âš¡ï¸ (Figma file ko fast (tez) rakhna).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh aapki Figma file ko 'saaf' (clean), 'organized' (vyavasthit), aur 'halka' (lightweight) rakhne ka process (tareeka) hai, taaki woh 'load' (khulne) aur 'run' (chalne) mein tez (fast) rahe.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Ek badi (heavy), gandi (messy) Figma file (jismein 50 'Pages', hazaaron 'hidden' (chupi hui) layers, aur 100-100MB ki 'unoptimized' (badi) images hon) bohot 'slow' (dheemi) ho jaati hai. Woh 'lag' (atak) karti hai, 'crash' ho sakti hai, aur team ke saath collaborate karna 'painful' (dardnaak) ho jaata hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** **Hamesha,** ek bade (large) project par kaam karte waqt. Har hafte (weekly) 'file hygiene' (safai) karna ek achhi aadat hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapki file 'lag' (atak) karegi. Load hone mein 2-3 minute legi. Aapka 'CPU/Memory' (computer resources) bohot use hoga. Aapke team members (khaaskar developers) aapse pareshan ho jayenge.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
    * **Image Optimization:** Badi (high-resolution) images (jaise 5MB ki photo) Figma file ko sabse zyada slow karti hain. Unhe 'compress' (chota) karna zaroori hai.
    * **Layer Hygiene:** Hazaaron 'unused' (bekaar) ya 'hidden' (chupi hui) layers ko 'delete' (hatana) zaroori hai.
    * **Use Components/Styles:** 100 'duplicate' (copy-paste) kiye gaye rectangles ki jagah, 100 'instances' (Module 6) use karna behtar hai.
    * **File Splitting:** Ek 'giant' (bahut badi) 50-page waali file ko 'split' (baant) dein. (e.g., 'Design System' (Library) file alag, 'iOS App' file alag, 'Website' file alag).
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Apni file mein badi (high-resolution) images ko 'compress' (optimize) karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  'Community' (Module 7.4) se ek 'Image Optimizer' plugin install karein. Sabse popular hain: `Downsize` ya `TinyImage Compressor`.
        2.  Maan lijiye humne `Downsize` (free) install kiya.
        3.  Apni Figma file mein, Right-click -> Plugins -> `Downsize`.
        4.  Plugin poori file (ya selected images) ko scan karega.
        5.  Aap settings set kar sakte hain (e.g., "Quality 70%", "Max width 2000px").
        6.  `Downsize` button dabayein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Plugin aapki saari badi images ko Figma ke andar hi 'compress' (chota) kar dega, bina unki 'visual' quality ko zyada kharaab kiye. Aapki file ka size (MB) kaafi kam ho jayega aur woh fast ho jayegi.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Badi (5000px wide, 10MB) photos ko 'Unsplash' (website) se download karke seedha Figma mein paste kar dena. (Hamesha 'Downsize' plugin use karein).
    * 'Drafts' (bekaar designs) ko 'Archive' (Module 1.2) page par move karne ki jagah, unhe 'hide' (aankh ğŸ‘ï¸ band karke chhupa dena). (Hidden layers bhi file ko heavy banati hain).
    * Ek hi file mein poori company ka kaam (Website, iOS, Android, Marketing) daal dena.
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Mera laptop (Mac M3) bohot fast hai, mujhe file optimize karne ki kya zaroorat hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Aapka laptop fast ho sakta hai, par aapke 'client' ya 'developer' (jise aap file 'view-only' bhejenge) ka laptop (ya browser) fast nahi ho sakta. Unke liye file 'lag' (atak) karegi. Hamesha apni file 'halki' (light) rakhein.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** 'File Performance' ek bohot bada mudda (issue) hai. Badi teams mein 'File Hygiene' (safai) ke 'rules' (niyam) hote hain. 'Design System' (Library file) ko hamesha 'split' (baant) kar rakha jaata hai (e.g., 'Foundations' [colors/text] ek alag library, 'Icons' alag library, 'Components' alag library).
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek 'Marketing Website' ki Figma file (jismein 20 badi-badi photos thin) 150MB ki ho gayi thi aur load hone mein 1 minute le rahi thi. 'Downsize' plugin use karke file 25MB ki ho gayi aur 5 second mein load hone lagi.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * **Badi images ko 'Downsize' (compress) karein.** (Sabse zaroori).
    * Unused (bekaar) layers aur pages ko 'Delete' (hatayein), 'Hide' (chhupayein) nahi.
    * 'Components' (Module 6) aur 'Styles' (Module 5) ka bharpoor istemaal karein.
    * Bade projects ko alag-alag 'files' (libraries) mein 'split' (baant) dein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **File slow kyun hoti hai?** Sabse bade kaaran: (1) Badi images, (2) Hazaaron layers, (3) Bohot zyada 'Effects' (jaise Background Blurs).
    * **'Hidden layers' (chupi hui) ko kaise dhoondein?** Figma mein `Ctrl + /` (ya `Cmd + /`) karke 'Select Hidden Layers' search karein (plugins bhi aate hain).
    * **'Clean up...' feature kya hai?** (Figma menu mein). Yeh 'detached instances' (toote hue components) ya 'missing styles' (gayab styles) ko dhoondhne aur fix karne mein madad karta hai.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. `Downsize` (plugin) install karein.
    * 2. Ek 'Frame' mein 5-6 badi (high-res) images 'Unsplash' (plugin) se daalein.
    * 3. `Downsize` plugin ko run karke dekhein ki woh kitna compression karta hai.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Plugins:** `Downsize`, `TinyImage Compressor`, `Clean Document`.

---

### 9.4: Automation Plugins (Rename It, Autoflow)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Automation Plugins ğŸ¤– (Boring, repetitive kaam ko automate karna).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh 'Community' (Module 7.4) ke woh 'magic' (jaadui) plugins (tools) hain jo aapke 'manual' (haath se), 'repetitive' (baar-baar hone waale) kaam ko 1-click mein kar dete hain.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Ek professional designer apna 'time' (samay) 'Problem Solving' (design sochna) mein lagata hai, 'Manual Labor' (boring kaam) mein nahi. Yeh plugins aapka *time* bachate hain, taaki aap behtar designer ban sakein.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Jab bhi aapko lage ki "Main yeh kaam pichhle 5 minute se copy-paste kar raha hoon."
    * `Rename It:` Jab aapko 100 layers (Frames) ka naam badalna ho.
    * `Autoflow:` Jab aapko 'User Flow' (Module 2.2) diagrams (screens ke beech arrows) banane hon.
    * `Content Reel:` (Topic 9.6) Jab aapko dummy data bharna ho.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka bohot saara 'time' (samay) 'waste' (barbaad) hoga. Aap 'Layers Panel' mein "Frame 58", "Frame 59", "Frame 60" ka naam haath se badalte rahenge, jabki doosra designer (jo plugin use karta hai) yeh kaam 5 second mein karke aage badh chuka hoga.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown (Must-Have Plugins):**
    * **`Rename It`:** 100 layers (e.g., "Frame 1", "Frame 2"...) ko 1-click mein `Rename` karta hai. (e.g., "Screen 1", "Screen 2"... ya "Screen %n"). Yeh layers ko 'ascending' (ASC 1, 2, 3) ya 'descending' (DESC) order mein bhi rename kar sakta hai.
    * **`Autoflow`:** Do 'Frames' (ya elements) ko select karke unke beech 'automatic' 'User Flow' (Module 2.2) waala 'arrow' (noodle) bana deta hai.
    * **`Content Reel` / `Lorem Ipsum`:** (Topic 9.6) Dummy data/text daalne ke liye.
    * **`Downsize`:** (Topic 9.3) Images ko optimize karne ke liye.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** 10 'Frames' (jo aapke 'Layers Panel' mein hain) ka naam `Rename It` se badalna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  'Community' se `Rename It` plugin install karein.
        2.  Apni 'Layers Panel' (Left) mein, 10 Frames ko (Shift daba kar) select karein (jinke naam "Frame 1", "Frame 2"... hain).
        3.  Right-click -> Plugins -> `Rename It`.
        4.  Plugin ka panel khulega.
        5.  `Find & Replace` tab (ya `Rename Sequence`) mein jaayein.
        6.  Input box mein likhein: `Screen %n` (ya `Screen %1` agar 1 se shuru karna hai). `%n` ka matlab hai 'number'.
        7.  `Rename` button dabayein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapki saari 10 layers ka naam 1 second mein badal kar `Screen 1`, `Screen 2`, `Screen 3`... ho jayega.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * In plugins ke baare mein pata hi na hona.
    * Sab kaam haath se (manually) karna aur sochna "designing mein itna hi time lagta hai."
    * Bahut saare (100+) plugins install kar lena jo aap kabhi use nahi karte (yeh Figma ko slow kar sakta hai).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main 'Autoflow' kyun use karun? Main 'Pen Tool' (Module 3.2) se bhi toh arrow (teer) bana sakta hoon."
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Aap bana sakte hain, par `Autoflow` ka arrow 'smart' hota hai. Agar aap 'Frame' (screen) ko move karenge, toh `Autoflow` ka arrow *saath mein* move hoga. Aapka Pen Tool waala arrow wahin reh jayega.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** 'Automation Plugins' workflow ka 'standard' (maanak) hissa hain. Team ke paas 'approved plugins' ki list hoti hai jo sab use karte hain. `Autoflow` ka use 'User Flow' diagrams (presentations ke liye) tezi se banane ke liye hota hai.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek designer ko 50 screens ka 'User Flow' (diagram) banana hai (Client ko present karne ke liye). Woh `Autoflow` plugin run karta hai -> Screen 1 (click) -> Screen 2 (click) -> (Arrow ban gaya). Screen 2 (click) -> Screen 3 (click) -> (Arrow ban gaya). 5 minute mein poora flow diagram ready.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * Apna 'Must-Have' plugin set banayein:
        * `Rename It` (Naming ke liye).
        * `Autoflow` (Flows ke liye).
        * `Content Reel` (Data ke liye).
        * `Downsize` (Images ke liye).
        * `Stark` (Accessibility ke liye).
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **Plugins install karna 'safe' (surakshit) hai?** Hamesha 'popular' (jinke >100k+ downloads/users hon) aur 'trusted' (bharosemand) publishers (jaise 'Figma' ya 'Microsoft') ke hi plugins install karein.
    * **Mera plugin kahan milenga?** Install karne ke baad, apni design file mein, Canvas par Right-Click -> 'Plugins' -> [Aapka Plugin].
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. `Rename It` (Task) waali exercise poori karein.
    * 2. Do 'Frames' (screens) banayein. `Autoflow` plugin install karein. Dono ko select karke `Autoflow` run karein (unke beech ek arrow ban jaana chahiye).
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * (Upar di gayi list hi sabse zaroori hai).

---

### 9.5: Custom Fonts

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Custom Fonts ğŸ…°ï¸ (Apne brand ka (ya naya) font use karna).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** 'Google Fonts' (jo Figma mein pehle se (built-in) hote hain) ke alava, apne 'local computer' (jo aapne download/purchase kiye hain) se custom fonts (`.otf`, `.ttf` files) ko Figma mein use karna.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Har brand (jaise Apple, Netflix, Google) ka apna 'custom' (khaas) font hota hai jo unki 'identity' (pehchaan) ka hissa hai. Aapka client aapko hamesha 'Inter' ya 'Roboto' (Google Fonts) nahi, balki unka apna 'brand font' (e.g., "Helvetica Neue", "Circular", "Gotham") use karne ko kahega.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Jab aapka client aapko `.ttf` ya `.otf` font file de. Ya jab aap 'Google Fonts' ke alava koi aur font (jo aapne 'Dafont' ya 'FontSquirrel' se download kiya hai) use karna chahte hon.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aap client ke 'Brand Guidelines' (brand ke niyam) ko follow nahi kar payenge. Aapka design 'off-brand' (brand jaisa nahi) lagega.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown (2 Tareeke):**
    * **1. Figma Desktop App (Sabse Aasan Tareeka):** Agar aap Figma ki 'Desktop App' (Browser ki jagah) use karte hain, toh aapko *kuch nahi karna*. Desktop App *automatically* (apne aap) aapke computer ke saare 'local fonts' (jo 'Font Book' (Mac) ya 'Fonts' (Win) folder mein install kiye hain) ko access kar leti hai.
    * **2. Figma Browser (Extra Step):** Agar aap 'Browser' (e.g., Google Chrome) mein Figma use karte hain, toh browser ko aapke 'local fonts' ka access *nahi* hota. Aapko **"Figma Font Installer"** (ek chota software/service) Figma ki website se download karke install karna padega.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek 'Custom Font' (jo aapne download kiya hai) ko Figma (Desktop App) mein use karna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Sabse pehle, font file (e.g., `Poppins.ttf`) ko apne computer par 'install' (daalna) karein. (Windows/Mac par file par double-click karein -> 'Install Font' button dabayein).
        2.  Agar aapki 'Figma Desktop App' khuli hai, toh use 'Restart' (poori tarah band karke waapas chalu) karein.
        3.  Apni Figma file kholein.
        4.  `T` (Text) se kuch likhein.
        5.  Right Panel (Text section) mein 'Inter' (default font) par click karein aur apna font (e.g., "Poppins") search karein.
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapka text custom font ('Poppins') mein badal jayega.
    * **(Agar Browser use kar rahe hain):** Figma 'Home' (Dashboard) par jaayein -> Top-right corner (aapka naam) -> Settings -> 'Fonts' section -> `Download the font installer`. Use install karein. Browser tab refresh karein.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * Font ko computer par install *kiye bina* Figma mein dhoondhna. (Pehle install karein!).
    * 'Figma Font Installer' (browser ke liye) install na karna aur sochna ki browser mein font kaam nahi kar raha.
    * **File share karna:** Yeh sochna ki agar *aapne* custom font use kiya hai, toh woh *sabko* (jise aap link bhejenge) dikhega. (Nahi! Agar receiver (link paane waale) ke paas woh font install nahi hai, toh use 'Missing Font' (font gayab hai) warning dikhegi).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Toh 'Missing Font' (font gayab) waali problem ko kaise solve karein?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Agar aap student hain, toh 'Google Fonts' (Inter, Roboto, Poppins) hi use karein. Woh 'cloud' (internet) par hain aur Figma mein pehle se (built-in) hote hain, isliye woh 'missing' nahi honge. Agar aap freelancer hain aur client ne custom font diya hai, toh (1) Developer ko `.ttf` file alag se dein, aur (2) Client (jo sirf 'view' karega) ke liye text ko 'flatten' (vector bana dena) (Right-click -> 'Outline Stroke') kar dein (par yeh bura tareeka hai, kyunki text edit nahi ho sakta).
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Is problem ko solve karne ke liye, Team 'Paid' (Organization) plan mein 'Shared Fonts' (saajha fonts) feature ka use karti hai. Ismein, Admin font ko *Figma par 'upload'* kar deta hai. Ab woh font team ke har member ke liye (bina install kiye) available ho jaata hai.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Client ne `Circular.ttf` (Spotify ka font) diya. Designer ne use install kiya (Desktop app use karke). Design banaya. Developer ko handoff (Module 10) karte waqt, `.ttf` file bhi saath mein di.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * (1) Font computer par 'Install' karein.
    * (2) Agar Browser, toh 'Font Installer' (Figma ka) run karein.
    * (3) Figma App ko 'Restart' karein.
    * Team ke saath 'Google Fonts' (cloud) use karna sabse aasan (safe) tareeka hai 'missing fonts' se bachne ka.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **'Missing Font' warning aa rahi hai! Kya karun?** Iska matlab hai ki file mein use hua font (e.g., "Helvetica") aapke computer par install nahi hai. Ya toh us font ko (kanooni tareeke se) install karein, ya 'Missing Font' warning par click karke use 'Inter' (default) se 'replace' (badal) dein.
    * **'Figma Desktop App' vs 'Browser'?** Professionals 'Desktop App' prefer karte hain, kyunki (1) woh thodi fast hai, aur (2) 'Local Fonts' automatically (apne aap) kaam karte hain.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. 'Google Fonts' (website) se koi naya font (e.g., "Lobster" ya "Poppins") download karein.
    * 2. Use computer par 'Install' karein.
    * 3. Figma (Desktop app 'restart' karke, ya Browser 'refresh' karke) mein us font ko dhoondh kar use karein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Figma Font Installer:** (Agar aap browser user hain).
    * **Google Fonts (Website):** Free fonts ka best source.

---

### 9.6: Using Placeholders (Lorem Ipsum, Content Reel)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Using Placeholders ğŸ“ (Dummy (nakli) content use karna).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh design process mein 'asli' (real) content (jaise text, images, names) ki jagah 'dummy' (nakli) ya 'placeholder' (jagah bharne waala) content ka istemaal karna hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Kyunki aksar, jab aap design (e.g., 'Profile Page') shuru karte hain, tab aapke paas client se 'asli' (real) user data (photos, names, bio) *nahi* mila hota hai. Agar aap 'asli' content ka intezaar (wait) karenge, toh aap design shuru hi nahi kar payenge. Placeholders aapko 'layout' (structure) ko design aur test karne dete hain.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Design ke shuruaati (early) ya 'Wireframing' (Module 2.3) phase mein. Jab bhi aapke paas 'asli' (real) content na ho. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh 'designer's block' (kaam shuru na kar paana) ko solve karta hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aap design shuru nahi kar payenge. Ya, (jo aur bura hai), aap 'asli' content ki jagah "Name", "Email", "Lorem ipsum..." haath se likhenge. Yeh professional nahi lagta aur 'real text' (asli text) jaisa 'feel' (ehsaas) nahi deta.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown (Tools/Plugins):**
    * **`Lorem Ipsum` (Text):** Yeh ek standard 'dummy' (Latin) text hai jo designers (sadiyon se) 'filler' (jagah bharne) ke liye use kar rahe hain. (Plugin `Lorem Ipsum` se 1-click mein mil jaata hai).
    * **`Content Reel` (Sabse Best Plugin):** Yeh 'Community' (Module 7.4) ka ek 'must-have' plugin hai. Yeh aapko 1-click mein *realistic* (asli jaise) *dummy* text (Names, Addresses, Headlines), *dummy* images (Avatars, Products), aur *dummy* icons daalne deta hai.
    * **`Unsplash` (Plugin):** (Module 7.4) 'Real' (asli), high-quality 'photos' (tasveeron) ke liye.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
    * **Task:** Ek 'Profile Card' (Avatar, Name, Email) mein `Content Reel` se dummy content daalna.
    * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  'Community' (Module 7.4) se `Content Reel` plugin install karein.
        2.  Apna 'Profile Card' (layout) design karein: Ek Circle `(O)` (Avatar ke liye), uske paas ek Text layer `(T)` (Name ke liye), aur uske neeche ek aur Text layer `(T)` (Email ke liye).
        3.  `Content Reel` plugin ko run karein (Right-click -> Plugins -> Content Reel).
        4.  Plugin ka panel khulega.
        5.  **Image:** Apne 'Circle' (shape) ko select karein. 'Content Reel' panel mein 'Images' tab -> 'Avatars' -> (kisi avatar par click karein). (Circle mein dummy photo fill ho jayegi).
        6.  **Name:** Apne 'Name' (Text layer) ko select karein. 'Content Reel' panel mein 'Text' tab -> 'Full Name' -> (kisi naam par click karein). (Dummy naam aa jayega).
        7.  **Email:** Apne 'Email' (Text layer) ko select karein. 'Content Reel' panel mein 'Text' tab -> 'Email' -> (click karein). (Dummy email aa jayega).
    * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapka 'Profile Card' (jo pehle khaali tha) 5 second mein 'real' (asli) data jaisa dikhne laga hai.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
    * **`Lorem Ipsum` ko *final design* mein chhod dena.** (Yeh bohot unprofessional (gair-peshevar) lagta hai).
    * `Unsplash` (ya `Content Reel`) se daali gayi 'dummy' images ko 'final' (aakhiri) design mein use kar lena. (In images ke 'copyrights' (adhikaar) hote hain. Hamesha check karein, ya client se 'asli' images maangein).
    * 'Lorem Ipsum' (Latin) text ko 'Hi-Fi' design mein use karna. (Problem: 'Lorem Ipsum' 'English' text jaisa 'space' (jagah) nahi leta, jisse aapka layout 'asli' text aane par 'toot' (break) sakta hai).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
    * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Toh `Lorem Ipsum` bekaar (useless) hai?"
    * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Nahi! `Lorem Ipsum` (plugin) 'Low-Fidelity Wireframes' (Module 2.3) ke liye 'perfect' hai, kyunki wahan focus 'layout' (dhaanche) par hota hai, 'content' (likhaawat) par nahi. 'High-Fidelity' (sundar) designs ke liye hamesha `Content Reel` (jo 'real-looking' (asli jaisa) English text deta hai) 100 guna behtar hai.
    * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Professionals 'data' (jaankari) ko bohot serious lete hain. Woh 'Content Reel' ya 'real data' (agar mil jaaye) par depend karte hain. Yeh design ko 'data-informed' (jaankari ke saath) banata hai.
    * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek designer ko 20 'User Testimonials' (reviews) ki list design karni hai. Woh 20 text boxes select karta hai -> `Content Reel` run karta hai -> 'Testimonials' category par 'Run' (ya click) karta hai -> 20 alag-alag dummy reviews 1-click mein fill ho jaate hain. (Kaam 30 minute ki jagah 30 second mein ho gaya).
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
    * **Wireframes (Lo-Fi):** `Lorem Ipsum` (Plugin) use karein.
    * **Designs (Hi-Fi):** `Content Reel` (Plugin) ya `Unsplash` (Plugin) use karein.
    * **Final Handoff (Module 10):** Hamesha koshish karein ki final handoff se pehle *saara* 'dummy' (nakli) content 'asli' (real) client content se badal (replace) diya jaaye.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
    * **`Lorem Ipsum` ka matlab kya hai?** Yeh ek 'scrambled' (toda-moda hua) Latin text hai (Cicero ki ek kitaab se). Iska koi 'matlab' (meaning) nahi hota. Yeh sirf 'filler' (jagah bharne waala) text hai.
    * **Kya `Content Reel` free hai?** Haan! Yeh (aur `Unsplash`, `Lorem Ipsum`) 'Community' (Module 7.4) par free plugins hain.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
    * 1. `Content Reel` (Task) waali exercise (Profile Card) poori karein.
    * 2. Ek bada 'Text Box' banayein aur `Lorem Ipsum` plugin (Community se install karke) se usmein 3 paragraph 'dummy' (Latin) text daalein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
    * **Plugins:** `Content Reel` (Must-have), `Lorem Ipsum`, `Unsplash` (Must-have).

---

Yeh tha hamara Module 9! ğŸŒŸ Aapne design ko 'polish' (chamkana) seekh liya haiâ€”Accessibility (a11y) se lekar, File performance (safai), aur Automation (time bachana) tak.

Aapka design ab 'Job-Ready' level ka 'professional' (peshevar) dikh raha hai.

Jab aap ready hon, bas **"Module 10 shuru karo"** likh dena, aur hum 'aakhiri' (final) module karenge: **Collaboration & Handoff** (Team ke saath kaam karna aur developers ko design dena).

=============================================================

Chalo bhai, shuru karte hain aapke Figma (Beginner-to-Job-Ready) notes ka Module 10\!

Yeh hamara aakhiri (final) module hai\! ğŸ¥³ Yahan hum seekhenge ki ek design ko 'finish' (poora) karke, team ke saath collaborate (milkar kaam) kaise karte hain, aur sabse zaroori, developers ko apna design 'handoff' (saupna) kaise karte hain taaki woh use 'code' (asli product) mein badal sakein. Yeh aapko 'Job-Ready' banayega.

### 10.1: Version Control & History

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Version Control & History ğŸ’¾ (Apne design ka 'Undo' button).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Version History Figma ka 'automatic backup' (apne aap save hone waala) system hai. Yeh aapke kaam ke 'versions' (sanskaran) ko time-to-time automatically save karta rehta hai, taaki agar aapse koi galti ho jaaye (jaise poori screen delete ho jaaye), toh aap 'time machine' ki tarah puraane version par waapas jaa sakein.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yeh ek 'safety net' (suraksha jaal) hai. Isse aapko "Design\_v5\_final\_FINAL\_v2.fig" naam se 10 alag-alag files save karne ki zaroorat nahi padti. Sirf *ek hi* file hoti hai, aur uski poori history (itihaas) Figma sambhaal ke rakhta hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Jab aapse koi badi galti ho jaaye (e.g., "Maine galti se poora 'User Flow' delete kar diya aur 'Undo' (Ctrl+Z) bhi kaam nahi kar raha"). Ya jab aapko dekhna ho ki "Yeh design 2 hafte pehle kaisa dikhta tha?"
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Agar aapka auto-save fail ho jaaye ya aapse koi aisi galti ho jaaye jo 'Undo' (Ctrl+Z) se theek na ho sake, toh aap apna *poora kaam* (work) kho sakte hain. Aapka ghanton (ya dinon) ka kaam barbaad ho sakta hai.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
      * **Location:** File ke naam (top center) ke paas waale 'chevron' (neeche waala arrow ğŸ”») par click karein -\> `File` -\> `Show version history`.
      * **Auto-Save:** Figma har 30 minute (ya activity ke hisaab se) automatically ek version save karta hai.
      * **Named Versions (Manual Save):** Yeh 'manual' (haath se) save karna hai. Yeh sabse zaroori hai. Aap `Ctrl+Alt+S` (ya `Cmd+Opt+S`) daba kar 'current' version ko ek 'naam' (jaise "Milestone 1: Wireframes Complete") dekar save kar sakte hain.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
      * **Task:** Ek important milestone (jaise 'Wireframes final') ko 'Named Version' (manual save) ki tarah save karna.
      * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Aapne apne wireframes (Module 2.3) poore kar liye hain.
        2.  Shortcut dabayein: `Ctrl + Alt + S` (Windows) ya `Cmd + Opt + S` (Mac).
        3.  Ek 'Save to Version History' (popup) khulega.
        4.  `Title:` (Naam) dein: "Milestone 1 - Wireframes Complete".
        5.  `Description:` (Vivaran) (optional) dein: "Initial wireframes for all 5 screens approved by client".
        6.  `Save` button dabayein.
      * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapka version save ho gaya hai. Ab agar aapse 3 din baad bhi poori file delete ho jaaye, toh aap 'Show version history' (Right Panel) mein jaakar is 'Named Version' (`Milestone 1`) ko 'Restore' (waapas laana) kar sakte hain.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
      * Sirf 'Auto-Save' par bharosa karna. (Auto-save 'Milestone' (khaas padaav) save nahi karta, bas time save karta hai. Hamesha `Ctrl+Alt+S` se 'Named Version' banayein).
      * Alag-alag file banana (`v1`, `v2`, `v3`). (Yeh Figma mein *nahi* karna hai).
      * Free plan mein Version History dhoondhna. (Free plan mein history 'limited' (seemit) (e.g., 7-30 din) hoti hai. Paid plan mein 'unlimited' (aseemit) history milti hai).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
      * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Figma toh 'auto-save' (apne aap save) karta hai. Mujhe `Ctrl+Alt+S` (manual save) ki kya zaroorat hai?"
      * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** 'Auto-save' har 30 minute mein save karta hai. Maan lijiye aapne 2 ghante tak ek naya 'direction' (design idea) try kiya, aur fir aapko laga ki "Nahi, 2 ghante pehle waala design hi achha tha." Ab 'auto-save' waali list mein se 2 ghante pehle waala version dhoondhna mushkil hai. Agar aapne `Ctrl+Alt+S` se "Milestone: Client Feedback v1" save kiya hota, toh aap 1-click mein waapas jaa sakte the.
      * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** 'Named Versions' (manual save) team workflow ke liye *sabse zaroori* hain.
          * `Save Version` (e.g., "Ready for Dev Handoff v1.0") -\> Developer ko handoff karna.
          * `Save Version` (e.g., "Sprint 5 Complete") -\> Sprint (kaam ka daur) khatam hone par.
          * `Save Version` (e.g., "Client Presentation - Oct 25") -\> Client ko dikhane se pehle.
      * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek designer ne poora 'checkout flow' redesign kiya. Fir team ne decide kiya ki 'puraana' (old) flow hi behtar tha. Designer 'Version History' mein gaya, 3 hafte puraana 'Named Version' ("Pre-Redesign") dhoondha, aur use 'Restore' (waapas) kar liya. 5 minute mein 3 hafte ka kaam 'reverse' (ulta) ho gaya.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
      * 'File' -\> `Save to Version History` (`Ctrl+Alt+S`) ko apni aadat bana lein.
      * Har 'milestone' (bada kadam) (e.g., Wireframes done, Handoff to dev) par 'Named Version' zaroor banayein.
      * Clear 'Title' (naam) aur 'Description' (vivaran) dein.
      * `v1`, `v2`, `v3` naam se alag-alag *files* na banayein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
      * **'Restore' (waapas laana) kaise karein?** 'Version History' panel (Right) mein, version ke `...` (more) icon par click karein -\> 'Restore this version'.
      * **Kya 'Restore' karne se mera naya (current) kaam delete ho jayega?** Nahi. Jab aap puraana version 'Restore' karte hain, Figma aapke 'current' (naye) kaam ko bhi history mein (ek naya version bana kar) save kar leta hai. Kuch bhi delete nahi hota.
      * **Main 2 versions ko 'compare' (tulna) kar sakta hoon?** Nahi, Figma mein side-by-side compare (tulna) nahi kar sakte (jaise code mein hota hai). Aapko version ko 'restore' (ya 'duplicate') karke dekhna padega.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
      * 1.  Apni design file kholein.
      * 2.  `Ctrl + Alt + S` dabayein aur ek 'Named Version' banayein (Naam: "My First Save").
      * 3.  Ab file ke naam (top center) ke arrow ğŸ”» -\> `Show version history` par click karke dekhein ki aapka 'save' wahan dikh raha hai ya nahi.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
      * (Yeh Figma ka core feature hai).

-----

### 10.2: Comments & Collaboration

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Comments & Collaboration ğŸ’¬ (Team ke saath file mein baat-cheet karna).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Figma 'multiplayer' (ek saath kaam karne waala) tool hai.
      * **Collaboration (Saath Kaam):** Aap (aur aapki team ke 10 log) *ek hi time par*, *ek hi file mein* design kar sakte hain. Aapko sabke mouse cursors (teer) dikhenge.
      * **Comments (Tippani):** Yeh file ke upar 'sticky notes' (notes chipkana) jaisa hai. Aap design ke *kisi bhi hisse* (jaise ek button) par 'pin' (laga) karke ek 'comment' (tippani) chhod sakte hain (e.g., "@Developer, yeh button `44px` ka hona chahiye").
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yeh 'communication' (baat-cheet) ko 'contextual' (sandarbh ke saath) aur 'real-time' (usi samay) bana deta hai. Aapko 'Slack' ya 'Email' par "Us file mein, Home screen par, top-right waale button ka color badal do" likhne ki zaroorat nahi hai. Aap *seedha* us button par 'click' karke comment likh sakte hain.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):**
      * **Collaboration:** Jab ek team (2+ designer) *ek saath* design (e.g., 'design sprint') kar rahi ho.
      * **Comments:** **Roz\!** Feedback (raay) dene ke liye, feedback maangne ke liye, developers ko notes dene ke liye.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aapka 'feedback loop' (raay lene-dene ka chakkar) bohot 'slow' (dheema) aur 'disconnected' (toota hua) hoga. Aapko feedback ke liye Slack/Email/Zoom par depend rehna padega, jahan 'context' (sandarbh) kho jaata hai (kis button ki baat ho rahi hai?).
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
      * **Share Button (Top Right):** Yahan se aap logon ko file mein 'invite' (aamantrit) karte hain (e.g., email se).
      * **Permissions (Ijaazat):** Aap set kar sakte hain ki woh `can view` (sirf dekh sakta hai) (Developers/PMs ke liye) ya `can edit` (badlaav kar sakta hai) (Doosre designers ke liye).
      * **Comment Tool (C):** Toolbar mein 'bubble' (baat-cheet) ğŸ’¬ icon (ya `C` dabayein).
      * **Adding a Comment:** `C` dabayein -\> design par kahin (e.g., button) click karein -\> comment likhein -\> (Use `@` (at) karke team member ko 'tag' (mention) karein, e.g., `@John`) -\> 'Post' (bhejein).
      * **Resolving Comments:** Jab kaam poora ho jaaye, comment par 'Checkmark' (sahi tik âœ“) par click karein. Comment 'Resolve' (sulajh) jaata hai (gayab ho jaata hai, par history mein rehta hai).
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
      * **Task:** Ek team member se 'feedback' (raay) maangna.
      * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Apne 'Home Screen' (Frame) par jaayein.
        2.  `C` (Comment tool) dabayein.
        3.  Apne 'Header' (component) par click karein.
        4.  Comment box mein likhein: "@[TeamMateName] (e.g., @Aman) kya aapko yeh header theek lag raha hai? Ya icon bohot bada hai?"
        5.  `Post` button dabayein.
      * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapke team member (Aman) ko ek 'email' (aur 'Slack', agar connected hai) notification jayega. Woh us link par click karega, aur Figma *seedha* us header par zoom karke aapka comment dikha dega.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
      * 'View' (dekhne) aur 'Edit' (badlaav) permissions (ijaazat) mein confuse hona. (Developers ko hamesha `can view` dein).
      * Comment chhodne ke baad `C` (Comment tool) se waapas `V` (Move tool) par aana bhool jaana. (Aap `V` dabana chahte hain, par `C` active hone se aap har jagah comment pin karte rehte hain).
      * Comments ko 'Resolve' (sulajhana âœ“) na karna. (Jisse file mein 100 puraane comments dikhte rehte hain).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
      * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main Slack/Email par hi feedback de sakta hoon. File mein 'comments' (tippani) kyun daalun?"
      * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Aap 'client' (ya 'mentor') ko `can view` (dekhne) ka link bhejte hain. Client (bina Figma account ke bhi) file kholta hai, `C` (Comment tool) se design par 'pins' (nishaan) laga kar feedback deta hai (e.g., "Yeh color badlo", "Yeh text bada karo"). Aapko *ek hi jagah* saara feedback mil jaata hai.
      * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** 'Comments' hi 'asynchronous' (alag-alag time par) communication ka main tareeka hain. Designer kaam karta hai -\> `Comment` (tippani) chhodta hai "@PM, please review." -\> PM (Product Manager) (2 ghante baad) review karta hai -\> `Comment` (tippani) chhodta hai "@Designer, looks good, but please add a 'Back' button." -\> Designer (agle din) us comment ko 'Resolve' (sulajha âœ“) karta hai.
      * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek designer, ek PM, aur 2 developers *ek hi time par* ek hi file mein hain. Designer 'design' kar raha hai (Design tab). PM 'comment' (tippani) kar raha hai. Developers 'code' (CSS) nikaal rahe hain (Inspect tab). Yahi Figma ki asli power (taakat) hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
      * Feedback (raay) ke liye hamesha 'Comment' tool (`C`) ka use karein.
      * Apne team members ko `@mention` (tag) karein taaki unhe notification (soochana) jaaye.
      * Jab feedback (kaam) poora ho jaaye, comment ko 'Resolve' (âœ“) karein.
      * Developers aur PMs ko `can view` (dekhne) ki ijaazat dein, `can edit` (badlaav) ki nahi.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
      * **'Resolve' (sulajhe hue) comments kahan jaate hain?** Woh delete nahi hote. File ke naam ğŸ”» -\> `Show resolved comments` se aap unhe waapas dekh sakte hain.
      * **Kya main 'emoji' (jaise ğŸ‘, â¤ï¸) use kar sakta hoon?** Haan\! Toolbar mein 'bubble' (ğŸ’¬) icon ke paas 'Reactions' (smiley) icon hota hai. Isse aap jaldi se 'stamp' (mohar) laga sakte hain (e.g., 'Approved' âœ…, 'Looks good' ğŸ‘).
      * **'Share' (baantne) ke options kya hain?** Top-right 'Share' button -\> `Anyone with the link` -\> `can view`. Yeh sabse aasan tareeka hai kisi ko (bina account ke bhi) file 'dekhne' (view) ke liye bhejne ka.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
      * 1.  Apni file mein `C` (Comment tool) dabayein aur apne 'Button' (component) par ek 'comment' (tippani) (khud ke liye) chhod dein (e.g., "Yeh button final hai").
      * 2.  Us comment par 'Reply' (jawaab) karein.
      * 3.  Us comment ko 'Resolve' (âœ“) karein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
      * **Slack / Jira (Integrations):** Figma comments ko seedha Slack ya Jira (project management tools) mein bhej sakte hain.

### 10.3: Developer Handoff (Inspect Tab, CSS Code)

**(Yeh ek CORE Foundational 'Job-Ready' topic hai. Poora dhyaan dein.)**

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Developer Handoff (Inspect Tab) ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ’» (Design ko code mein badalne ke liye dena).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** 'Handoff' (saupna) woh process (prakriya) hai jismein aap (Designer) apna 'final' (aakhiri) design 'Developers' (Engineers) ko dete hain, taaki woh use *asli* (real) 'code' (jaise CSS, Swift, Android) mein bana sakein. Figma mein, yeh **Right Panel** ke `Inspect` (jaanch) tab (Module 1.5) ke zariye hota hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Yahi woh 'bridge' (pul) hai jo 'Design' (jo dikhta hai) aur 'Engineering' (jo banta hai) ko jodta hai. Agar handoff 'kharab' (bura) hoga, toh developer 'galat' (wrong) cheez banayega (e.g., galat color, galat spacing). 'Inspect' tab developer ko *aapke design se seedha code* (CSS, XML) nikaalne deta hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Jab aapka design 'final' (aakhiri), 'approved' (sveekrit), aur 'ready for development' (banne ke liye taiyaar) ho. Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh 'Red-lining' (laal lines) ki problem ko solve karta hai. Puraane zamaane mein (Photoshop/Sketch), designers ko 'manually' (haath se) design ke upar 'laal lines' (red lines) banakar 'spacing' (e.g., "16px") aur 'font size' (e.g., "18px Bold") likhna padta tha (jise 'Spec' (specs) kehte the). Figma `Inspect` tab se yeh sab 'automatically' (apne aap) kar deta hai.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** **Sabse badi problem:** Developer 'guess' (andaaza) lagayega. "Yeh button kitna bada hai? 50px ya 52px?", "Yeh blue color ka hex code kya hai?", "In dono ke beech 16px space hai ya 20px?". Is 'guesswork' (andaaze) se, jo 'product' (asli app) banega, woh aapke 'design' (Figma file) jaisa *nahi* dikhega. Phir aapko 'bug fixing' (galtiyan sudhaarne) mein hafton (weeks) lag jaayenge.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown (Inspect Tab):**
      * Developer (jiske paas `can view` ijaazat hai) `Inspect` tab (Right Panel) par jaata hai.
      * Woh design mein *kisi bhi* element (e.g., Button) par 'click' karta hai.
      * `Inspect` tab use *sab kuch* bata deta hai:
          * `Properties (Gunn):` Width (chaudai), Height (unchaai), Color (hex code), Font (naam, size, weight), Padding (Auto Layout waali).
          * `Code:` Us element ka 'ready-made' (taiyaar) *CSS*, *iOS (Swift)*, ya *Android (XML)* code, jise woh seedha 'copy' (nakal) kar sakta hai.
          * `Assets (Export):` (Topic 10.4) Agar element (e.g., Icon) 'Exportable' (export laayak) banaya gaya hai, toh developer use yahin se download kar sakta hai.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
      * **Task:** Ek Developer ke 'nazar' (perspective) se 'Button' ka code (CSS) 'Inspect' (jaanch) karna.
      * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  (Apne aap ko developer samjhein) Apni file ka 'Share' (baantne) link kholein (jismein `can view` (dekhne) ki ijaazat ho, ya `Inspect` tab par click karein).
        2.  Sabse pehle, **Right Panel** mein `Prototype` tab se `Inspect` tab par switch karein.
        3.  Apne 'Design Frame' (e.g., iPhone) ke andar apne 'Primary Button' (component) par 'click' karein.
        4.  **Right Panel (Inspect Tab) mein dekhein:**
        5.  `Properties:` Aapko dikhega: `Width: 150px`, `Height: 48px`, `Fill: #0D99FF`, `Text: Inter, 16px, SemiBold`.
        6.  `Auto Layout:` Aapko dikhega: `Padding: 16px (T/B), 24px (L/R)`.
        7.  `Code:` Thoda neeche scroll karein. 'Code' section mein (dropdown se 'CSS' chunein).
      * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapko CSS code dikhega, kuch aisa:
        ```css
        display: flex;
        flex-direction: row;
        align-items: center;
        padding: 16px 24px;
        background: #0D99FF;
        border-radius: 8px; 
        /* ...etc */
        ```
        Developer is code ko seedha 'Copy' (nakal) karke apne project mein 'Paste' (chipka) sakta hai.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
      * **Developer ko `can edit` (badlaav) ki ijaazat de dena.** (Bohot badi galti\! Woh galti se aapka design hila (move) ya 'delete' (hata) sakta hai). Hamesha `can view` dein.
      * **Layers Panel (Left) ko 'ganda' (messy) chhod dena.** (e.g., "Rectangle 54", "Group 82"). Developer ko `Inspect` tab mein yahi 'gande' naam dikhenge aur woh confuse ho jayega. Hamesha layers ko 'rename' (naam badlein) karein (e.g., `Button/Primary`, `Card/Header`). (Module 1.3).
      * **'Auto Layout' (Module 4.4) ka istemaal *na* karna.** Agar aapne 'haath se' (manually) button (Rectangle + Text) banaya hai, toh `Inspect` tab 'padding' (spacing) nahi dikhayega, sirf X/Y position dikhayega. Agar 'Auto Layout' use kiya hai, toh developer ko *seedha* 'Padding: 16px' dikhega (jaisa CSS mein hota hai).
      * 'Icons' aur 'Images' ko 'Exportable' (export laayak) banana bhool jaana (Topic 10.4).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
      * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Toh kya `Inspect` tab se poora CSS code mil jaata hai aur developer ko kuch nahi karna padta?"
      * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** **Nahi\!** Yeh 'ekdum sahi' (perfect) production-ready (taiyaar) code nahi hota. Yeh ek 'helper' (madadgaar) hai. Ek student (jo full-stack [design+code] hai) `Inspect` tab se 'values' (jaise hex code `#0D99FF`, padding `16px`, font-size `18px`) ko 'copy' (nakal) karta hai aur apne 'asli' (real) CSS code (e.g., Tailwind CSS) mein 'paste' (chipkaata) hai.
      * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:**
        1.  Designer 'Design System' (Components [â–], Styles [âˆ·], Variables [â“¥]) ka use karke design 'final' (aakhiri) karta hai.
        2.  Designer 'File' ko `Save to Version History` (Module 10.1) karta hai (Naam: "Ready for Handoff v1.2").
        3.  Designer 'Developer' ko `@mention` (tag) karke 'Comment' (Module 10.2) chhodta hai ("@Dev, yeh flow handoff ke liye ready hai.").
        4.  Developer `can view` (dekhne) waale link se file kholta hai.
        5.  Developer `Inspect` tab mein jaata hai aur `Styles` (e.g., `Color: Brand/Primary`) aur `Components` (e.g., `Button/Primary`) ke 'naam' (names) dekhta hai.
        6.  Developer apne 'code' (React) mein *usi naam* ka component (`<Button type="primary" ... />`) use karta hai. Use 'values' (16px, \#0D99FF) copy karne ki bhi zaroorat nahi padti, kyunki 'Design System' (Figma) aur 'Code Component Library' (React) pehle se hi 'synced' (jude hue) hote hain. Yahi 'pro' (peshevar) workflow hai.
      * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek developer ko 'shadow' (parchhayi) (Module 5.2) code karni hai. Shadow mein 4 values (X, Y, Blur, Color) hoti hain. Designer ka banaya 'Shadow' code (CSS) `Inspect` tab se 1-click mein 'copy' (nakal) ho jaata hai, jisse galti ki gunjaaish (chance) 'zero' (shunya) ho jaati hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
      * **Developer ko hamesha `can view` (dekhne) ki ijaazat dein.**
      * Handoff se pehle, **Layers Panel (Left) ko 'clean' (saaf) aur 'rename' (naam badla hua) karein.** (Sabse zaroori).
      * `Auto Layout` (Module 4) ka bharpoor istemaal karein (taaki 'padding' aur 'spacing' dikhe).
      * `Components` (Module 6) aur `Styles` (Module 5) ka istemaal karein (taaki 'reusable' (baar-baar istemaal) naam dikhein).
      * Assets (Icons, Images) ko 'Exportable' (export laayak) banayein (Topic 10.4).
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
      * **Kya developer ko Figma ka 'paid' (khareeda hua) account chahiye?** **Nahi\!** `Inspect` tab `can view` (dekhne) waale 'Free' (muft) account par poori tarah kaam karta hai.
      * **Kya `Inspect` tab 'Variables' (Module 7.2) dikhata hai?** Haan\! Naye version mein, `Inspect` tab 'Styles' (e.g., `Brand/Primary`) ki jagah 'Variables' (e.g., `color/brand-primary-500`) ka 'naam' (token name) dikhata hai, jo developers ke liye *aur bhi behtar* hai.
      * **'Red-lining' (laal lines) kaise dekhein?** `Inspect` tab mein hote hue, ek element (e.g., Button) ko 'select' (chunein). Phir 'Alt' (Win) / `Option` (Mac) dabaye rakhein aur 'mouse' ko doosre element (e.g., Text) par le jaayein. Figma 'automatic' (apne aap) unke beech 'red lines' (laal rekhaayein) aur 'spacing' (doori) dikha dega.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
      * 1.  'Inspect Tab' (Task) waali exercise (Button ko inspect karna) poori karein.
      * 2.  Ek 'Button' (element) ko select karein. `Alt`/`Option` dabaye rakhein aur mouse ko 'Header' (doosre element) par le jaakar unke beech ki 'spacing' (doori) check karein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
      * **Figma for Developers (Official Docs):** (Figma ke developer-specific guides).
      * **Zeplin, Avocode:** (Yeh 'third-party' (bahari) handoff tools hain, par ab 'Inspect' tab itna achha ho gaya hai ki inki zaroorat kam padti hai).
