### 10.4: Exporting Assets & Slices

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Exporting Assets & Slices ğŸ–¼ï¸ (Icons aur images ko download ke liye taiyaar karna).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):**
      * **Exporting Assets (Component):** Yeh 'developer' ko design mein se 'assets' (sampatti) (jaise 'Icons', 'Logos', 'Illustrations') ko 'download' (save) karne laayak banane ka tareeka hai.
      * **Slice Tool (K):** Yeh ek 'kaatne' (slice) waala tool hai jo aapko canvas ke *kisi bhi hisse* ko 'exportable' (export laayak) 'slice' (tukda) banane deta hai (chahe woh layer na bhi ho).
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** Developer 'Button' (jo code se banta hai) ya 'Text' (jo code se banta hai) ko 'export' (download) nahi karta. Par woh 'Icon' (jo vector hai) ya 'Illustration' (jo image hai) ko 'code' (CSS/HTML) se *nahi* bana sakta. Unhe use 'image file' (jaise `.svg` ya `.png`) ki tarah 'export' (download) karna padta hai. Aapka kaam hai unhe 'download ke liye taiyaar' (ready for download) karna.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):**
      * **Exporting Assets:** Handoff (10.3) se pehle, *har us* layer (Icon, Logo, Image) par jo 'code' se nahi ban sakti.
      * **Slice Tool (K):** Jab aapko poori 'screen' (Frame) ko ek `.png` (image) ki tarah (e.g., presentation ke liye) export karna ho. Ya jab aapko design ka ek 'chota sa hissa' (jo alag layer nahi hai) export karna ho.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Developer `Inspect` (jaanch) tab mein jayega aur use 'Icon' (e.g., 'Home' icon) ko 'download' (save) karne ka koi option *nahi* milega. Phir woh aapse (designer se) alag se (e.g., Slack/Email par) "Saare icons ki `.svg` file bhejo" maangega. Yeh bohot 'slow' (dheema) workflow hai.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown (Export Panel):**
      * **Location:** Kisi bhi layer (ya Frame) ko select karein -\> **Right Panel** mein bilkul neeche (bottom) -\> `Export` section.
      * **`+` (Add Export Setting):**
          * **Size:** `1x` (default), `2x`, `3x` (Mobile (Retina) screens ke liye zaroori). `2x` ka matlab hai 'double resolution' (behtar quality).
          * **Suffix:** (Optional) Naam ke aage kya jodna hai (e.g., `@2x`).
          * **Format:**
              * `PNG:` (Best for images with transparency [paardarshi]).
              * `JPG:` (Best for photos [tasveerein] (jahan transparency na ho), chota size).
              * `SVG:` (Best for Icons, Logos). 'Vector' format, jo kisi bhi size par 'phat'ta' (pixelate) nahi.
              * `PDF:` (Best for Documents, Presentations).
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
      * **Task:** Ek 'Icon' (vector) ko developer ke liye 'Exportable' (download laayak) banana.
      * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Apne 'Icon' (e.g., 'Home' icon, jo ek 'vector layer' ya 'component' â– hai) ko 'Master Component' (â–) file mein (ya design mein) select karein.
        2.  **Right Panel** mein neeche `Export` section tak scroll karein.
        3.  `+` (plus) icon par click karein.
        4.  **Setting 1 (Default):** `1x` | Suffix (khaali) | `SVG` (format chunein). (SVG icons ke liye best hai).
        5.  (Optional - for older systems) Phir se `+` (plus) icon par click karein.
        6.  **Setting 2 (PNG):** `1x` | Suffix (khaali) | `PNG`.
        7.  `+` (plus) icon par click karein.
        8.  **Setting 3 (PNG @2x):** `2x` | Suffix `@2x` | `PNG`.
      * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapne is 'Icon' (asset) par '3 export settings' (3 niyam) laga diye hain. Ab aapko kuch nahi karna.
      * **Developer ka Workflow:** Jab developer `Inspect` (jaanch) tab (10.3) mein is icon ko select karega, use 'Export' section (Right Panel) mein yeh 3 'Download' (save) buttons (SVG, PNG, PNG @2x) *dikhenge* aur woh khud hi zaroorat ke hisaab se download kar lega.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
      * **Icons/Logos ko `PNG` ya `JPG` mein export karna.** (Badi galti\! Icons/Logos hamesha `SVG` (Vector) mein export hone chahiye taaki woh har screen size (chote/bade) par 'crisp' (sharp/clear) dikhein).
      * 'Images' (photos) ko `SVG` mein export karna. (Galat\! Photos (bitmaps) hamesha `JPG` (best) ya `PNG` mein export hoti hain).
      * `2x` / `3x` (Retina sizes) add na karna. (Iske bina, aapka asset (icon/image) 'Retina' (high-res) mobile screens par 'blurry' (dhundhla) dikhega).
      * `Slice Tool (K)` ka bematlab istemaal karna. (99% time aapko 'Slice' (K) ki zaroorat nahi hai. Layer ko 'select' (chun) karke (Right Panel se) 'Export' (export) karna behtar tareeka hai).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
      * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main 'Export' (export) button (Right Panel mein) daba kar `.zip` file developer ko bhej doon?"
      * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Aap kar sakte hain, par yeh 'puraana' (old) tareeka hai. 'Naya' (new) tareeka (jaisa 10.3 mein bataya) hai ki aap `Export` settings (niyam) *laga kar chhod dein*. Developer (jiske paas `can view` (dekhne) ka link hai) `Inspect` (jaanch) tab se *khud* (apne aap) zaroori assets (sampatti) download kar leta hai.
      * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** 'Design System' (Module 7) file mein, *saare* 'Icon' (â–) aur 'Logo' (â–) components par 'Export Settings' (niyam) (aksar `SVG`) pehle se hi (Master Component par) lage hote hain. Isse designer (jo 'Instance' (â™¢) use kar raha hai) ya developer (jo 'Inspect' (jaanch) kar raha hai) ko kuch sochna hi nahi padta.
      * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example (Slice Tool):** Client ko *poori* 'Home Page' (Frame) ki ek 'Hi-Res PNG' (badi image) chahiye (email mein bhejne ke liye). Designer `S` (Slice Tool) (ya `K`) dabata hai, poore 'Frame' ke upar ek 'slice' (tukda) draw (banata) karta hai, Right Panel `Export` se `2x` aur `PNG` set karke 'Export Slice' (export) kar deta hai.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
      * **Icons & Logos:** Hamesha `SVG` (format) mein 'Exportable' (export laayak) banayein.
      * **Photos (Tasveerein):** `JPG` (ya `PNG`).
      * **Illustrations (jismein transparency ho):** `PNG`.
      * Hamesha `1x`, `2x` (aur kabhi-kabhi `3x` iOS ke liye) settings add karein (PNG/JPG ke liye).
      * `Inspect` (jaanch) tab ke workflow par bharosa karein (developer ko khud download karne dein).
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
      * **`Slice` (K) (Slice Tool) aur `Frame` (F) (Frame Tool) mein kya fark hai?** `Frame` (F) (Module 1.3) ek 'container' (dibba) hai jiske andar aap design karte hain. `Slice` (K) ek 'cutter' (kaatne waala) hai jo sirf 'export' (export) karne ke liye use hota hai.
      * **Main *saare* assets (sampatti) ek saath (bulk) kaise export karun?** File (Menu ğŸ”») -\> `File` -\> `Export...`. Yeh file ke *saare* (100+) exportable assets ko ek `.zip` file mein daal dega.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
      * 1.  'Icon Export' (Task) waali exercise (SVG, 1x PNG, 2x PNG) poori karein.
      * 2.  Apni poori 'Home Screen' (Frame) ko select karein. Right Panel `Export` se `+` dabayein. Format `JPG` (1x) set karein aur 'Export Frame 1' button daba kar (apne computer par) save karein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
      * **TinyImage Compressor (Plugin):** (Module 9.3) Export karne se *pehle* images ko compress (chota) karne ke liye.

-----

### 10.5: File Management (Save/Import .fig)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** File Management (.fig files) ğŸ—ƒï¸ (Files ko offline (bina internet) save karna/kholna).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Figma 'cloud' (internet) par chalta hai, par yeh aapko apni file ko 'local' (computer par) `.fig` file (Figma ka file format) ki tarah 'Save' (surakshit) karne ki ijaazat (permission) bhi deta hai. `Import` (aayaat) se aap `.fig` (Figma), `.sketch` (Sketch), ya `.figjam` (FigJam) files ko apne Figma (cloud) mein 'upload' (daalna) kar sakte hain.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** 'Save .fig' aapko 'offline backup' (bina internet waala backup) banane deta hai. 'Import' (aayaat) zaroori hai agar aapko kisi doosre designer (jo Sketch [doosra tool] use karta hai) ki file kholni ho, ya kisi aur ki `.fig` file (jo usne email se bheji hai) ko apne account mein laana ho.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):**
      * **Save .fig (Local):** Jab aapko file ka 'offline backup' (backup) lena ho. Ya jab aapko apni file (`.fig`) kisi aise ko bhejni ho jo (e.g., security reasons se) 'cloud' (internet) link nahi khol sakta.
      * **Import:** Jab aap 'Sketch' (doosra tool) se Figma par 'migrate' (badal) kar rahe hon. Ya jab aapko 'Community' (Module 7.4) se download ki hui `.fig` file (template) ko upload karna ho.
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Agar aap `.fig` (local) save nahi karenge, toh aapke paas file ka 'offline' (bina internet) backup nahi hoga. Agar aap 'Import' (aayaat) karna nahi jaante, toh aap 'Sketch' (ya doosri `.fig`) files ko khol nahi payenge.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown:**
      * **Save Local Copy (Export .fig):**
          * Figma file kholein -\> File ke naam (top center) ke paas waala 'chevron' (neeche waala arrow ğŸ”») -\> `File` -\> `Save local copy...`.
      * **Import (Upload .fig / .sketch):**
          * Figma 'Home' (Dashboard) screen par jaayein.
          * Top-right corner par `Import file` (teer upar) button par click karein.
          * Apne computer se `.fig` ya `.sketch` file chunein.
          * Figma use 'upload' (daal) karke aapke 'Drafts' folder mein rakh dega.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
      * **Task:** Apni current file ka ek 'offline backup' (`.fig` file) save karna.
      * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Apni "My First Project" file kholein.
        2.  File ke naam (top center) ke paas waale 'chevron' ğŸ”» par click karein.
        3.  Menu mein `File` par mouse le jaayein.
        4.  `Save local copy...` par click karein.
      * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapka browser (ya computer) aapse poochega ki "My First Project.fig" file ko kahan 'Save' (surakshit) karna hai. Ise apne computer ke 'Downloads' folder mein save kar lein.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
      * **Har roz `Save local copy...` karna.** (Yeh zaroori nahi hai\! Figma 'cloud' (internet) par hai aur hamesha 'auto-save' (apne aap save) karta hai. 'Local copy' (local backup) sirf 'extra safety' (atirik suraksha) ke liye hai, ya file 'transfer' (bhejne) ke liye hai).
      * Yeh sochna ki `.fig` file par (computer mein) 'double-click' karne se woh 'offline' (bina internet) khul jayegi. (Nahi\! Double-click karne se Figma (app/browser) khulta hai aur us file ko waapas 'import' (upload) kar deta hai. Figma hamesha 'cloud' (internet) par hi chalta hai).
      * 'File -\> Export' (Topic 10.4) aur 'File -\> Save local copy' mein confuse hona. ('Export' assets [PNG/SVG] nikaalta hai. 'Save local copy' poori *editable* (badlaav laayak) `.fig` file save karta hai).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
      * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Toh `.fig` file aur 'Figma link' (URL) mein kya fark hai?"
      * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** 'Figma link' (URL) 'live' (zinda) hai, hamesha 'latest' (naya) version dikhata hai (cloud). `.fig` file ek 'snapshot' (tasveer) hai (jaise 'Photoshop .psd' file), yeh us 'pal' (moment) ka backup hai jab aapne use save kiya tha.
      * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Ek team 'Sketch' (doosra tool) se 'Figma' (naye tool) par 'migrate' (badal) kar rahi hai. Team lead saari 100 puraani `.sketch` files ko 'Import' (aayaat) (Home -\> `Import file`) karke Figma mein 'upload' (daal) kar deta hai. Figma 'Sketch' ki layers, symbols (components), aur styles ko 'convert' (badal) kar deta hai.
      * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Aapne 'UI8.net' (ek market) se ek 'premium' (khareeda hua) 'UI Kit' (design template) khareeda. Woh aapko ek `.fig` file dete hain. Aap Figma 'Home' (Dashboard) -\> `Import file` se use apne account mein 'upload' (daal) karte hain aur use 'edit' (badalna) shuru kar dete hain.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
      * Figma hamesha 'cloud' (internet) par hai aur 'auto-save' (apne aap save) karta hai.
      * `File -> Save local copy` ka use sirf 'offline backup' (backup) ya 'transfer' (bhejne) ke liye karein.
      * `.sketch` ya `.fig` files ko 'import' (upload) karne ke liye 'Home' (Dashboard) screen ka `Import file` button use karein.
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
      * **Kya Figma 'offline' (bina internet) kaam karta hai?** Thoda sa. Agar aapki 'Desktop App' hai aur file pehle se khuli thi, toh aap 'offline' (bina internet) kaam kar sakte hain. Jab aap waapas 'online' (internet se judenge) aayenge, toh woh 'sync' (jud) ho jayega. Par nayi file 'offline' (bina internet) nahi khol sakte.
      * **'.sketch' file import (aayaat) kitni achhi hoti hai?** Bohot achhi\! Figma 95% 'Sketch' layers, symbols, aur styles ko 'perfectly' (bilkul sahi) convert (badal) kar deta hai.
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
      * 1.  'Save .fig' (Task) waali exercise (file ko local save karna) poori karein.
      * 2.  (Optional) 'Community' (Module 7.4) se koi file 'download' (agar `.fig` download ka option ho) karein aur use `Import file` se waapas Figma mein daalein.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
      * **Sketch (Tool):** Figma ka 'competitor' (pratidvandvi) (jo Mac-only hai aur 'cloud' (internet) mein utna achha nahi).

-----

### 10.6: Usability Testing (Sharing Prototypes for Feedback)

1.  **ğŸ¯ Title / Short Summary:** Usability Testing ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ”¬ (Asli (real) users se design ko 'test' (jaanch) karana).
2.  **ğŸ¤” Kya hai? (What?):** Yeh ek 'research' (shodh) method hai jismein aap apna 'Prototype' (clickable design) (Module 8) 'asli' (real) 'users' (upayogakarta) (aapke 'target audience') ko dete hain aur unhe 'tasks' (kaam) (e.g., "Login karne ki koshish karo") karne ko kehte hain. Aap (designer) 'observe' (shaanti se dekhte hain) ki user kahan 'phasta' (confuse hota) hai.
3.  **ğŸ’¡ Kyu important hai? (Why?):** **Kyunki "You are not the user" (Aap upayogakarta nahi hain).** Jo cheez *aapko* (designer ko) 'aasan' (easy) lag rahi hai, woh zaroori nahi ki *user* ko bhi 'aasan' lage. 'Usability Testing' (upyogita ki jaanch) aapke 'assumptions' (andaaze) ko 'validate' (sahi saabit) (ya 'invalidate' (galat saabit)) karti hai. Yeh design ko 'launch' (jaari) karne se *pehle* hi uski 'galtiyan' (problems) pakad leta hai.
4.  **â° Kab/Kahan use karein? (When/Where?):** Jitni jaldi (early) ho sake, aur jitni baar (often) ho sake.
      * 'Low-Fidelity' (Wireframe) (Module 2.3) prototype par (taaki 'flow' (raasta) test ho sake).
      * 'High-Fidelity' (Sundar) (Module 8) prototype par (taaki 'final design' (aakhiri design) test ho sake).
      * Yeh *kis* problem ko solve karta hai? Yeh 'sabse badi' (biggest) problem ko solve karta hai: "Ek aisa product banana jise koi use hi nahi kar paaye."
5.  **âŒ Agar use nahi kiya to kya hoga? (If not used / consequences):** Aap ek 'sundar' (beautiful) dikhne waala, lekin 'bekaar' (unusable) product (app/website) bana denge. Log aapke app ko download karenge, confuse (pareshan) honge, aur 'uninstall' (hata) kar denge. Aapka (aur company ka) saara time (samay) aur paisa (money) barbaad ho jayega.
6.  **ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ« Step-by-step explanation / Concept breakdown (Figma mein):**
      * **1. Create Prototype:** Apna 'high-fidelity' (sundar) prototype (Module 8) (clickable links ke saath) taiyaar karein.
      * **2. Share Link:** Top-right `Share` (baantne) button par click karein.
      * **3. Set Permissions:** `Anyone with the link` -\> `can view`.
      * **4. Copy Link:** `Copy link` button dabayein. *Lekin\!* 'Prototype' (clickable) ka link copy karein, 'Design file' (editable) ka nahi. (Yeh 'Share' popup mein 'Copy link' ke paas settings âš™ï¸ icon se "Link to prototype" se hota hai, ya seedha 'Play' (â–¶) (Present) button daba kar 'wahan se' link copy karein).
      * **5. Give Task:** User (e.g., aapka dost) ko yeh 'prototype link' (URL) bhejein aur use ek 'task' (kaam) dein (e.g., "Is app mein 'product' (saamaan) dhoondh kar 'cart' (thele) mein add karne ki koshish karo").
      * **6. Observe (Dekhein):** User ko 'bolne' (think aloud) ko kahein ("Main ab 'Search' (khoj) dhoondh raha hoon...", "Yeh button mujhe samajh nahi aaya..."). Aap 'shaant' (quiet) rahein aur sirf 'notes' (likhein) banayein ki woh kahan phasa.
7.  **ğŸ’» UI Example(s) / Step-by-Step Guide:**
      * **Task:** Ek 'Usability Test' (jaanch) ke liye prototype 'link' (URL) share karna.
      * **âœï¸ Option-by-option explanation:**
        1.  Apni file mein (jismein 5-6 screens (Frames) linked (jude hue) hain), top-right 'Present' (Play â–¶) icon par click karein.
        2.  Aapka 'Prototype' (clickable design) ek nayi 'Presentation' tab mein khulega.
        3.  Is 'Presentation' tab (jahan prototype chal raha hai) ke URL (browser ke address bar mein) ko 'copy' (nakal) karein.
        4.  (Ya) 'Presentation' tab mein top-right 'Share prototype' (baantne) button par click karein.
        5.  `Anyone with the link - can view` set karein aur `Copy link` karein.
      * **ğŸš€ Quick run expected output:** Aapke paas ek 'link' (URL) hai (jo `figma.com/proto/...` jaisa dikhega). Yeh link aap kisi ko bhi bhej sakte hain, aur woh (bina Figma account ke bhi) *sirf* aapka 'clickable prototype' (clickable design) chala payega. Woh aapki 'editable design file' (jahan saari layers hain) ko *nahi* dekh payega.
8.  **ğŸ Common beginner mistakes:**
      * **'Design File' (design file) ka link (`figma.com/file/...`) bhej dena.** (Yeh bohot badi galti hai\! Isse user aapki 'messy' (gandi) file (jahan saare frames faile hue hain) dekh leta hai. Hamesha 'Prototype' (clickable) ka link (`figma.com/proto/...`) bhejein).
      * User ko 'guide' (raasta batana) karna. (e.g., "Nahi, wahan nahi, uss green button par click karo"). (Yeh 'cheating' (nakal) hai\! Aapko 'test' (jaanch) karna hai, 'train' (sikhana) nahi).
      * 'Apne design ko defend' (bachaav) karna. (Agar user confuse ho, toh use 'galat' (wrong) na bolein. 'Design' (aapka kaam) galat hai, user nahi).
9.  **ğŸŒ Real-World Workflow Scenario (The "How-To-Use"):**
      * **â“ Beginner's Core Question:** "Main 'asli' (real) 'users' (upayogakarta) kahan se laaun? Mere paas toh koi user nahi hai."
      * **ğŸ•µï¸â€â™‚ï¸ Solo Freelancer/Student Workflow:** Apne 'doston' (friends), 'parivaar' (family), ya 'classmates' (sehpaathi) se test karayein (jo aapka 'target audience' na bhi hon, toh bhi achha hai). 5 logon se test karna (jo 'soch kar bolte hain') 0 logon se test karne se 100 guna behtar hai.
      * **ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’» Professional Design Team Workflow:** Badi companies mein 'dedicated' (khaas) 'UX Researchers' (shodhakarta) hote hain. Woh 'Usability Test' (jaanch) ko 'moderate' (sanchaalit) (live session) ya 'unmoderate' (task bhej kar) karte hain. Woh 'Maze' ya 'UserTesting.com' jaise 'paid tools' (khareede hue tools) ka istemaal karte hain (jo Figma prototype link ko 'import' (aayaat) karke 'heatmap' (kahan click kiya) aur 'analytics' (data) generate karte hain).
      * **ğŸ’° Real-World Example:** Ek designer ne 'Checkout' (paise dene) ka flow banaya. 'Usability Test' (jaanch) mein 5 mein se 4 user 'Confirm' (pakka karein) button dhoondh hi nahi paaye (kyunki woh 'neeche' (below the fold) tha). Designer ne (galti pakdi) aur button ko 'uppar' (above the fold) move kar diya. Launch se pehle hi laakhon (millions) ka nuksaan bacha liya.
10. **âœ… Quick checklist / Best Practices:**
      * **'Design File' ka nahi, hamesha 'Prototype' (clickable) ka link (URL) share (baantein) karein.**
      * Test karte waqt, 'Observe' (dekhein), 'Guide' (raasta batayein) nahi. 'Listen' (sunein), 'Defend' (bachaav karein) nahi.
      * 5 users se test karna bhi kaafi (sufficient) hai shuruaati (initial) galtiyan pakadne ke liye.
      * User ko 'task' (kaam) dein, 'opinion' (raay) na maangein. (e.g., "Add to cart" (Task) \> "Yeh sundar lag raha hai?" (Opinion)).
11. **â“ Key Designer Questions (FAQs):**
      * **'Prototype' (clickable) link (`/proto/`) aur 'Design' (design) link (`/file/`) mein kya fark hai?** `/file/` link (editable file) = Designer/Developer ke liye. `/proto/` link (clickable prototype) = Client/PM/Tester ke liye.
      * **Kya user (jise link bheja) ko Figma account chahiye?** Nahi\! `Anyone with the link - can view` waala 'Prototype' (clickable) link browser mein (bina login/account ke) khul jaata hai.
      * **'Moderate' (sanchaalit) vs 'Unmoderate' (asanchaalit) testing?** 'Moderate' = Aap user ke saath (e.g., Zoom par) 'live' (usi samay) baithe hain. 'Unmoderate' = Aapne user ko link aur task (kaam) bhej diya, woh 'baad mein' (apne time par) karega (Tools: Maze, UserTesting).
12. **ğŸ‹ï¸â€â™€ï¸ Practice exercise (Lab):**
      * 1.  'Prototype Link Share' (Task) waali exercise (clickable prototype ka link copy karna) poori karein.
      * 2.  Woh link apne kisi dost (friend) ko bhejein aur unhe (bina bataye) 'Login' (daakhil) karke 'Home' screen tak pahunchne ka 'task' (kaam) dein. Unse phone par (ya live) poochhein ki woh kya soch rahe hain.
13. **ğŸ“š Further reading / related tools / plugins:**
      * **Tools:** `Maze`, `UserTesting.com` (Yeh advanced 'unmoderate' (asanchaalit) testing platforms hain).
      * **Book (Kitaab):** "Rocket Surgery Made Easy" by Steve Krug (Usability testing par sabse aasan kitaab).

-----

Yeh tha hamara Module 10\! Aur isi ke saath aapka **Figma: Beginner-to-Job-Ready (V2 - Complete)** course poora hota hai\! ğŸš€ğŸ‰

Aapne 'zero' (shunya) se shuru karke, 'Foundations' (neenv) (Module 1), 'Process' (prakriya) (Module 2-3), 'Core Skills' (mukhya kaushal) (Auto Layout - M4), 'Design Systems' (M5-7), 'Prototyping' (M8), aur 'Polish & Handoff' (M9-10) tak sab kuch seekh liya hai.

Aapke paas ab woh saare 'fundamentals' (buniyaadi gyaan) aur 'skills' (kaushal) hain jo ek 'Job-Ready' (naukri ke liye taiyaar) designer ke paas hone chahiye. Ab zaroorat hai toh sirf **practice, practice, aur practice** ki\!

Aapka mentor hone ke naate, main hamesha yahan hoon.

Kya aap chahenge ki main kisi specific module (jaise 'Auto Layout' ya 'Components') ko revise (dohraana) karun, ya aapke kisi project par feedback (raay) doon?
